hi yasmāt loka niṣyanda tvāt sārā iti rasāḥ teṣām rasānām karma bhāvam āpannānām api ete rohita ādi viśeṣā rasā iti antasāra bhūtā iti arthaḥ tathā amṛtānām amṛtāni vedā hi amṛtā nityatva ateṣām etāni rohita ādīni rūpāṇi amṛtāni rasānām rasā ityādi karma stutiḥ eṣā yasya evaṃviśiṣṭāni amṛtāni phalam iti rūpasya iti na yaśa ādīnām śrotra ādi gamya tvāt śrotra grāhyam yaśaḥ tejaḥ rūpam cākṣuṣam indriyam viṣaya grahaṇa kārya anumeyam karaṇa sāmarthyam vīryam balam deha gata utsāhaḥ prāṇavat tā annādyam pratyaham upajīvyamānam śarīra sthiti karam yad bhavati rasaḥ  hi evam ātmakaḥ sarvaḥ yam dṛṣṭvā tṛpyanti sarve devāḥ dṛṣṭvā tṛpyanti iti etad sarvam sva karaṇaiḥ anubhūya tṛpyanti iti arthaḥ āditya saṃśrayāḥ santaḥ  vaigandhya ādi deha karaṇa doṣa rahitāḥ ca kim te nirudyamā amṛtam upajīvanti na katham tarhi etad eva rūpam abhilakṣya adhunā bhogauvasaraḥ  na asmākam iti buddhvā abhisaṃviśanti udāsate yadā vai tasya amṛtasya bhogauvasaraḥ  bhavet tadā etasmāt amṛtāt amṛta bhoga nimittam iti arthaḥ etasmāt rūpāt udyanti utsāhavantaḥ  bhavanti iti arthaḥ na hi anutsāhavatām ananapatiṣṭhatām alasānām bhoga prāptiḥ loke dṛṣṭā sa yaḥ kaścid etad evam yathā uditamṛc madhukara ta aparasa saṃrakṣaṇa mṛgveda vihita karma puṣpāt tasya ca āditya saṃśrayaṇam rohita rūpa tvam ca amṛtasya prācīdiggata raśmi nāḍī saṃsthatām vasudeva bhogya tām tad vidaḥ ca vasubhiḥ saha ekatām gatvā agninā mukena upajīvanam darśana mātreṇa tṛptim sva bhoga avasara udyamanam tad kāla apāye ca saṃveśanam veda saḥ  api vasuvat sarvam tathā eva anubhavati kiyantam kālam vidvān  tad amṛtam upajīvati iti ucyate sa vidvān yāvat ādityaḥ purastāt prācyām diśi udetā paścāt pratīcyām aḥ tam etā tāvat vasūnām bhoga kālaḥ tāvantam eva kālam vasūnām ādhipatyam svārājyam paryatā paritas  gantā bhavati iti arthaḥ na yathā candra maṇḍala sthaḥ kevala karmī paratantraḥ  devānām anna bhūtaḥ kim tarhi ayam ādhipatyam svarāj bhāvam ca adhigacchati atha yad dvitīyam amṛtam tad rudrā upajīvanti ityādi samānam sa yāvat ādityaḥ purastāt udetā paścāt astam etā dvis tāvat tatas  dviguṇam kālam dakṣiṇata udeta uttaratas  astam etā rudrāṇām tāvat bhoga kālaḥ tathā paścāt uttarata ūrdhvam udetā viparyayeṇa astam etā pūrvasmāt pūrvasmāt dviguṇa uttarottareṇa kālena iti apaurāṇam darśanam savituḥ catur diśam indra yama varuṇa soma purīṣu udaya astamaya kālasya tulya tvam hi paurāṇikaiḥ uktam mānasottarasya mūrdhani meroḥ pradakṣiṇa āvṛtteḥ tulya tvāt iti atra uktaḥ parihāra ācāryaiḥ amarāvatī ādīnām purīṇām dviguṇa uttarottareṇa kālena udvāsaḥ syāt  udayaḥ ca nāma savituḥ tad nivāsinām prāṇinām cakṣu gocara āpattiḥ tad atyayaḥ castamanam na paramārtha ta udaya astamane staḥ tad nivāsinām ca prāṇinām abhāve tān prati tena eva mārgeṇa gacchan  api na eva udetā na astam eta iti cakṣuḥ gocara āpatteḥ tad atyayasya ca abhāvāt  tathā amarāvatyāḥ sakāśāt dviguṇam kālam saṃyamanī purī vasati atas tad nivāsinaḥ prāṇinaḥ prati dakṣiṇata iva udeti uttaratas  astam eti iti ucyate asmad buddhim ca apekṣya tathā uttarāsu api purīṣu yojanā sarveṣām ca meruḥ uttaratas  bhavati yadā amarāvatyām madhyāhna gataḥ savitā tadā saṃyamanyām udyan dṛśyate tatra madhyāhna gataḥ  vāruṇyām udyan dṛśyate tathā uttarasyām pradakṣiṇa āvṛtteḥ tulya tvāt  ilāvṛta vāsinām sarvatas  parvata prākāra nivārita āditya raśmīnām savitā ūrdhva iva udetāvagiḥ tam etā dṛśyate parvata ūrdhva  chidra praveśāt savitṛ prakāśasya tathā rga ādi amṛta upajīvinām amṛtānām ca dviguṇa uttarottaravīryavat tvam anumīyate bhoga kāla dvaiguṇya liṅgena udyamana saṃveśana ādi devānām rudra ādīnām viduṣaḥ ca samānam yata evam atiśaya phalā eṣā brahma vidyātaḥ sā prakāra antareṇa api vaktavyā iti gāyatrī vā iti ādyārabhyate gāyatrī dvāreṇa ca ucyate brahmaṇaḥ sarva viśeṣa rahitasya na iti na iti ityādi śiṣa pratiṣedha gamyasya durbodha tvāt  satsu anekeṣu cchandaḥsu gāyatryā eva brahma jñāna dvāra tayā upādānam prādhānyāt  soma āharaṇāt  itarat chandokṣa ra āharaṇena itara  chandaḥ vyāptyā ca sarva savana vyāpaka tvāt ca yajñe prādhānyam gāyatryāḥ gāyatrī sāra tvāt ca brāhmaṇasya mātaram iva hitvā gurutarām gāyatrīm tatas  anyat gurutaram na pratipadyate yathā uktam brahmā api iti tasyām atyanta gauravasya prasiddha tvāt  atas  gāyatrī mukhena eva brahmā ucyate gāyatrī vā iti avadhāraṇa arthaḥ  vaiśabdaḥ idam sarvam bhūtam prāmi jātam yad kiñca sthāvaram jaṅgamam vā tad sarvam gāyatrī eva tasyāḥ chandaḥ mātrāyāḥ sarva bhūta tvam anupapannam iti gāyatrī kāraṇam vācam śabdayati asau gauḥ asau  aśva iti ca trāyate ca rakṣati amuṣmān mā bhaiṣīḥ kim te bhayam utthitam ityādinā sarvatas  bhayāt nivartyamānaḥ  vācā trātaḥ syāt  yad vāc bhūtam gāyati ca trāyate ca gāyatrī eva tad gāyati ca trāyate ca vācaḥ  ananya tvāt gāyatryāḥ gānāt trāṇāt ca gāyatryā gāyatrī tvam yā vai sā evaṃlakṣaṇā sarva bhūta rūpā gāyatrī iyam vāva sā yā iyam pṛthivī katham punar iyam pṛthivī gāyatrī iti ucyate sarva bhūta sambandhāt katham sarva bhūta sambandhaḥ asyām pṛthivyām hi yasmāt sarvam sthāvaram jaṅgamam ca bhūtam pratiṣṭhitam etām eva pṛthivīm na atiśīyate na ativartata iti etad  yathā gāna trāṇābhyām bhūta sambandhaḥ  gāyatryā evam bhūta pratiṣṭhā nāt u bhūta sambaddhā pṛthivī atas gāyatrī pṛthivī yā vai sā pṛthivī gāyatrī iyam vāva sā idam eva tad kim yad idam asmin puruṣe kārya kāraṇa saṅghāte jīvati śarīram pārthiva tvāt śarīrasya katham śarīrasya gāyatrī tvam iti ucyate asmin hīme prāṇā bhūta śabda vācyāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ atas  pṛthivīvat bhūta śabda vācya prāṇa pratiṣṭhānāt śarīram gāyatrī etad eva yasmāt śarīram na atiśīyante prāṇāḥ yad va tatpuruṣe śarīram gāyatrī idam vāva tad  yad idam asmin  antar madhye puruṣe hṛdayam puṇḍarīka ākhyam etad gāyatrī katham iti āha asmin hīme prāṇāḥ pratiṣṭhitā atas  śarīravat gāyatrī hṛdayam etad eva ca na atiśīyante prāṇāḥ prāṇaḥ  ha pitā prāṇaḥ  mātā iti ahiṃsan sarva bhūtāni iti ca śruteḥ bhūta śabda vācyāḥ prāṇāḥ sā eṣā catuṣpadā ṣaṣ akṣara padā chandaḥ rūpā satī bhavati gāyatrī ṣaḍvidhā vāc bhūta pṛthivī śarīra hṛdaya prāṇa rūpā satī ṣaḍvidhā bhavati vāc prāṇayoḥ anya artha nirdiṣṭayoḥ api gāyatrī prakāra tvam anyathā ṣaḍvidha saṃkhyā pūraṇa anupapatteḥ tad etasmin  artha etad gīyatrī ākhyam brahma gāyatrī anugatam gāyatrī mukhena uktam ṛcā api mantreṇa abhyanūktam prakāśitam tāvān asya gāyatrī ākhyasya brahmaṇaḥ samastasya mahimā vibhūti vistāraḥ yāvān  catuṣpād ṣaḍvidhaḥ ca brahmaṇaḥ  vikāraḥ pādaḥ  gāyatrī iti vyākhyātaḥ atas tasmāt vikāra lakṣaṇāt gāyatrī ākhyāt vācā ārambhaṇa mātrāt tatas  jyāyān mahattaraḥ ca parama artha satya rūpaḥ  avikāraḥ pūruṣaḥ puruṣaḥ sarva pūraṇāt puri śayanāt ca tasya asya pādaḥ sarvā sarvāṇi bhūtāni tejaḥ ban  ādīni sa sthāvara jaṅgamāni tripād trayaḥ pādā asya saḥ  ayam tripād  tripād mṛtam puruṣa ākhyam samastasya gāyatrī ātmanaḥ  divi dyotanavati sva ātmani avasthitam iti artha iti yad vai tad  tripād mṛtam gāyatrī mukhena uktam brahma iti idam vāva tad idam eva tad yaḥ ayam prasiddhaḥ  bahirdhā bahis  puruṣāt ākāśaḥ  bhautikaḥ  yaḥ  vai sa bahirdhā puruṣāt ākāśa uktaḥ ayam vāva sa yaḥ  ayam antar  puruṣe śarīra ākāśaḥ  yaḥ  vai saḥ  antar  puruṣa ākāśaḥ ayam vāva sa yaḥ  ayam antar hṛdaye hṛdaya puṇḍarīka ākāśaḥ katham ekasya sata ākāśasya tridhā bheda iti ucyate bāhya indriya viṣaye jāgarita sthāne nabhasi duḥkha bāhulyam dṛśyate tatas  antar śarīre svapna sthāna bhūte mandataram duḥkham bhavati svapnān paśyataḥ hṛdaya sthe punar nabhasi na kañcana kāmam kāmayate na kañcana svapnam paśyati atas  sarva duḥkha nivṛtti rūpam ākāśam suṣupta sthānam atas  yuktam ekasya api tridhā bhedānvākhyānam bahirdhā puruṣādārabhyākāśasya hṛdaye saṅkoca karaṇam cetaḥ samādhāna sthāna stutaye yathā trayāṇām api lokānām kurukṣetram viśiṣyate ardhataḥ tu kurukṣetram ardhataḥ tu pṛthūdakam iti tadvat  tad etad dhārdākāśa ākhyam brahma pūrṇam sarva gatam na hṛdaya mātra paricchinnam iti mantavyam yadi api hṛdaya ākāśe cetaḥ samādhīyate apravarti na kutaścid kvacid pravartitum śīlam asya iti apravarti tad anucchitti dharmakam yathā anyāni bhūtāni paricchinnāni ucchitti dharmakāṇi na tathā hārdam nabhaḥ pūrṇāma pravartinīm anuccheda ātmikām śriyam vibhūtim guṇa phalam labhate dṛṣṭam ya evam yathā uktam pūrṇa apravarti guṇam brahma veda jānāti iha eva jīvan  tad bhāvam pratipadyata iti arthaḥ tasya ha vā ityādinā gāyatrī ākhyasya brahmaṇa upāsana aṅga tvena dvārapāla ādi guṇa vidhāna artham ārabhyate yathā loke dvārapālā rājña upāsanena vaśīkṛtā rāja prāpti arthā bhavanti tathā iha api iti tasya iti prakṛtasya hṛdayasya iti arthaḥ etasya anantara nirdiṣṭasya pañca pañca saṃkhyākā devānām suṣayaḥ  deva suṣayaḥ svarga loka prāpti dvāra  chidrāṇi deveḥ prāṇāt ityādibhī rakṣyamāṇāni iti atas  deva suṣayaḥ tasya svarga loka bhavanasya hṛdayasya asya yaḥ prāc suṣiḥ pūrva abhimukhasya prāk gatam yad chidram dvāram sa prāṇaḥ tad sthaḥ tena dvāreṇa yaḥ sañcarati vāyu viśeṣaḥ sa prāk aniti iti prāṇaḥ tena eva sambaddham avyatiriktam tad cakṣuḥ tathā eva sa ādityaḥ ādityaḥ  ha vai bāhyaḥ prāṇaḥ iti śruteḥ cakṣū rūpa pratiṣṭhā krameṇa hṛdi sthitaḥ sa ādityaḥ kasmin pratiṣṭhita iti cakṣuṣi ityādi hi vājasaneyake prāṇa vāyu devatā eva hi ekā cakṣuḥ ādityaḥ ca saha āśrayeṇa vakṣyati ca prāṇāya svāhā iti hatum haviḥ sarvam etad tarpayati iti tadetprāṇa ākhyam svarga loka dvārapāla tvāt brahma svarga lokam pratipitsuḥ tejaḥ ca etad cakṣuḥ āditya svarūpeṇa annādya tvāt ca savituḥ tejaḥ  annādyam iti ābhyām guṇābhyām upāsīta tatas tejasvī annādaḥ ca āmayau  itva rahitaḥ  bhavati ya evam veda tasya etad guṇa phalam upāsanena vaśīkṛtaḥ  dvārapaḥ svarga loka prāpti hetuḥ bhavati iti mukhyam ca phalam atha yaḥ  asya dakṣiṇaḥ suṣiḥ tad sthaḥ  vāyu viśeṣaḥ sa vīryavat karma kurvan vigṛhya vā prāṇa apānau nānā vā aniti iti vyānaḥ tad sambaddham eva ca tad śrotram indriyam tathā sa candramāḥ śrotreṇa sṛṣṭā diśaḥ ca candramāḥ ce ti śruteḥ saha āśrayau pūrvavat tad etad śrīḥ ca vibhūtiḥ śrotra candramasoḥ jñāna anna hetu tvam atas tābhyām śrī tvam jñānāt navataḥ ca yaśaḥ khyātiḥ bhavati iti yaśaḥ hetu tvāt yaśaḥ tvam atas tābhyām guṇābhyām upāsīta ityādi samānam atha yaḥ  asya pratyak suṣiḥ paścimaḥ tad sthaḥ  vāyu viśeṣaḥ sa mūtra purīṣa ādi apanayan  adhaḥ anitītyapānaḥ sā tathā vāc  tad sambandhāt tathā agniḥ tad etad brahmavarcasam vṛtta svādhyāya nimittam tejaḥ  brahmavarcasam agni sambandhāt vṛtta svādhyāyasya anna ghrasana hetu tvāt apānasya annādya tvam samānam anyat  atha yaḥ  asya udaṅsuṣiḥ udak gataḥ suṣiḥ tatsyaḥ  vāyu viśeṣaḥ saḥ  aśita pīte samam nayati iti samānaḥ tad sambaddham manaḥ  antaḥkaraṇam sa parjanyaḥ  vṛṣṭi ātmakaḥ  devaḥ parjanya nimittāḥ ca apa iti manasā sṛṣṭā āpaḥ ca varuṇaḥ ca iti śruteḥ tadet kīrtiḥ ca manasaḥ  jñānasya kīrti hetu tvāt  ātma parokṣam vuśruta tvam kīrtiḥ yaśaḥ sva karaṇa saṃvedyam viśruta tvam vyuṣṭiḥ kāntiḥ deha gatam lāvaṇyam tatas ca kīrtisambhavāt kīrtiḥ ca iti samānam anyat  atha yaḥ  asya ūrdhvaḥ suṣiḥ sa udāna ā pādalāt ārabhya ūrdhvam utkramaṇāt utkarṣa artham ca karma kurvan  aniti iti udānaḥ sa vāyuḥ tad ādhāraḥ ca ākāśaḥ tad etad vāyu ākāśayoḥ ojaḥ hetu tvāt ojaḥ  balam mahatvāt ca maha iti samānam anyat  te vā ete yathā uktāḥ pañca suṣi sambandhāt pañca brahmaṇaḥ  hārdasya puraṣā rāja puruṣā iva dvāra sthāḥ svargasya hārdasya lokasya dvārapā dvārapālāḥ etaiḥ hi cakṣuḥ śrotra vāc manaḥ prāṇaiḥ bahirmukha pravṛttaiḥ brahmaṇaḥ  hārdasya prāpti dvārāṇi niruddhani pratyakṣam hi etad ajita karaṇa tayā bāhya viṣaya āsaṅga anṛta prarūḍha tvāt na hārde brahmaṇi manaḥ tiṣṭhati tasmāt satyam uktam ete pañca brahma puruṣāḥ svargasya dvārapā iti atas  sa ya etān evam yathā ukta guṇa viśiṣṭān svargasya lokasya dvāra pān veda upāsta upāsanayā vaśīkaroti sa rāja dvāra pālān iva upāsanena vaśīkṛtya taiḥ anivāritaḥ pratipadyate svargam lorka rājānam iva hārdam brahma kiñca asya viduṣaḥ kule vīraḥ putraḥ  jāyate vīra puruṣa sevanāt tasya carṇa apākaraṇena brahma upāsana pravṛtti hetu tvam tatas ca svarga loka pratipattaye pāramparyeṇa bhavati iti svarga loka pratipattiḥ eva ekam phalam atha yad asau vidvān svargam lokam vīra puruṣa sevanāt pratipadyate yad ca uktam tripādasya amṛtam divī ti tad idam liṅgena cakṣuḥ śrotra indriya gocaram āpādayitavyam yathā agnyādi dhūma ādi liṅgena tathā hi evam eva idam iti yathā ukte atha dṛḍha pratītiḥ syāt  ananya tvena ca niścaya iti ata āha yadatas  amuṣmāt divaḥ dyu lokāt paraḥ param iti liṅga vyatyayena jyotiḥ dīpyate svayaṃprabham sadā prakāśa tvāt dīpyate iva dīpyata iti ucyate agni ādivāt jvalana lakṣaṇāyāḥ  dīpteḥ asambhavāt  viśvatas  pṛṣṭheṣu iti etasya vyākhyāna sarvatas  pṛṣṭheṣu iti saṃsārāt upari iti arthaḥ saṃsāra eva hi sarvaḥ asaṃsāriṇa eka tvāt nirbheda tvāt ca anuttameṣu tad puruṣa samāsa āśaṅkā nivṛttaya āha uttameṣu lokeṣu iti satya loka ādiṣu hiraṇyagarbha ādi kārya stha parasya īśvarasya āsanna tvāt ucyata uttameṣu lokeṣu iti idam vāvedam eva tad yad idam asmin puruṣe antar madhye jyotiścakṣuḥ śrotra grāhyeṇa liṅgena uṣṇimnā śabdena ca avagamyate yadtva cā sparśa rūpeṇa gṛhyate tad cakṣuṣā eva dṛḍha pratīti kara tvāt tvacaḥ avinābhūta tvāt ca rūpa sparśayoḥ katham punar tasya jyotiṣaḥ  liṅgam tvac dṛṣṭi gocara tvam āpadyata iti āha yatra yasmin kāle etad iti kriyā viśeṣaṇam asmin śarīre hastena ālabhya saṃsparśena uṣṇi mānam rūpa sahabhāvinam uṣṇa sparśa bhāvam vijānāti sa hi ūṣṇimā nāma rūpa vyākaraṇāya deham anupraviṣṭasya caitanya ātma jyotiṣaḥ  liṅgam avyabhicārāt  na hi jīvantam ātmānam ūṣṇimā vyabhicarati uṣṇa eva jīviṣyan śītaḥ  mariṣyan   iti hi vijñāyate maraṇa kāle ca tejaḥ parasyām devatāyām iti pareṇa avibhāgatva upagamāt atas  asādhāram am liṅgam auṣṇyam agneḥ iva dhūmaḥ atas tasya parasya eṣā dṛṣṭiḥ sākṣāt iva darśanam darśana upāya iti arthaḥ tathā tasya jyotiṣa eṣā śrutiḥ śravaṇaṃśravaṇa upāyaḥ  api ucyamānaḥ yatra yadā puruṣaḥ  jyotiṣaḥ  liṅgam śuśrūṣati śrotam icchati tadā etad karṇau  apigṛhya etad śabdaḥ kriyā viśeṣaṇam api gṛhya apidhāya iti arthaḥ  aṅgulibhyām prorṇutya ninadam iva rathasya iva ghoṣaḥ  ninadaḥ tam iva śṛṇoti nadathuḥ iva ṛṣabha kūjitam iva śabdaḥ  yathā ca agneḥ bahis jvalata evam śabdam antar  śarīra upaśṛṇoti tad etad jyotiḥ dṛṣṭa śruta liṅga tvāt dṛṣṭam ca śrutam ca iti upāsīta tathā upāsanāt cakṣuṣyaḥ  darśanīyaḥ śrutaḥ  viśrutaḥ ca yad sparśa guṇa upāsana nimittam phalam tad rūpe sampādayati cakṣuṣya iti rūpa sparśayoḥ sahabhāvi tvāt  iṣṭa tvāt ca darśanīya tāyāḥ evam ca vidyāyāḥ phalam upapannam syāt na tu mṛdutva ādi sparśavat tve ya evam yathā uktau guṇau veda svarga loka pratipattiḥ tu uktam adṛṣṭam phalam dvis abhyāsa ādara arthaḥ punar tasya eva tripāda mṛtasya brahmaṇaḥ  ananta guṇavataḥ  ananta śakteḥ aneka bheda upāsyasya viśiṣṭa guṇa śaktimatvena upāsanam vidhitsan  āha sarvam samastaṃ khalu iti vākya alaṅkāra arthaḥ  nipātaḥ idam jagat nāma rūpa vikṛtam pratyakṣa ādi viṣayam brahma kāraṇam vṛddhatama tvāt brahma katham sarvasya brahma tvam iti ata āha tad jalān iti tasmāt brahmaṇaḥ  jātam tejaḥ ban  ādi krameṇa sarvam atas tad jam tathā tena eva janana krameṇa pratiloma tayā tasmin  eva brahmaṇi līyate tad ātma tayā śliṣyata iti tallam tathā tasmin  eva sthiti kāle aniti prāṇiti ceṣṭata iti evam brahma ātma tayā triṣu kāleṣu aviśiṣṭam tad vyatirekeṇa agrahaṇāt  atas tad eva idam jagat  yathā ca idam tad eva ekam advitīyam tathā ṣaṣṭhe vistareṇa vakṣyāmaḥ yasmāt ca sarvam idam brahma atas  śāntaḥ  rāga dveṣa ādi doṣa rahitaḥ saṃyataḥ sanyat tad sarvam brahma tad vakṣyamāṇaiḥ guṇaiḥ upāsīta katham upāsīta kratum kurvīta kratuḥ niścayaḥ  adhyavasāya evam eva na anyathā iti avicalaḥ pratyayaḥ tam kratum kurvīta upāsīta iti anena vyavahitena sambandhaḥ kim punar  kratu karaṇena kartavyam prayojanam katham vā kratuḥ kartavyaḥ kratu karaṇam ca abhipreta artha siddhi sādhanam katham iti asya arthasya pratipādana artham atha ityādi granthaḥ atha khalu iti hetu arthaḥ yasmāt kratu mayaḥ kratu prāyaḥ adhyavasāya ātmakaḥ puruṣaḥ  jīvaḥ yathākratuḥ yādṛśaḥ kratuḥ asya saḥ  ayam yathākratuḥ yathā adhyavasāyaḥ  yādṛś niścayaḥ  asmin  loke jīvan  iha puruṣaḥ  bhavati tathā itaḥ asmāt dehāt pretya mṛtvā bhavati kratu anurūpa phala ātmakaḥ  bhavati iti arthaḥ evam hi etad śāsrataḥ dṛṣṭam yam yam vā api smaran bhāvam tyajati ante kalevaram ityādi yata evam vyavasthā śāsra dṛṣṭātas  sa evam jānan katum kurvīta yādṛśam kratum vakṣyāmaḥ tam yata evam śāsra prāmāṇyāt upapadyate kratu anurūpam phalam atas  sa kartavyaḥ kratuḥ katham manaḥ mayaḥ  manaḥ prāyaḥ manute anena iti manaḥ tad sva vṛttyā viṣayeṣu pravṛttam bhavati tena manasā tad mayaḥ tathā pravṛtta iva tad prāyaḥ nivṛtta iva ca ata eva prāṇa śarīraḥ prāṇaḥ  liṅga ātmā vijñāna kriyā śakti dvaya saṃmīrchitaḥ yaḥ  vai prāṇaḥ sā prajñā yā vā prajñā sa prāṇaḥ iti śruteḥ sa śarīram yasya sa prāṇa śarīraḥ manaḥ mayaḥ úāṇa śarīra netā iti ca śruti antarāt bhā rūpaḥ bhā dīptiḥ caitanya lakṣaṇam rūpam yasya sa bhā rūpaḥ satya saṅkalpaḥ satyā avitathāḥ saṅkalpā yasya saḥ  ayam satya saṅkalpaḥ na yathā saṃsāriṇa iva anaikāntika phalaḥ saṅkalpa īśvarasya iti arthaḥ anṛtena mithyā phalatva hetunā pratyūḍha tvāt saṅkalpasya mithyā phala tvam vakṣyati anṛtena hi pratyūḍhā iti ākāśa ātmā ākāśa iva ātmā svarūpam yasya sa ākāśa ātmā sarva gata tvam sūkṣma tvam rūpa dihīna tvam ca ākāśa tulyatā īśvarasya sarva karmā sarvam viśvam tena īśvareṇa kriyata iti jagat sarvam karma asya sa sarva karmā sa hi sarvasya kartā iti śruteḥ sarva kāmaḥ sarve kāmā doṣa rahitā asya iti sarva kāmaḥ dharma viruddhaḥ  bhūteṣu kāmaḥ  asmi iti smṛteḥ nanu kāmaḥ  asmi iti vacanāt iha bahuvrīhiḥ tathā kāmaḥ  asmi iti smṛti arthaḥ  vācyaḥ sarva gandhaḥ sarve gandhāḥ sukha karā asya saḥ  ayam sarva gandhaḥ puṇyaḥ  gandhaḥ pṛthivyām iti smṛteḥ tathā rasā api vijñeyāḥ apuṇya gandha rasa grahaṇasya pāpma sambandha nimittatva śravaṇāt  tasmāt tena ubhayam jighrati surabhi ca durgandhi ca pāpmanā hi eṣu viddhaḥ iti śruteḥ na ca pāpma saṃsarga īśvarasya avidyā ādi doṣasya anupapatteḥ sarvam idam jagat abhyāttaḥ  abhivyāptaḥ atateḥ vyāpti arthasya kartari niṣṭhā tathā avākī ucyate anayā iti vāc vāc eva vākaḥ dvā vacerghañantasya pratiṣedhena pratiṣidhyante tāni apāṇi pādaḥ  javanaḥ  grahītā paśyati acakṣuḥ sa śṛṇoti akarṇaḥ ityādi mantra varṇāt anādaraḥ  asaṃbhramaḥ aprāpta prāptau hi saṃbhramaḥ syāt anāpta kāmasya na tu āpta pṛthivyā ityādinā jyāyaḥ parimāṇāt ca jyāyaḥ tvam darśayan  ananta parimāṇa tvam darśayati manaḥ maya ityādinā jyā yānebhyaḥ  lokebhya iti antena yathā ukta guṇa lakṣaṇa īśvaraḥ  dhyeyaḥ  na tu tad mayatva ādi guṇa viśiṣṭa eva īśvaraḥ  dhyeyaḥ ata eva ṣaṣṭha saptamayoḥ iva tad tvam asya ātmā eva idam sarvam iti na iha svārājye abhiṣiñcati eṣa ma ātmā etad brahma etam itas  pratyābhisambhavitā asmi iti liṅgāt na tu ātma śabdena pratyagātmā eva ucyate mama iti ṣaṣṭhyāḥ sambandha artha pratyāyaka tvāt etam abhisambhavitā asmi iti ca karma kartṛtva nirdeśāt  nanu ṣaṣṭhe api atha sampatsya iti sat sampatteḥ kāla antarita tvam darśayati na ārabdha saṃskāra śeṣa sthiti artha paratvāt na kāla antarita artha tā anyathā tad tvam asi iti etasya arthasya bādha prasaṅgāt  yadi api ātma śabdasya pratyak artha tvam sarvam khalu idam brahma iti ca prakṛtam eṣa ma ātma antar hṛdaya etad brahmā iti ucyate tathā api antardhānam īṣat aparityajya eva etam ātmānam itas  asmāt śarīrāt pretya abhisambhavitā asmi iti uktam yathākratu rūpasya ātmanaḥ pratipattā asmi iti yasya evaṃvidaḥ syāt bhavet addhā satyam evam syām aham pretya evam na syām iti na ca vicikitsā asti iti etasmin  arthe kratu phala sambandhe sa tathā eva īśvara bhāvam pratipadyate vidvān iti etad āha sma uktavān kila śāṇḍalyaḥ  nāma ṛṣiḥ dvis abhyāsa ādara arthaḥ asya kule vīraḥ  jāyata iti uktam na vīra janma mātram dhyātvā dvis vacanam ādara artham putra āyuṣa upāsana m uktam japaḥ ca atha idānīm ātmanaḥ  dīrgha jīvanāya idam upāsanam japam ca vidadhat āha jīvanhi svayam putra ādi phalena yujyate na anyathā iti yajña tvam katham tasya puruṣasya yāni caturviṃśati varṣāṇi āyuṣaḥ tad prātaḥsavanam yajñasya kena sāmānyena iti āha caturviṃśati akṣarā gāyatraḥ  chandaḥ gāyatram gāyatrī chandaskam hi vidhiyajñasya vasavaḥ  devāḥ prāptā iti atas  viśinaṣṭi prāṇā vāva vasavaḥ  vāc ādayaḥ  vāyavaḥ ca tehi yasmāt idam puruṣa ādi prāṇijātam ete vāsayanti prāṇeṣu hi dehe vatsatu sarvam ida vasati na anyathā iti atas  vasanāt vāsanāt ca vasavaḥ tam ced yajña sampāditam etasmin prātar  savana sampanne vayasi kiñcid vyādhi ādi maraṇa śaṅkā raṇam upatapet duḥkham utpādayet sa tadā yajña sampādī puruṣa ātmānam yajñam evayasyataḥ  rudrāḥ tathā ādityāḥ prāṇāḥ te hi idam śabda ādi jātam ādadate ata ādityāḥ tṛtīyasavanam āyuḥ ṣoḍaśa uttara varṣa śatam samāpayata anusanta nuta yajñam samāpayata iti arthaḥ samānam anyat  niścitā hi vidyā phalāya iti etad darśayan  udāharati etad yajña darśanam ha sma vai kila tad vidvān āha mahidāsaḥ  nāmataḥ itarāyāḥ  apatyam aitareyaḥ kim kasmāt me mama etad upatapanam upatapasi sa ajīvat  anyaḥ  api evaṃniścaḥ ṣoḍaśam varṣa śatam prajīvati ya evam yathā uktam yajña sampādanam veda jānāti sa iti arthaḥ sa yad aśi śiṣatoti ādi yajña sāmānya nirdeśaḥ puruṣasya pūrveṇa eva sambadhyate yad aśiśiṣati aśitum icchati tathā pipāsati pātum icchati yad na ramata iṣṭa ādya prāpti nimittam yadā evan jātīyakam duḥkham anubhavati tā asya dīkṣāḥ duḥkha sāmānyāt vidhi yajñasya iva atha yad aśnāti yad pibati yad ramate ratim ca anubhavati iṣṭa ādi saṃyogāt tad upasadaiḥ samāna tām eti upasadām ca payaḥ vratatva nimittam sukham asti alpa bhojanīyāni ca ahānya āśvāsannāni iti praśvāsaḥ  atas  aśana ādīnām upasadām ca sāmānyam atha yad hasati yad jakṣati bhakṣayati yad maithunam carati stuta śasraiḥ eva tad samāna tām eti śabdavattva sāmānyāt atha yad tapaḥ  dānam ārjavam ahiṃsā satya vacanam iti tā asya dakṣiṇāḥ dharma puṣṭi karatva sāmānyāt  yasmāt ca yajñaḥ puraṣaḥ tasmāt tam janayiṣyati mātā yadā tad āhuḥ anye soṣyati iti tasya mātaram yadā ca prasūtā bhavati tadā asoṣṭa pūrṇikā iti vidhiyajña iva soṣyati somam devadattaḥ  asa uṣṭa somam yajñadatta iti atas  śabda sāmānyāt vā puruṣaḥ  yajñaḥ punar utpādanam eva asya tatpuruṣa ākhyasya yajñasya yad soṣyati asa uṣṭa iti śabda sambandhi tvam vidhiyajñasya iva kiñca tad maraṇam eva asya puruṣa yajñasya avabhṛthaḥ samāpti sāmānyāt  tad ha etad yajña darśanam ghoraḥ  nāmata āṅgirasaḥ  gotrataḥ kṛṣṇāya devakīputrāya śiṣya ayokatvā uvāca tad etad trayam ityādi vyavahitena sambandhaḥ sa ca etad darśanam śrutvā apipāsa eva āmya abhyaḥ  vidyā abhyaḥ  babhūva ittham ca viśiṣṭā iyam vidyā yad kṛṣṇasya devakīputrasya anyām vidyām prati tṛṣ viccheda karī iti puruṣa yajña vidyām stauti ghora āṅgirasaḥ kṛṣṇāya uktvā imām vidyām kim uvāca iti tad āha sa evam yathā ukta yajña vidanta velāyām maraṇa kāla etad mantra trayam pratipadyeta japet iti arthaḥ kim tad akṣitam akṣīṇam akṣatam vāsi iti ekam yajuḥ sāmarthyāt āditya stham prāṇam ca ekīkṛtya āha tathā tam eva aha acyutam svarūpāt apracyutam asi iti dvitīyam yajuḥ prāṇa saṃśitam prāṇaḥ ca sa saṃśitam samyak tanūkṛtam ca sūkṣmam tad tvam asi iti tṛtīyam yajuḥ tatra etasmin  arthe vidyā stuti pare dve ṛcau mantrau bhavataḥ  na japa arthe trayam pratipadyeta iti tritva saṃkhyā bādhanāt  pañca saṃkhyā hi tadā syāt  ādiditi atra ākārasya anubandhastakāraḥ  anarthaka icchabdaḥ ca pratnasya cirantanasya purāṇasya iti arthaḥ retasaḥ kāraṇasya bīja bhūtasya jagataḥ sadā ākhyasya jyotiḥ prakāśam paśyanti āśabda utsṛṣṭa anubandhaḥ paśyanti iti anena sambadhyate kim tad jayotiḥ paśyanti vāsaram aharahar iva tad sarvatas  vyāptam brahmaṇaḥ  jyotiḥ nivṛtta cakṣuṣaḥ  brahma vidaḥ  brahmacarya ādi nivṛtti sādhanaiḥ śuddha antaḥkaraṇā ā samantatas  jyotiḥ paśyanti iti arthaḥ paraḥ param iti liṅga vyatyayena jyotiṣparatvāt  yad idhyate dīpyate divi rasānām raśmīnām prāṇānām ca jagata īraṇāt sūryaḥ tam udaganma gatavantaḥ  jyotiḥ uttamam sarva jyotirbhya utkṛṣṭatama mahaḥ prāptā vayam iti arthaḥ idam tad jyotiḥ yad ṛgbhyām stutam yad yajuḥ trayeṇa prakāśitam dvis abhyāsaḥ  yajña kalpanā parisamāpti arthaḥ manaḥ maya īśvara ukta ākāśa ātmā iti ca brahmaṇaḥ  guṇa eka deśa tvena atha idānīm mana ākāśayoḥ samasta brahma dṛṣṭi vidhāna artha ārambhaḥ  manaḥ  brahma ityādi manaḥ  manute anena iti antaḥkaraṇam tad brahma param iti upāsīta iti etad ātma viṣayam darśanam adhyātmam atha adhidaivatam devatā viṣayam idam vakṣyāmaḥ ākāśaḥ  brahma iti upāsīta evam abhuyam adhyātmam adhidaivatam ca ubhayam brahma dṛṣṭi viṣayam ādiṣṭam upadiṣṭam bhavati ākāśa manasoḥ sūkṣma tvāt  manasā upalabhya tvāt ca brahmaṇaḥ  yogyam manaḥ  brahma dṛṣṭeḥ ākāśaḥ ca sarva gata tvāt sūkṣma tvāt upādhi hīna tvāt ca tad etad mana ākhyam catuṣpād brahma catvāraḥ pādā asya iti katham catuṣpād tvam manasaḥ  brahmaṇa iti āha vāc prāṇaḥ cakṣuḥ śrotram iti ete pādā iti adhyātmam atha adhidaivatam ākāśasya brahmaṇaḥ  agniḥ vāyuḥ ādityaḥ  diśa iti ete evam ubhayam eva catuṣpād brahma ādiṣṭam bhavati adhyātmam ca eva adhidaivatam ca tatra vāc eva manasaḥ  brahmaṇaḥ caturthaḥ pāda itara pāda traya apekṣayā vācā hi pādena iva gavā ādi vaktavya viṣayam prati pratiṣṭhati atas  manasaḥ pāda iva vāc  tathā prāṇaḥ  ghrāṇaḥ pādaḥ tena api gandha viṣayam prati caṅkramati tathā cakṣuḥ pādaḥ śrotram pāda iti evam adhyātmam catuṣpāttavam manasaḥ  brahmaṇaḥ atha adhidaivatam agnivāyu āditya diśa ākāśasya brahmaṇa udāra iva goḥ pādā vilagnā upalabhyante tena tasya ākāśasya agni ādayaḥ pādā ucyante evam ubhayam adhyātmam ca eva adhidaivatam catuṣpāda ādiṣṭam bhavati tatra vāc eva manasaḥ  brahmaṇaḥ caturthaḥ pādaḥ saḥ  agninā adhidaivatena jyotiṣā bhāti ca brahmavarcasena ya evam yathā uktam vedaḥ tathā prāṇa eva brahmaṇaḥ caturthaḥ pādaḥ sa vāyunā gandhāya bhāti ca tapati ca tatā cakṣuḥ ādityena rūpa grahaṇāya śrotram digbhiḥ śabda grahaṇāya vidyā phalam samānam sarvatra brahma sampattiḥ adṛṣṭam phalam ya evam veda dvis uktiḥ darśana samāpti arthā ādityaḥ  brahmaṇaḥ pāda ukta iti tasmin sakala brahma dṛṣṭi artham idam ārabhyate ādityaḥ  brahma iti ādeśa upadeśaḥ tasya upavyākhyānam kriyate stuti artham asat avyakṛta nāma rūpam idam jagat aśeṣam agre prāk avasthāyām utpatteḥ āsīt na tu asat eva katham asataḥ sajjāyeta iti asat kārya tvasya pratiṣedhāt  nanviha asat eva iti vidhānāt vikalpaḥ syāt  na kriyāsu iva vastuni vikalpa anupapatteḥ katham tarhi idamasat eva iti nanu avocāmā vyākṛta nāma rūpa tvāt asa diva asat iti nanu eva śabdaḥ  avadhāraṇa arthaḥ satyam evam na tu sattva abhāvam avadhārayati kim tarhi vyākṛta nāma rūpa abhāvam avadhārayati nāma rūpa vyākṛta viṣaye sat śabda prayogaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ tad ca nāma rūpa vyākaraṇam āditya āyattam prāyaśas  jagataḥ tad abhāve hi andham tama idam na prajñāyeta kiñcana iti atas tad stuti pare vākye sat api idam rājñaḥ kulam sarva guṇa sampanne pūrṇavarmaṇi rājani asati iti tadvat  na ca sattvam asat tvam veha jagataḥ pratipipādayiṣitam ādityaḥ  brahma iti ādeśa paratvāt upasaṃhariṣyati anta ādityam brahma iti upāsta iti tad sadā āsīt tad asat śabda vācyam prāk utpatteḥ stimitam anispandam asat iva satkārya abhimukham īṣat upajāta pravṛtti sadā āsīt tatas  labdha parispandam tad samabhavat alpatara nāma rūpa vyākaraṇena aṅkurībhūtam i va bījam tatas  api krameṇa sthūlībhavat tadadbhya āṇḍam samavartata saṃvṛttam āṇḍam iti dairdhyam chāndasam tad aṇḍam saṃvatsarasya kālasya prasiddhasya mātrām parimāṇam abhinna svarūpam eva āśayata sthitam babhūva tad tatas  saṃvatsara parimāṇāt kālāt ūrdhvam nirabhidyata nirbhinnam vayasām iva aṇḍam tasya nirbhinnasya aṇḍasya kapāle dve rajatam ca suvarṇam ca abhavatām saṃvṛtte tad tayoḥ kapālayoḥ yad rajatam kapālam āsīt seyam pṛthivī pṛthivī upalakṣitam adhas  aṇḍa kapālam iti arthaḥ yad suvarṇam kapālam sā dyauḥ dyu loka upalakṣitam ūrdhvam kapālam iti arthaḥ yad jara āyu garbha pariveṣṭanam sthūlamaṇḍasya dvi śakalībhāva kāla āsīt te parvatā babhūvuḥ yad ulvam sūkṣmam garbha pariveṣṭanam tad saha medyaiḥ sa meghaḥ  nīhāraḥ  avaśyāyaḥ babhūva iti arthaḥ yā garbhasya jātasya dehe dhamanayaḥ śirāḥ tā nadyaḥ  babhūvuḥ yad tasya bastau bhavam vāsteyam udakam sa samudraḥ atha yad tad ajāyata garbha rūpam tasmin  aṇḍe saḥ  asau  ādityaḥ tam ādityam jāyamānam ghoṣāḥ śabdā ulūlava urūravaḥ  vistīrṇa ravā udatiṣṭhat   utthitavanta īśvarasya iva iha prathama putra janmani sarvāṇi ca sthāvara jaṅgamāni bhūtāni sarve ca teṣām bhūtānām kāmāḥ kāmyanta iti viṣayāḥ strī vasra anna ādayaḥ yasmāt āditya janma nimittā bhūta kāma utpattiḥ tasmāt adyatve api tasya āditi asya udayam prati pratyāyanam pratyasta gamanam ca pratyathavā punar  punar  pratyāgamanam pratyāyanam tad prati tad nimittīkṛtyā iti arthaḥ sarvāṇi ca bhūtāni sarve ca kāmā ghoṣā ulūlavaḥ ca anūttiṣṭhanti prasiddham hi etad udaya ādau savituḥ sa yaḥ kaścid etam evam yathā uktamahimānam vidvān san  ādityam brahma iti upāste sa tad bhāvam pratipadyata iti arthaḥ kiñca dṛṣṭam phalam abhyāśaḥ kṣipram tad vidaḥ  yad iti kriyā viśeṣaṇam enam evaṃvidam sādhavaḥ śobhanā ghoṣāḥ sādhu tvam ghoṣa ādīnām yad upabhoge pāpa anubandha abhāvaḥ ā ca gaccheyuḥ āga  cheyuḥ ca upa ca nimreḍeḥ an  upa nimreḍeran  ca na kevalam āgamana mātram ghoṣāṇām upasukhayeyuḥ ca upasukham ca kuryar iti arthaḥ dvis abhyāsaḥ  adhyāya parisamāpti arthaḥ ādara arthaḥ ca vāyu prāṇayoḥ brahmaṇaḥ pāda dṛṣṭi adhyāsaḥ purastāt varṇitaḥ atha idānīm tayoḥ sākṣāt brahma tvena upāsya tvāya uttaram ārabhyate sukha avabodha artha ākhyāyikā vidyā dāna grahaṇa vidhi pradarśana arthā ca śraddhā anna dānān uddhatatva ādīnām ca vidyā prāpti sādhana tvam pradarśyata ākhyāyikayā jāna śrutiḥ jana śrutasya apatyam haḥ aitihya arthaḥ putrasya pautraḥ pautrāyaṇaḥ sa eva śraddhā deyaḥ śraddhā puraḥsaram eva brāhmaṇa ādibhyaḥ  deyam asya iti śraddhā deyaḥ bahu dāyī prabhūtam dātum śīlam asya iti bahu dāyī bahu pākyaḥ  bahu paktavyam ahani ahani gṛhe yasya asaubahu pākyaḥ bhojana arthibhyaḥ  bahu asya gṛhe annam pacyata iti arthaḥ evaṅguṇa sampannaḥ  asau jānaśrutiḥ pautrāyaṇaḥ  viśiṣṭe deśe kāle ca kasmiṃścid āsa babhūva sa ha sarvatas  sarvāsu dikṣu grāmeṣu nagareṣu ca āvasathānetya vasanti yeṣu iti āvasathāḥ tān māpayāñcakre kāritavān iti arthaḥ sarvata eva me mama annam teṣu āvasatheṣu vasantaḥ  atsyanti bhokṣyanta iti evam abhiprāyaḥ tatra evam sati rājani tasmin dharma kāle harmya tala sthe atha ha haṃsā niśāyām rātrau  atipetuḥ ṛṣayaḥ  devatā vā rājñaḥ  anna dāna guṇaiḥ toṣitāḥ santaḥ  haṃsa arūpā bhūtvā rājñaḥ  darśana gocare atipetuḥ tad tasmin kāle teṣām patatām haṃsānām ekaḥ pṛṣṭhatas  patan  agratas  patantam haṃsam abhyuvāda abhyuktavān haḥ haḥ ayi iti bhaḥ bhaḥ iti sambodhya bhallākṣa bhallākṣā iti ādaram darśayan yathā paśya paśya āścaryam iti tadvat  bhallākṣā iti manda dṛṣṭi tvam sūcayan  āha athavā samyak brahma darśana abhimānavat tvāt tasya asakṛt upālabdhaḥ tena pīḍyamānaḥ  amarṣitayā tad sūcayati bhallākṣā iti jānaśruteḥ pautrāyaṇasya samam tulyam divā dyu lokena jyotiḥ prabhāsvaram anna dāna ādi janita prabhāva jamātatam vyāptam dyu loka spṛś iti arthaḥ divāhnā vā samam jyotiḥ iti etad  tad mā prasāṅkṣīḥ sañjanam saktim tena jyotiṣā sambandham mā kārṣīḥ iti arthaḥ tad prasañjanena tad jyotiḥ tvā tvām mā pradhākṣīḥ mā dahatu iti arthaḥ puruṣa vyatyanena mā pradhākṣīt iti tam evam uktavantam para itaraḥ  agra gāmī pratyuvācāre nikṛṣṭaḥ  ayam rājā varākaḥ tam kamu enam santam kena māhātmyena yuktam santam iti kutsayati enam evam sa bahu mānam etad vacanam āttha raikvam iva sayugvānam saha yugvanā gantryā vartata iti sa yugvā raikvaḥ tam iva attha enam ananurūpam asmin  ayuktam īdṛśam vaktum raikva iva iti abhiprāyaḥ itaraḥ ca āha yaḥ  nu katham tvayā ucyate sa yugvā raikva iti uktavantam bhallākṣa āha śṛṇu yathā sa raikvaḥ yathā loke kṛtāyaḥ kṛtaḥ  nāma ayaḥ dyūta samaye prasiddhaḥ caturaṅkaḥ sa yadā jayati dyūte pravṛttānām tasmai vijitāya tad artham itare tri dvi eka aṅkā adhare ayāḥ tretā dvāpara kali nāmānaḥ saṃyanti saṃgacchante antarbhavanti catur aṅke kṛtāye tri dvi eka aṅkānām vidyamāna tvāt tad antarbhavanti iti arthaḥ yathā ayam dṛṣṭānta evam enam raikvam kṛta aya sthānīyam tretā ādyāya sthānīyam sarvam tad abhisamā iti antar bhavati raikve kim tad yad kiñca loke sarvāḥ prajāḥ sādhu śobhanam dharma jātam kurvanti tad sarvam raikvasya dharme antarbhavati tasya ca phale sarva prāṇi dharma phalam antarbhavati iti arthaḥ tathā anyaḥ  api kaścid yaḥ tad vedyam veda kim tad yad vedyam sa raikvaḥ  veda tad vedyam anyaḥ api yaḥ  veda tam api sarva prāṇi dharma jātam tad phalam ca raikvam iva abhisameti iti anuvartate sa evaṃbhūtaḥ  mayā vidvān etad ikta evam uktaḥ  raikvavat sa eva kṛtāya sthānīyaḥ  bhavati iti abhiprāyaḥ tad u ha tad etad īdṛśam haṃsa vākyam ātmanaḥ kutsārūpam anyasya viduṣaḥ  raikva ādeḥ praśaṃsā rūpam upaśuśrāva śrutavān harmya tala sthaḥ  rājā jānaśrutiḥ pautrāyaṇaḥ tad ca haṃsa vākyam smaran  eva paunaḥ punyena rātri śeṣam ativāhayāmāsa tatas  sa bandibhī rājā stuti yuktābhiḥ vāgbhiḥ pratibodhyamāna uvāca kṣattāram saṃjihāna eva śayanam nidrām vā parityajan  eva he aṅga vatsāre sa sayugvānam iva raikvam āttha kim mām sa eva stuti arhe na aham iti abhiprāyaḥ athavā sayugvānam raikvam āttha gatvā mama tad didṛkṣā ā ta t eva śabdaḥ  avadhāraṇa arthaḥ  anartha kaḥ  vā vācyaḥ sa ca kṣattā pratyuvāca raikva ānayana kāmaḥ  rājñaḥ  abhiprāya jñaḥ  yaḥ  nu katham sa yugvā raikva iti rājñā evam ca ukta ānetum tad cihnam jñatum icchanyaḥ  nu katham sa yugvā raikva iti avocat sa ca bhallākṣa vacanam eva avocat tasya smaran sa ha kṣattā nagaram grāmam vā gatvā anviṣya raikvam na avidam na vyajñāsiṣam iti pratyeyāya pratyāgatavān tam ha uvāca kṣattaram are yatra brāhmaṇasya brahma vida ekānte araṇye nadī pulina ādau vivikte deśe anveṣaṇa anumārgaṇam bhavati tad tatra enam raikvam archa ṛccha gaccha tatra mārgaṇam kuru iti arthaḥ iti uktaḥ kṣattā an viṣya tam vijane deśe adhastāt śakaṭasya gantryāḥ pāmānam kharjūm kaṣamāṇam kaṇḍūyamānam dṛṣṭvā ayam nūnam sa yugvā raikva iti upa samīpa upaviveśa vinayena upaviṣṭavān tam ca raikvam ha abhyuvāda uktavān tvam asi he bhagavaḥ  bhagavan sayugvā raikva iti evam pṛṣṭaḥ  aham asmi hi arā ara iti hāna ādara eva pratijajñe abhyupagatavān sa tam vijñāya  idam vijñātavān asmi iti pratyeyāya pratyāgata iti arthaḥ tad tatra ṛṣeḥ gārhasthyam pratyabhiprayam buddhvā dhana arthitām ca u ha eva jānaśrutiḥ pautrāyaṇaḥ ṣaṣ śatāni gavām niṣkam kaṇṭha hāram aśvatarī ratham aśva tarībhyām yuktam ratham tad ādāya dhanam gṛhītvā praticakrame raikvam prati gatavān tam ca gatvā abhyuvāda ha abhyuktavān he raikva gavām ṣaṣ śatāni imāni tubhyam mayā ānītāni ayam niṣkaḥ  aśvatarī rathaḥ ca ayam etad dhanam ādatsva bhagavaḥ  anuśādhi ca me mām etām yām ca devatām tvam upāḥse tad devatā upadeśena mām anuśādhi iti arthaḥ tam evam uktavantam rājānam pratyuvāca paraḥ  raikvaḥ aha iti ayam nipātaḥ  vinigraha arthīyaḥ  anyatra iha tu anarthakaḥ eva śabdasya pṛthak prayogāt  hāretvā hāreṇa yuktetvā gantrī sā iyam hāretvā gobhiḥ saha tava eva astu tiṣṭhatu na mama aparyāptena karma artham anena prayojanam iti abhiprāyaḥ  he śūdra iti nanu rājā asau kṣattṛ sambandhāt sa ha kṣattāram uvāca iti uktam vidyā grahaṇāya ca brāhmaṇa samīpa upagamāt śūdrasya ca anadhikārāt katham idam ananu rūpam raikveṇa ucyate he śūdra iti tatra āhuḥ ācāryāḥ haṃsa vacana śravaṇāt śuc enam āviveśa tena asau śucā śrutvā raikvasya mahimānam vā ādravati iti ṛṣiḥ ātmanaḥ parokṣa jña tām darśayan śūdrā iti āha iti śūdravat vā dhanena eva enam vidyā grahaṇāya upajagāma na ca śuśrūṣayā na tu jātyā eva śūdra iti apare punar āhuḥ alpam dhanam āhṛtam iti ruṣā eva enam uktavān śūdra iti liṅgam ca bahu āharaṇa upādānam dhanasya iti tad uharṣeḥ matam jñātvā punar eva jānaśrutiḥ pautrāyaṇaḥ  gavām sahasram adhikam jāyām carṣeḥ abhimatām duhitaram ātmanaḥ tad ādāya praticakrame krāntavān raikva idam gavām sahasra mayam niṣkaḥ  ayam aśvatarī ratha iyam jāyā artham mama duhitā ānīta ayam ca grāmaḥ  yasmin   āḥse tiṣṭhasi sa ca tvad arthe mayā kalpitaḥ tad etad sarvam ādāya anuśādhi eva mā mām he bhagava iti uktaḥ tasyāḥ  jāyā artham ānītāyā rājñaḥ  duhituḥ ha eva mukham dvāram vidyāyā dāne tīrtham upodgṛhṇan jānan  iti arthaḥ brahmacārī dhana dāyī medhāvī śrotriyaḥ priyaḥ vidyayā vā vidyā prāha tāni tīrthāni ṣaṣ mama iti vidyāyā vacanam vijñāyate hi evam jānan  upodgṛhṇan  uvāca uktavān ājahāra āhṛtavān bhavān yad imā gā yad ca anyat dhanam tad sādhu iti vākya śeṣaḥ śūdra iti pūrva ukta anukṛti mātram na tu kāraṇa antara apekṣayā pūrvavat  anena eva mukhena vidyā grahaṇa tīrthena ālāpayiṣyathā ālāpayasi iti mām bhāṣayasi iti arthaḥ te ha ete grāmā raikvaparṇā nāma vikhyātā mahā vṛṣeṣu deśeṣu yatra yeṣu grāmeṣu uvāsa uṣitavān raikvaḥ tān asau grāmānadāt asmai raikvāya rājā tasmai rājñe dhanam dattavate ha kilā uvāca vidyām sa raikvaḥ vāyuḥ vāva saṃvargaḥ  vāyuḥ bāhyaḥ  vāva iti avadhāraṇa arthaḥ saṃvargaḥ saṃvarjanāt saṃgrahaṇāt saṃgrasanāt vā saṃvargaḥ vakṣyamāṇā agni ādyā devatā ātma bhāvam āpādayati iti atas  saṃvargaḥ sa varjava ākhyaḥ  guṇa u dhyeyaḥ  vāyuvat  kṛta āya anta bharva dṛṣṭāntāt katham saṃvargat tvam vāyoḥ iti āha yadā yasmin kāle vā agniḥ udvāyati udvāsanam prāpnoti upaśāmyati tadā asau  agniḥ vāyum eva apyeti vāyu svābhāvyam apigacchati tathā yadā sūryaḥ  astam eti vāyum eva apyeti yadā candraḥ  astam eti vāyum eva apyeti nanu katham sūryācandramasoḥ svarūpa avasthitayoḥ vāyau  api gamanam na eṣa doṣaḥ astamane adarśana prāpteḥ vāyu nimitta tvāt  vāyunā hi astam nīyate sūryaḥ calanasya vāyu kārya tvāt athavā pralaye sūryācandramasoḥ svarūpa bhraṃśe tejaḥ rūpayoḥ vāyau  eva api gamanam syāt  tathā yadā apa ucchuṣyanti ucchoṣam āpnuvanti tadā vāyum eva apiyanti vāyuḥ hi yasmāt eva etān agni ādyāt mahā balān saṃvṛṅkte atas  vāyuḥ saṃvarga guṇa upāsya iti arthaḥ iti adhidaivatam devatāsu saṃvarga darśanam uktam atha anantaram adhyātmam ātmani saṃvarga darśanam idam ucyate prāṇaḥ  mukhyaḥ vāva saṃvargaḥ sa puruṣaḥ  yadā yasmin kāle svapiti prāṇam eva vāc apyeti vāyum iva agniḥ prāṇam cakṣuḥ prāṇam śrotram prāṇam manaḥ prāṇaḥ  hi yasmāt eva etān vāc ādīn sarvān saṃvṛṅkta iti tau vā etau dvau saṃvargau saṃvarjana guṇa u vāyuḥ eva deveṣu saṃvargaḥ prāṇaḥ prāṇeṣu vāc ādiṣu mukhyaḥ atha etayoḥ stuti artham iyam ākhyāyikā ārabhyate hā iti aitihya arthaḥ śaunakam ca śunakasya apatyam śonakam kāpeyam kapi gotram abhipratāriṇam ca nāmataḥ kakṣasenasya apatyam kākṣaseniṃ bhojanāya upaviṣṭau pariviṣyamāṇau sūpakāraiḥ brahmacārī brahma vid chaṇḍaḥ  bibhikṣe bhikṣitavān brahmacāriṇaḥ  brahma vid mānitām buddhvā tam jijñāsamānau tasmā u bhikṣām na jajatuḥ na dattavantau ha kim ayam bakṣyati iti sa ha uvāca brahmacārī mahātmanaḥ catura iti dvitīyā bahuvacanam deva ekaḥ  agni ādīn vāyuḥ vāc ādīn prāṇaḥ kaḥ sa prajāpatiḥ jagāra grasitavān kaḥ sa jagāra iti praśnam eke bhuvanasya bhavanti asmin bhūtāni iti bhuvanam bhūḥ ādiḥ sarvaḥ  lokaḥ tasya gopā gopāyitā rakṣitā goptā iti arthaḥ tam kam prajāpatim he kāpeya na abhipaśyanti na jānanti martyā maraṇa dharmāṇaḥ  avivekinaḥ  vā he abhipratārin bahudhā adhyātma adhidaivatādhibhūta prakāraiḥ vasantam yasmai vā etad ahani ahani anna madanāya āhriyate saṃskriyate ca tasmai prajāpataya etad annam na dattam iti tad u ha brahmacāriṇaḥ  vacanam śaunakaḥ kāpeyaḥ pratimanvānaḥ  manasā ālocayan brahmacāriṇam pratyeyāya ājagāma gatvā ca āha yam tvam avocaḥ  na paśyanti martyā iti tam vayam paśyāmaḥ katham ātmā sarvasya sthāvara jaṅgamasya kiñca devānām agni ādīnām ātmani saṃhṛtya grasitvā punar janita utpādayitā vāyu rūpeṇa adhidaivatam agni ādīnām adhyātmam ca prāṇa rūpeṇa vāc ādīnām prajānām ca danitā atha vā ātmā devānām agni vāc ādīnām janitā prajānām sthāvara jaṅgamānām hiraṇya daṃṣṭraḥ  abhagna daṃṣṭra iti yāvat  babhasaḥ bhakṣaṇa śīlaḥ anasūriḥ sūriḥ medhāvī na sūrira sūriḥ tad pratiṣedhaḥ  anasūriḥ sūrirā ivā iti arthaḥ mahāntam atipramāṇam aprameyam asya prajāpateḥ mahimānam vibhūtim āhuḥ brahma vidaḥ yasmāt svayam anyaiḥ anadyamānaḥ  abhakṣyamāṇaḥ  yad anannam agni vāc ādi devatā arūpam atti bhakṣayati iti vā iti nirarthakaḥ vayam he brahmacārin ā idam evam yathā ukta lakṣaṇam brahma vayamā upāsmahe vayam iti vyavahitena sambandhaḥ anye na vayam idam upāsmahe kim tarhi param eva brahma upāsmaha iti varṇayanti datta asmai bhikṣām iti avocat bhṛtyān tasmā u ha daduḥ te hi bhikṣām te vai ye grasyante agni ādayaḥ  yaḥ ca teṣām grasitā vāyuḥ pañca anye vāc ādibhyaḥ tathā anye tebhyaḥ pañca adhyātmam vāc ādayaḥ prāṇaḥ ca te sarve daśa santaḥ tad kṛtam bhavati te catur aṅka ekāya evam catvāraḥ tri aṅkāyaḥ evam trayaḥ  apare dvi aṅkāyaḥ evam dvau  anyau  ekāṅkāya evam ekaḥ  anya iti evam deśa santaḥ tad kṛtam bhavati yata evam tasmāt sarvāsu dikṣu daśasu api agni ādyā vāc ādyāḥ ca daśa saṃkhyā sāmānyāt annam eva daśa akṣarā virāj  virāj annam iti hi śrutiḥ atas  annam eva daśa saṃkhya tvāt  tatas  eva daśa kṛtam kṛte antarbhāvāt caturāya tvena iti avocāma sā eṣā virāj daśa saṃkhyā sati annam ca annādi at nādinī ca kṛta tvena daśa saṃkhyayā annam kṛta saṃkhyayā annādī tayā anna anna ādinyā idam sarvam jagat daśa diś saṃstham dṛṣṭam kṛta saṃkhyā bhūtayā upalabdham evaṃvidaḥ  asya sarvam kṛta saṃkhyā bhūtasya daśa diś saṃbaddham dṛṣṭam upalabdham bhavati kiñca anna ādaḥ ca bhavati ya evam veda yathā ukta darśī dvis abhyāsa upāsanam āpti arthaḥ sarvam vāc ādi agni ādi ca anna anna ādatva saṃstutam jagat ekīkṛtya ṣoḍaśadhā pravibhajya tasmin brahma dṛṣṭiḥ vidhātavyā iti ārabhyate śraddhā tapasoḥ brahma upāsana aṅgatva pradarśanāya ākhyāyikā satya kāmaḥ  ha nāmataḥ  ha śabda aitihya arthaḥ  jabālāyāḥ  apatyam jābālaḥ  jabalām svām mātaram āmantrayāñcakra āmantritavān brahmacaryam svādhyāya grahaṇāya he bhavati vivatsyāmi ācārya kule kiṅgotraḥ  aham kim asya mama gotram saḥ  aham nu aham asmi iti evam pṛṣṭā jabālā sā ha enam putram uvāca na aham etad tava gotram veda he tāta yad gotraḥ tvam asi kasmāt na vetsi iti uktā āha bahu bhartṛ gṛhe paricaryā jātam atithi abhyāgata ādi caranti aham paricāriṇī paricaranti iti paricaraṇa śīlā eva aham paricaraṇa citta tayā gotra ādi smaraṇe mama manaḥ  na abhūt  yauvane ca tad kāle tvām alabhe labdhavati asmi tadā eva te pitā uparatas  atas  anāthā aham sā aham etad na veda yad gotraḥ tvam asi jabālā tu nāma aham asmi satya kāmaḥ  nāma tvam asi sa tvam satyakāma eva aham jābālaḥ  asmi iti ācāryāya bruvīthāḥ yadi ācāryeṇa pṛṣṭa iti abhiprāyaḥ sa ha satya kāmaḥ  hāridru matam haridrumataḥ  apatyam hāridru matam gautamam gotrata etya gatvā uvāca brahmacaryam bhagavati pūjāvati tvayi vatsyāmyata upeyām upagaccheyam śiṣya tayā bhagavantam iti uktavantam tam ha uvāca gautamaḥ kiṅgotraḥ  nu somya asi iti vijñāta kula gotraḥ śiṣya upanetavya iti pṛṣṭaḥ pratyāha satyakāmaḥ sa ha uvāca na aham etad veda bhaḥ yad gotraḥ aham asmi kim tu apṛccham pṛṣṭavān asmi mātaram sā mayā pṛṣṭā mām pratyabravīt mātā bahu aham caranti ityādi pūrvavat  tasyāḥ  aham vacaḥ smarāmi saḥ  aham satya kāmaḥ  jābālaḥ  asmi bhaḥ iti tam ha uvāca gautamaḥ  na etad vacaḥ  abrāhmaṇaḥ  viśeṣeṇa vaktum arhati ārjava artha saṃyuktam ṛjavaḥ  hi brahmaṇā na itare svabhāvataḥ yasmāt na satyāt brāhmaṇa jāti dharmāt agā na apetavān asi atas  brāhmaṇam tvām upaneṣye atas  saṃskāra artham homāya samidham somya ahara iti uktvā tam upanīya kṛśānām abalānām gaḥ yūthāt nirākṛtya apakṛṣya catuḥśatā catvāri śatāni gavām uvāca imā gāḥ somya anusaṃvraja anugaccha iti uktaḥ tā araṇyam pratyabhiprasthāpayan  uvāca na asahasreṇa āpūrṇena sahasreṇa na āvarteya na pratyāgaccheyam sa evam uktvā gā araṇyam tṛṇa udaka bahulam dvandvaṃrahitam praveśya sa ha varṣa gaṇam dīrgham provāsa proṣitavān tāḥ samyak gāvaḥ  rakṣitā yadā yasmin kāle sahasram saṃpeduḥ saṃpannā babhūvuḥ tam etam śraddhā tapobhyām siddham vāyudevatā diś saṃbandhinī tuṣṭā sati ṛṣabham anupraviśya ṛṣabha āpanna anugrahāya atha ha enam ṛṣabhaḥ  abhyuvāda abhyuktavān satyakāma  iti saṃbodhya tamasau satya kāmaḥ  bhagava iti ha pratiśuśrāva prativacanam dadau praptāḥ somya sahasram smaḥ pūrṇā tava pratijñātaḥ prāpaya naḥ asmān ācārya kulam kiñca aham braṅmaṇaḥ parasya te tubhyam pādam bravāṇi kathayāni iti uktaḥ pratyuvāca bravītu kathayatu me mahyam bhagavān iti ukta ṛṣabhaḥ tasmai satyakāmāya ha uvāca prācī dikkalā brahmaṇaḥ pādasya caturthaḥ  bhāgaḥ tathā pratīcī dikkalā dakṣiṇā diś kala udīcī diś kala eṣa vai saimya brahmaṇaḥ pādaḥ catu śaṣkalaḥ catasraḥ kalā avayavā yasya saḥ  ayam catuṣkalaḥ pādaḥ  brahmaṇaḥ prakāśavān nāma prakāśavān iti avaṃ nāma abhidhānam yasya tathā uttare api pādāḥ trayaḥ catuṣkalā brahmaṇaḥ sa yaḥ kaścid evam yathoktam etam brahmaṇaḥ catuṣkalam pādam vidvān prakāśavān iti anena guṇena viśiṣṭam upāste tasya idam phalam prakāśavān asmin loke bhavati prakhyātaḥ  bhavati iti arthaḥ tathā adṛṣṭam phalam prakāśavataḥ  ha lokān deva ādi saṃbandhinaḥ  mṛtaḥ sañjayati prāpnoti ya etam eva vidvān  catuṣkalam pādam brahmaṇaḥ prakāśavān iti upāste saḥ  agniḥ te pādam vaktā iti upararāma ṛṣabhaḥ sa satyā kāmaḥ  ha śvobhūte paredyus naityakam nityam karma kṛtvā gā abhiprasthāpayāñcakāra ācārya kulam prati tāḥ śanais carantya ācārya kula abhimukhyaḥ prasthitā yatra yasmin kāle deśe abhi sāyam niśāyām abhisaṃbabhūvurekatra abhimukhyaḥ saṃbhūtāḥ tatra agnim upasamādhāya gā uparudhya samidham ādhāya paścāt agneḥ praṅupopaviveśa ṛṣabhavacaḥ  dhyāyan tam agniḥ abhyuvāda satyakāma iti saṃbodhya tamasau satya kāmaḥ  bhagava iti ha pratiśuśrāva prativacanam dadau brahmaṇaḥ somya te pādam bravāṇi iti bravītu me bhagavāni iti tasmai ha uvāca pṛthivī kalā antarikṣam kalā dyauḥ kalā samudraḥ kalā iti ātma gocaram eva darśanam agniḥ abravīt  eṣa vai somya catuṣkalaḥ pādaḥ  brahmaṇaḥ  anantavān nāma sa yaḥ kaścid yathā uktam pādam anantavat tvena guṇena upāste sa tathā eva tad guṇa u bhavati asmin  loke mṛtaḥ ca anantavataḥ  ha lokān sa jayati ya etam evam ityādi pūrvavat  haṃsaḥ te pādam vaktā iti sa ha śvobhūte gā abhiprasthāpayāñcakāra tā yatra abhisāyam babhūvuḥ tatra agnim upasamādhāyā gā uparudhya samidham ādhāya paścāt agneḥ prāṅupopaviveśa tam haṃsa upanipatya abhyuvāda satyakāma iti bhagava iti ha pratiśuśrāva saḥ  agniḥ haṃsaḥ te pādam vaktā iti uktavopara rāma haṃsa ādityaḥ śauklyāt patana sāmānyāt ca sa ha śvobhūta ityādi samānam agniḥkalā sūryaḥ kalā candraḥ kalā vidyut kalā eṣa vai somya iti jyotiḥ viṣayam eva ca darśanam provāca atas haṃsasya āditya tvam pratīyate vidvat phalam jyotiṣmān dīpti yuktaḥ  asmin  loke bhavati candrāt itya ādīnām jyotiṣmata eva ca mṛtvā lokān jayati samānam uttaram haṃsaḥ api mad guṣṭe pādam vaktā iti upararāma mad gurudaka caraḥ pakṣī sa ca apsambandhāt prāṇaḥ sa ha śvobhūta ityādi pūrvavat  sa ca madguḥ prāṇaḥ sva viṣayam eva ca darśanam uvāca prāṇaḥ kalā ityādi āyatanavān iti evam nāma āyatanam nāma manaḥ sarva karaṇa upahṛtānām bhogānām tad yasmin pāde vidyata iti āya tanavān nāma pādaḥ tam pādam tathā eva upāste yaḥ sa āyatanavān āśrayavān asmin  loke bhavati tathā āyatanavata eva sa avakāśān  lokān mṛtaḥ  jayati ya etam evam ityādi pūrvavat  sa evam brahma vid san prāpa ha prāptavān ācārya kulam tam ācāryaḥ  abhyuvāda satyakāma iti bhagava iti ha pratiśuśrāva brahma vid iva vai somya bhāsi prasanna indriyaḥ prahasita vadanaḥ ca niścintaḥ kṛtārthaḥ  brahma vid bhavati ata ācāryaḥ  brahma vid iva bhāsoti kaḥ  nu iti vitarkayan  uvāca kaḥ tvām anuśaśāsa iti sa ca āha satya kāmaḥ  anye manuṣyebhyaḥ devatā mām anuśiṣṭavatyaḥ kaḥ  anyaḥ  bhagavat śiṣyam mām manuṣyaḥ san  anuśāsitum utsaheta iti abhiprāyaḥ atas  anye manuṣyebhya iti ha pratijajñe pratijñātavān bhagavān  tu eva me kāme mama icchāyām brūyāt kim anyaiḥ uktena na aham tad gaṇayāmi iti abhiprāyaḥ kiñca śrutam hi yasmāt mama vidyata eva asmin  arthe bhagavat samebhya ṝṣibhyaḥ ācāryāt ha eva vidyā viditā sādhiṣṭham sādhutamatvam prāpat iti prāpnoti iti atas  bhagavān eba brūyāt iti ukta ācāryaḥ  abravīt tasmai tām eva daivataiḥ uktām vidyām atra ha na kiñcana ṣoḍaśa kalavidyāyāḥ kiñcid eka deśa mātram api na vīyāya na vigatam iti arthaḥ dvis abhyāsaḥ  vidyā parisamāpti arthaḥ punar brahma vidyām prakāra antareṇa vakṣyāmi iti ārabheta gatim ca tad vidaḥ  agnividyām ca ākhyāyikā pūrvavat śraddhā tapasoḥ brahma vidyā sādhanatva pradaśrana arthā upakosalaḥ  ha vai nāmataḥ kamalasya apatyam kāmalāyanaḥ satyakāme jābāle brahmacaryam uvāsa tasya haḥ etihyārthaḥ tasya ācāryasya dvādaśa varṣāṇi agnīn paricacāra agnīnām paricaraṇam kṛtavān sa ha sma ācāryaḥ  anyān brahmacāriṇaḥ svādhyāyam grāhayitvā samāvartayan  tam eva upakosalam ekam na samāvartayati sma ha tam ācārya jāyā uvāca taptaḥ brahmacārī kuśalam samyak agnīn paricacārīt paricaritavān bhagavān  ca agniṣu bhaktam na samāvartayati atas  asmad bhaktam na samāvartayati iti jñātvā tvām agnayaḥ  mā paripravocan garhām tava mā kuryuḥ atas  prabrūhi asmai vidyām iṣṭām upakosalāya iti tasmā evam jāyaya uktaḥ  api ha aprocya eva anuktvā eva kiñcid pravāsāṃcakre pravasitavān sa ha upakosalaḥ  vyādhinā mānasena duḥkhena anaśitum anaśanam kartum dadhre dhṛtavān manaḥ tam tūṣṇīm agni agāre avasthitam ācārya jāyā uvāca he brahmacārinnaśāna bhuṅkṣva kim nu kasmāt nu kāraṇāt na aśnāsi iti sa ha uvāca bahavaḥ  aneke asmin puruṣe akṛtārthe prākṛte kāmā icchāḥ kartavyam prati nānā atyayaḥ  atigamanam yeṣām vyādhīnām kartavya cintānām te nānā atyayā vyādhayaḥ kartavya tā prāpti nimittāni citta duḥkhāni iti arthaḥ taiḥ pratipūrṇaḥ  asmi atas  na āśiṣyāmi iti uktvā tūṣṇīṃbhūte brahmacāriṇi atha ha agnayaḥ śuśrūṣayā varjitāḥ kāruṇya āviṣṭāḥ santasrayaḥ  api sa mūdire saṃbhūya uktavantaḥ hanta idānīm asmai brahmacāriṇe asmad bhaktāya duḥkhitāya tapasvine śraddadhānāya sarve anuśāsmaḥ  anuprabravāma brahma vidyām iti evam saṃpradhārya tasmai ha ūcuḥ uktavantaḥ prāṇaḥ  brahma kam brahma kham brahma iti sa ha uvāca brahmacārī vijānāmi aham yad bhavadbhiḥ uktam prasiddha padārthaka tvāt prāṇaḥ  brahma iti yasmin sati jīvanam yad apagame ca na bhavati iti tasmin vāyu viśeṣe loke rūḍhaḥ  atas  yuktam brahma tvam tasya tena prasiddha padārthaka tvāt vijānāmi aham yad prāṇaḥ  brahma iti kam ca tu kham na vijānāmi iti nanu kaṅkhaṃśabdayoḥ api sukha ākāśa viṣaya tvena prasiddha padārthaka tvam eva kasmāt brahmacāriṇaḥ  ajñānam nṛnam sukhasya kaṃśa bda vācyasya kṣaṇa pradhvaṃsi tvāt khaṃśabda vācyasya ca ākāśasya acetanasya katham brahma tvam iti manyate katham ca bhavatām vākyam apramāṇam syāt iti atas  na vijānāmi iti āha tam evam uktantam brahmacāriṇam te ha agnayaḥ ūcuḥ yad vāva yad eva vayam kam avocāma tad eva kham ākāśam iti evam khena viśeṣyamāṇam kam viṣaya indri saṃyoga jāt sukhāt nivartitam syāt nīlena iva viśeṣyamāṇam utpalam rakta ādibhyaḥ yad eva kham iti ākāśam avocāma tad eva ca kam sukham iti jānīhi evam ca sukhena viśeṣyamāṇam kham bhautikāt acetanāt khāt nivartitam syāt nīlotpalavat eva sukham ākāśa stham na itarat laukikam ākāśam ca sukha āśrayam na itarat bhautikam iti arthaḥ nanu ākāśam ced sukhena viśeṣayitum iṣṭam astu anyataradeva viśeṣaṇam yad vāva kam tad eva kham iti atiriktam itarat  yad eva kham tad eva kam iti pūrva viśeṣeṇam vā nanu sukha ākāśayoḥ ubhayoḥ api laukika sukha ākāśābhyām vyāvṛttiḥ iṣṭa iti avocāma sukhena ākāśe viśeṣite vyāvṛttiḥ ubhayoḥ artha prāptā eva iti ced satyam evam kintu sukhena viśeṣitasya eva ākāśasya dhyeya tvam vihitam na tu ākāśa guṇasya viśeṣaṇasya sukhasya dhyeya tvam vihitam syāt  viśeṣaṇa upādānasya viśeṣya niyantṛ tvena eva upakṣayāt atas  khena sukham api viśeṣyate dhyeya tvāya kutas ca etad niścīyate kaṃśabdasya api brahma śabda sambandhāt kam brahma iti yadi hi sukha guṇa viśiṣṭasya khasya dhyeya tvam vivakṣitam syāt kam kham brahma iti brūyuḥ agnayaḥ prathamam na ca evam uktavantaḥ kim tarhi kam brahma kham brahma iti atas  brahmacāriṇaḥ  moha apanayanāya kaṅkhaṃśabdayoḥ itaretara viśeṣaṇa viśeṣyatva nirdeśaḥ  yukta eva yad vāva kam ityādiḥ tad etad agnibhiḥ uktam vākya artham asmad bodhāya śrutiḥ āha prāṇam ca ha asmai brahmacāriṇe tasya ākāśaḥ tad ākāśaḥ prāṇasya sambandhyāśraya tvena hārda ākāśa iti arthaḥ sukha guṇavattva nirdeśāt tam ca ākāśam sukha guṇa viśiṣṭam brahma tad stham ca prāṇam brahma samparkāt eva brahma iti ubhayam prāṇam ca ākāśam ca samuccitya brahmaṇī ūcuḥ agnaya iti sambhūya agnayaḥ  brahmacāriṇe brahma uktavantaḥ atha anantaram pratyekam sva sva viṣayām vidyām vaktum ārebhire tatra ādau  enam brahmacāriṇam gārhapatyaḥ  agniḥ anuśaśāsa pṛthivī agniḥ annam āditya iti mama etāḥ casraḥ tanavaḥ tatra ya āditya eṣa puruṣaḥ  dṛśyate saḥ  aham asmi gārhapatyaḥ  agniḥ yaḥ ca gārhapatyaḥ  agniḥ sa eva aham ādityaḥ  puruṣaḥ  asmi iti punar  parāvṛttyā sa eva aham asmi iti vacanam pṛthivī annayoḥ iva bhojyatva lakṣaṇayoḥ sambandhaḥ  na gārhapatya ādityayoḥ attṛtva paktṛtva prakāśana dharmā aviśiṣṭā iti ata eka tvam eva anayoḥ atyantam pṛthivī annayoḥ tu bhojya tvenābhyām sambandhaḥ sa yaḥ kaścid evam yathā uktam gārhapatyam agnim anna annāda tvena caturdhā pravibhaktam upāste saḥ  apahate vināśayati pāpa kṛtyām pāpam karma lokī lokavān  ca asmadāyena lokena āgneyena tad vān bhavati yathā vayam iha ca loke sarvam varṣa śatam āyuḥ eti prāpnoti jyok ujjavalam jīvati na aprakhyāta iti etad  na ca asya avarāḥ ca te puruṣāḥ ca asya viduṣaḥ santati jā iti arthaḥ na kṣīyante santati ucchedaḥ  na bhavati iti arthaḥ kim ca tam vayam upabhuñjāmaḥ pālayāmaḥ  asmin  ca loke jīvantam amuṣmin  ca para loke ya etam evam vidvān upāste yathektam tasya etad phalam iti arthaḥ atha ha enam anvāhārya pacanaḥ  anuśaśāsa dakṣiṇa agniḥ āpaḥ  diśaḥ  nakṣatrāṇi candramā iti etā mama catasraḥ tanavaḥ caturdhā aham anvāhārya pacana ātmānam pravibhajya avasthitaḥ tatra ya eṣa candramasi puruṣaḥ  dṛśyate saḥ  aham asmi sa eva aham asmi iti pūrvavat  anna sambandhāt jyotiṣṭva sāmānyāt ca anvāhārya pacana candramasoḥ eka tvan dakṣiṇā ṇa  diś sambandhāt ca apām nakṣatrāṇām ca pūrvavat anna tvena eva sambandhaḥ nakṣatrāṇām candramasaḥ  bhogyatva prasiddheḥ apānna utpādaka tvāt anna tvam dakṣiṇa agneḥ pṛthivīvat gārhapatyasya samānam anyat  atha ha enam āhavanīyaḥ  anuśaśāsa prāṇa ākāśaḥ  dyauḥ vidyut iti mama api etāḥ catasraḥ tanavaḥ ya eva vidyuti puruṣaḥ  dṛśyate saḥ  aham asmi ityādi pūrvavat sāmānyāt  divā dyvā  kāśayoḥ tu āśraya tvāt vidyut āhavanīyayoḥ bhogya tvena eva sambandhaḥ samānam anyat  te punar  sambhūya ūcuḥ hepa kosalā eṣā somya te tava asmad vidyā agni vidyā iti arthaḥ ātma vidyā pūrva uktā prāṇaḥ  brahma kam brahma kham brahma iti ca ācāryaḥ tu te gatim vaktā vidyā phala prāptaya iti uktvā uparemuḥ agnayaḥ ājagāma hāsya ācāryaḥ kālena tam ca śiṣyam ācāryaḥ  abhyuvāda upakosala iti bhagava iti ha pratiśuśrāva brahma vida iva somya te mukham prasannam bhāti kaḥ  nu tvā anuśa śāsa iti uktaḥ pratyāha kaḥ  nu mā anuśiṣyāt anuśāsanam kuryāt bhaḥ bhagavan  tvayi proṣita iti iha apa iva nihnute apanihnuta iva iti vyavahitena sambandhaḥ  na cāpa nihnute na ca yatāvat agnibhiḥ uktam bravīti iti abhiprāyaḥ katham ime agnayaḥ  mayā paricaritā uktavantaḥ  nūnam yatas tvām dṛṣṭvā vepamānā iva īdṛśā dṛśyante pūrva manyādṛśāḥ santa iti iha agnīn abhyūde abhyuktavān kākva agnīn darśayan kim nu somya kila te tubhyam avocan  agnaya iti pṛṣṭa iti evam idam uktavanta iti evam ha pratijajñe pratijñātavān pratīka mātram kiñcid na sarvam yathā uktam agnibhiḥ uktam avocat  yata āha ācāryaḥ  lokān vāva pṛthivī ādīn he somya kila te avocat na brahma sākalyena aham tu te tubhyam tad brahma yad icchasi tvam śrotum vakṣyāmi śṛṇu tasya mayā ucyamānasya brahmaṇaḥ  jñāna māhātmyam yathā puṣkara palāśe padma patra āpaḥ  na śilaṣyanta evam yatā vakṣyāmi brahma evaṃvidi pāpam karma na śilaṣyate na sambadhyata iti evam uktavatī ācārya āha upakosalaḥ  bravītu me bhagavān iti tasmai ha uvāca ācāryaḥ ya eṣaḥ  akṣiṇi puruṣaḥ  dṛśyate nivṛtta cakṣurbhiḥ brahmacarya ādi sādhana sampannaiḥ śāntaiḥ vivekibhiḥ dṛṣṭeḥ draṣṭā cakṣuṣaḥ cakṣuḥ ityādi śruti antarāt nanu agnibhiḥ uktam vitatham yata ācāryaḥ tu te gatim vaktā iti gati mātrasya vaktā iti avocan bhaviṣyat viṣaya aparijñānam ca agnīnam na eṣa doṣaḥ sukha ākāśasya eva akṣiṇi dṛśyata iti draṣṭuḥ anuvādāt  eṣa ātmā prāṇinām iti ha uvāca evam uktavān etad yad eva ātma tattvam avocāma etad amṛtam amaraṇa dharmya vināśyata eva abhayam yasya hi vināśa āśaṅkā tasya bhaya upapattiḥ tad abhāvāt abhayam ata eva etad brahma bṛhadanantam iti kiñca asya brahmaṇaḥ  akṣi puruṣasya māhātmyam tad tatra puruṣasya sthāne akṣiṇi yadi api asmini arpiḥ vā udakam vā siñcati vartmanī eva gacchati pakṣmau  eva gacchati na cakṣuṣā sambandhyate padma patreṇa iva udakam sthānasya api etad māhātmyam kim punar  sthāninaḥ  akṣi puruṣasya nirañjana tvam vaktavyam iti abhiprāyaḥ etam yathā uktam puruṣam saṃyadvāma iti ācakṣate kasmāt  yasmāt etam sarvāṇi vāmāni vananīyāni saṃbhajanīyāni śobhanāni abhisaṃyanti abhisaṅgacchanti iti atas  saṃyadvāmaḥ tathā evaṃvidam enam sarvāṇi vāmāni abhisaṃyanti ya evam veda eṣa u eva vāmanīryasmāt eṣa hi sarvāṇi vāmāni puṇya karma phalāni puṇya anurūpam prāṇibhyaḥ  nayati prāpayati vahati ca ātma dharma tvena viduṣaḥ phalam sarvāṇi vāmāni nayati ya evam veda eṣa u eva bhāmanīḥ eṣa hi yasmāt sarveṣu lokeṣu āditya candra agni ādi rūpaiḥ bhāti dīpyate tasya bhāsā sarvam idam vibhāti iti śruteḥ atas  bhāmāni nayati iti bhāmanīḥ ya evam vedāsau  api sarveṣu lokeṣu bhāti atha idānīm yathā ukta brahma vidaḥ  gatiḥ ucyate yad yadi u ca eva asmin  evaṃvidi śavyam śava karma mṛte kurvanti yadi ca na kurvanti ṛtvijaḥ sarvathā api evaṃvittena śava karmaṇā akṛtena api pratibaddhaḥ  na brahma[dmaṭa prāpnoti na ca kṛtena śava karmaṇā asya kaścana abhyadhikaḥ  lokaḥ na karmaṇā vardhate naḥ kanīyān iti śruti antarāt śava karmaṇi anādaram darśayan vidyām stauti na punar  śava karmā evaṃvidaḥ  na kartavyam iti akriyamāṇe hi śava karmaṇi karmaṇā phala ārambhe pratibandhaḥ kaścid anumīyate anyatra yata iha vidyā phala ārambha kāle śava karma syāt vā na vā iti vidyāvataḥ  apratibandhena phala ārambham darśayati ye sukha ākāśam akṣi stham saṃyadvāmaḥ  vāma nīrbhāma nīḥ iti evaṅguṇam upāsate prāṇa sahitām agni vidyām ca teṣām anyat karma bhavatu mā vā bhūt sarvathā api te arciṣam eva abhisambhavanti arciḥ abhimāninīm devatām abhisambhavanti pratipadyanta iti arthaḥ arciṣaḥ  arciḥ devatāyāḥ  aharahar abhimāninīm devatām ahna āpūryamāṇa pakṣam śukla pakṣa devatām āpūryamāṇa pakṣa ādyān ṣaṣ māsān udaṅṅuttarām diśam eti savitā tān māsān uttarāyaṇa devatām tebhyaḥ  māsebhyaḥ saṃvatsaram saṃvatsara devatām tatas  saṃvatsarāt ādi dityam ādityāt candramasam candramasaḥ  vidyutam tad tatrasthān  tān puruṣaḥ kaścid brahma lokādetyāmānavaḥ  mānavyām sṛṣṭau bhavaḥ  mānavaḥ  na mānavaḥ  amānavaḥ sa puruṣa enān brahma satya loka stham gamayati gantṛ gantavya gamayitṛtva vyapadeśebhyaḥ sat mātra brahma prāptau tad anupapatteḥ brahmā eva san brahmā api eti iti hi tatra vaktum nyāyyam sarva bheda nirāsena sat mātra pratipattim vakṣyati na ca adṛṣṭaḥ  mārgaḥ  agamanāya upatiṣṭhate sa enam aviditaḥ  na bhunakti iti śruti antarāt eṣa devapathaḥ devaiḥ arcira ādibhiḥ gamayitṛ tvena adhikṛtaiḥ upalakṣitaḥ panthā deva patha ucyate brahma gantavyam tena ca upalakṣita iti brahmapathaḥ etena pratipadyamānā gacchantaḥ  brahma imam mānavam manu sambandhinam manoḥ sṛṣṭi lakṣaṇam āvata na āvartanta āvartante asmin janana maraṇa prabandha cakra ārūḍhā ghaṭīyantravat punar  punar iti ārvataḥ tam na pratipadyante na āvartante na āvartante iti dvis uktiḥ saphalāyāḥ  vidyāyāḥ parisamāpti pradarśana arthā rahasya prakaraṇe prasaṅgāt āraṇyakatva sāmānyāt ca yajñe kṣata utpanne vyāhṛtayaḥ prāyaścitta arthā vidhātavyāḥ tad abhijñasya ca ṛtvijaḥ  brahmaṇaḥ  maunam ityata idam ārabhyate eṣa ha vā eṣa vāyuḥ yaḥ  ayam pavate ayam yajñaḥ ha vā iti prasiddha artha avadyotakau nipātau vāyu pratiṣṭhaḥ  hi yajñaḥ prasiddhaḥ śrutiṣu svāhā vātedhāḥ ayam vai yajñaḥ  yaḥ  ayam pavate ityādi śrutibhyaḥ vāta eva hi calana ātmava tvāt kriyā samavāyī vāta eva yajñasya ārambhakaḥ  vātaḥ pratiṣṭhā iti ca śravaṇāt  eṣa ha yangacchan  calan  idam sarvam jagat punāti pāvayati śodhayati na hi acalataḥ śuddhiḥ asti doṣa nirasanam calataḥ  hi dṛṣṭam na sthirasya yadi asmāt ca yad naṣa idam sarvam punāti tasmāt eṣa eva yajñaḥ  yad punāti iti tasya asya evam viśiṣṭasya yajñasya vāc ca mantra uccāraṇe vyāpṛtā manaḥ ca yathābhūta artha jñāne vyāpṛtam te ete vāc manase vartanī mārgau yābhyām yajñaḥ tāyamānaḥ pravartate te vartanī prāṇa apāna paricalanavatyā hi vācaḥ cittasya ca uttarottara kramaḥ  yadyajñaḥ iti hi śruti antaram atas  vāc manasābhyām yajñaḥ  vartata iti vāc manase vartanī ucyete yajñasya tayoḥ vartanyoḥ anyatarām vartanīm manasā viveka jñānavatā saṃskaroti brahmaṛtvij vācā vartanyā hotā adhvaryuḥ udgātā iti ete trayaḥ  api ṛtvijaḥ  anyatarām vāc lakṣaṇām vartanīm vācā eva saṃskurvanti tatra evam sati vāc manase vartanī saṃskārye yajñe atha sa brahmā yatra yasmin kāla upākṛte prārabdhe prātaranuvāke śasre purā pūrvam paridhānīyāyā ṛcaḥ  brahma etasmin  antare kāle vyavavadati maunam parityajati yadi tadā anyatarām eva vā#ac vartanīm saṃskaroti brahmaṇā asaṃskriyamāṇā manaḥ vartanī hīyate vinaśyati cchidrībhavati anyatarā sa yajñaḥ  vāc vartanyā eva anyatarayā vartitum aśaknuvanriṣyati katham iva iti āha sa yathā ekapād puruṣaḥ  brajan gacchan  adhvānam riṣyati rathaḥ  vā ekena cakreṇa vartamānaḥ  gacchanriṣyati evam asya yajamānasya kubrahmaṇā yajñaḥ  riṣyati vinaśyati yajñam riṣyantam yajamānaḥ  ariṣyati yajña prāṇaḥ  hi yajamānaḥ atas  yuktaḥ  yajñareṣe reṣaḥ tasya sa tam yajñam iṣṭvā tādṛśam pāpīyān pāpa taraḥ  bhavati atha punar yatra brahmā vidvān maunam parigṛhya vāc visargam akurvanvartate yāvat paridhānīyāyā na vyavavadati tathā eva sarva ṛtvija ubhe eva vartanī saṃskurvanti na hīyate anyatarā api kim iva iti āha pūrva ukta viparītau dṛṣṭāntau evam asya yajamānasya yajñaḥ sva vartanībhyām vartamānaḥ pratitiṣṭhati svena ātmanā avinaśyan vartata iti arthaḥ yajñam pratitiṣṭhantam yajamānaḥ  anupratitiṣṭhati sa yajamāna evam mauna vijñānavat brahma upetam yajñam iṣṭvā śreyān bhavati śreṣṭhaḥ  bhavati iti arthaḥ atra brahmaṇaḥ  maunam vihitam tad reṣe brahmatva karmaṇi ca anyasmin  ca hotrādi karmareṣe vyāhṛti homaḥ prāyaścittam iti tad artham vyāhṛtayaḥ vidhātavyā iti āha prajāpatiḥ lokān abhyata pat lokān uddiśya tatra sārajighṛkṣayā dhyāna lakṣaṇam tapaḥ cacāra teṣām tapyamānānām lokānām rasān sāra rūpān prāvṛhat uddhṛtavān jagrāha iti arthaḥ kān agnim rasam pṛthivyāḥ vāyum antarikṣāt  ādityam divaḥ punar api evam evam agni ādyāḥ sa etāḥ tisraḥ  devatā uddiśya abhyatapat tatas  api sāram rasam trayī vidyām jagrāha sa etām punar abhyatapat trayīm vidyām tasyāḥ tapyamānāyāḥ  rasam bhūḥ iti vyāhṛti mṛgbhyaḥ  jagrāha bhuvar iti vyāhṛtim yajurbhyaḥ svar iti vyāhṛtim sāmabhyaḥ ata eva loka deva veda rasā mahāvyāhṛtayāḥ atas tad tatra yajñe yad i ṛkta ṛc sambandha adṛś nimittam riṣyet yajñaḥ kṣatam prāpnuyāt bhūḥ svāhā iti gārhapatye juhuyāt  sā tatra prāyaścittiḥ katham ṝcām eva tad iti kriyā viśeṣaṇam rasena ṛcām vīryeṇa oja sarcām yajñasya ṛc sambandhinaḥ  yajñasya viriṣṭam vicchinnam kṣata rūpam utpannam sandadhāti pratisandhatte atha yadi yajuṣṭaḥ  yajuḥ nimittam riṣyet bhuvaḥ svāhā iti dakṣiṇa agnau juhuyāt  tathā sāma nimitte reṣe svar  svāhā iti āhavanīye juhuyāt  tathā pūrvavat yajñam sandadhāti brahma nimitte tu reṣe triṣu agniṣu tisṛbhiḥ vyāhṛtibhiḥ juhuyāt  trayyā hi vidyāyāḥ sa reṣaḥ atha kena brahma tvam iti anayā eva trayyā vidyayā iti śruteḥ nyāya antaram vā mṛgyam brahmatva nimitte reṣe tad yathā lavaṇena suvarṇam sandadhyāt  kṣāreṇa ṭaṅkaṇa ādinā khare  mṛdutva karam hi tad  suvarṇena rajatam aśakya sandhānam sandadhyāt  rajatena tathā trapu trapuṇā sīsam sīsena loha lohena dāru dāru carmaṇā carma bandhanena evam eṣām lokān ām āsām devatā nāmasya asrayyā vidyāyā vīryeṇa rasa ākhyena ojasā yajñasya viriṣṭam sandadhāti bheṣaja kṛtaḥ  ha vā eṣa yajñaḥ roga ārta iva pumān  cikitsakena su śikṣitena eṣa yajñaḥ  bhavati kaḥ  asau yatra yasmin yajña evaṃvid yathā ukta vyāhṛti homa prāyaścitta vid brahma ṛtvij bhavati sa yajña iti arthaḥ kiñca eṣa ha vā udak pravaṇa udak nimnaḥ  dakṣiṇa ucchrāyaḥ  yajñaḥ  bhavati uttara mārga pratipatti hetuḥ iti arthaḥ yatra evaṃvid brahmā bhavati evaṃvidam ha vai brahmāṇam ṛtvijam pratyeṣa anugāthā brahmaṇaḥ stuti parā yatas  yata āvartate karma pradeśāt ṛtvijām yajñaḥ kṣatībhavan  tad tad yajñasya kṣata rūpam pratisanda dhat prāyaścittena gacchati paripālayati iti etad  mānavaḥ  bhrahmā mauna ācaraṇāt mananāt vā jñāvanattvāt tatas  brahma eva eka ṛtvikkurūn kartṝn yoddhṝn ārūḍhān aśvā vaḍavā yathā abhirakṣati evaṃviddha vai brahmā yajñam yajamānam sarvān  ca ṛtvijaḥ  abhirakṣati tad kṛta doṣa apanayanāt yata evaṃviśiṣṭaḥ  brahmā vidvān  tasmāt evaṃvidam eva yathā ukta vyāhṛtya ādi vidam brahmāṇam kurvīta na anevaṃvidam kadācana iti dvis abhyāsaḥ  adhyāya parisamāpti arthaḥ iti śrīmat govinda bhagavat pūjya pāda śiṣya parama haṃsapar ivrājaka ācārya śrīmat śaṅkara bhagavat pāda kṛtau cchānda ugya upaniṣad vivaraṇe caturthaḥ  adhyāyaḥ atha pañcamaḥ  adhyāyaḥ sa guṇa brahma vidyāyāḥ  uttarā gatiḥ uktā atha idānīm pañcame adhyāye pañca agni vidaḥ  gṛhasthasya ūrdhvaretasām ca śraddhālūnām vidyā antara śīlinām tām eva gati manūdyā anyā dakṣiṇa diś sambandhinī kevala karmiṇām dhūma ādi lakṣaṇā punarāvṛtti rūpā tṛtīyā ca tatas  kaṣṭatarā saṃsāra gatiḥ vairāgya hetoḥ vaktavyā iti ārabhyate prāṇaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ  vāc ādibhyaḥ prāṇaḥ  vāva saṃvarga ityādi ca bahuśas  atīte granthe prāṇa grahaṇam kṛtam sa katham śreṣṭhaḥ  vāc ādiṣu sarvaiḥ saṃhatya kāritva aviśeṣe katham ca tasya upāsanam iti tasya śreṣṭhatva ādi guṇa vidhitsayā idam anantaram ārabhyate yaḥ  ha vai kaścid jyeṣṭham ca prathamam vayasā vāva jyeṣṭhaḥ ca vayasā vāc ādibhyaḥ garbha sthe hi puruṣe prāṇasya vṛttiḥ vāc ādibhyaḥ pūrvam labdha ātmikā bhavati yayā garbhaḥ  vivardhate cakṣuḥ ādi sthāna avayava niṣpattau satyām paścāt vāc ādīnām vṛtti lābha iti prāṇaḥ  jyeṣṭhaḥ  vayasā bhavati śreṣṭha tvam tu pratipādayiṣyati suhaya ityādi nidarśanena atas  prāṇa eva jyeṣṭhaḥ ca śreṣṭhaḥ ca asmin kārya karaṇa saṅghāte yaḥ  ha vai vasiṣṭham vasitṛtamama ācchādayitṛtamam vasumattamam vā yaḥ  veda sa tathā eva vasiṣṭhaḥ  ha bhavati svānām jñātīnām kaḥ tarhi vasiṣṭha iti āha vāc vāva vasiṣṭhaḥ  vāgminaḥ  hi puruṣā vasanti abhibhavanti anyān vasumattamāḥ ca atas  vāc vasiṣṭhaḥ yaḥ  ha vai pratiṣṭhām veda sa ca asmin  loke amuṣmin  ca pare pratitiṣṭhati ha kā tarhi pratiṣṭhā iti āha cakṣuḥ vāva pratiṣṭhā cakṣuṣā hi paśyan same ca durge ca pratitiṣṭhati yasmāt atas  pratiṣṭhā cakṣuḥ yaḥ  ha vai sampadam veda tasmā asmai daivāḥ ca mānuṣāḥ ca kāmāḥ sampadyante ha kā tarhi sampad iti āha śrotram vāva sampad  yasmāt śrotreṇa vedā gṛhyante tad artha vijñānam ca tatas  karmāṇi kriyante tatas  kāma sampad iti evam kāma sampad hetu tvāt śrotram vāva saṃpad  yaḥ  ha vā āyatanam veda āyatanam ha svānām bhavati āśrayaḥ  bhavati iti arthaḥ kim tadāyatanam iti āha manaḥ  ha vā āyatanam indriya upahṛtānām viṣayāṇām bhoktṛ arthānām pratyaya rūpa āmām mana āyatanam āśrayaḥ atas  manaḥ  ha vā āyatanam iti uktam atha ha prāṇā evam yathā ukta guṇāḥ santaḥ  ahaṃśreyasī aham śreyān asmi aham śreyān asmi iti etasmin prayojane vyūdire nānā viruddham codira uktavantaḥ te ha tai ha evam vivadamānā ātmanaḥ śreṣṭhatva vijñānāya prajāpatim pitaram janayitāram kañci dā itya ūcuḥ uktavantaḥ  he bhagavan kaḥ  naḥ asmākam madhye śreṣṭhaḥ  abhyadhikaḥ  guṇaiḥ iti evam pṛṣṭavantaḥ tān pitā uvāca ha yasmin vaḥ  yuṣmākam madhye utkrānte śarīram idam pāpiṣṭham iva atiśayena jīvataḥ  api samutkrānta prāṇam tatas  api pāpiṣṭhataram iva atiśayena dṛṣyate kuṇapam aspṛśyam aśuci dṛśyeta sa vaḥ  yuṣmākam śreṣṭha iti avocat kākvā tad duḥkham parijihīrṣuḥ tathā ukteṣu pitrā prāṇeṣu sā ha vāc ucca krāma utkrāntavatī sā ca utkramya saṃvatsara mātram proṣya sva vyāpārāt nivṛttā satī punar  paryetya itarān prāṇān uvāca katham kena prakāreṇa aśakata śaktavantaḥ  yūyam mad ṛte mām vinā jīvitum dhārayitum ātmānam iti te ha ūcuḥ yathākalā ityādi akalā mūkā yathā loke avadantaḥ  vācā jīvanti katham prāṇantaḥ prāṇena paśyantaḥ cakṣuṣā śṛṇvantaḥ śrotreṇa dhyāyantaḥ  manasā evam sarva karaṇa ceṣṭām kurvanta iti arthaḥ evam vayam ajīviṣmā iti arthaḥ ātmanaḥ  aśreṣṭha tām prāṇeṣu buddhvā praviveśa ha vāc punar  sva vyāpāre pravṛttā babhūva iti arthaḥ samānam anyat cakṣuḥ het cakrāma śrotram ha uccakrāma manaḥ  ha uccakrāma ityādi yathā bālā amanasaḥ  aprarūḍha manasa iti arthaḥ evam parīkṣiteṣu vāc ādiṣu atha anantaram ha sa mukhyaḥ prāṇa uccikramiṣan  utkramitum icchan kim akarot iti ucyate yathā loke suhayaḥ śobhanaḥ  aśvaḥ paḍvīśa śaṅkūn pāda bandha nakīlān parīkṣaṇāya ārūḍhena kaśyā āhataḥ san saṅkhidet samutkhanet samutpāṭayet  evam itarān vāc ādīn prāṇān samakhidat samuddhṛtavān te prāṇāḥ sañcālitāḥ santaḥ sva sthāne sthātum anutsahamānā abhisametya mukhyam prāṇam tam ūcuḥ hem bhagavat nedhi bhava naḥ svāmī yasmāt tvam naḥ asmākam śreṣṭhaḥ  asi mā ca asmāt dehāt utkramīḥ iti atha ha enam vāc ādayaḥ prāṇasya śreṣṭha tvam kāryeṇa apādayanta āhuḥ balim iva harantaḥ  rājñe viśaḥ katham vāc  tāvat uvāca yad aham vasiṣṭhaḥ  asmi yad iti kriyā viśeṣaṇam yad vasiṣṭhatva guṇa asmi iti arthaḥ tvam tad vasiṣṭhaḥ tena vasiṣṭhatva guṇa u ajñānāt mama iti mayā abhimata iti etad  tathā uttareṣu yojyam cakṣuḥ śrotra manaḥsu śruteḥ idam vacaḥ  yuktam idam vāc ādibhiḥ mukhyam prāṇam pratyabhihitam yasmāt na vai loke vācaḥ  na cakṣūṃṣi na śrotrāṇi na manāṃsi iti vāc ādīni karaṇāni ācakṣate laukikā āgama jñā vā kim tarhi prāṇā iti eva ācakṣate kathayanti yasmāt prāṇaḥ  hi eva etāni sarvāṇi vāc ādīni karaṇa jātāni bhavati atas  mukhyam prāmam pratyanurūpam eva vāc ādibhiḥ uktam iti prakaraṇa artham upasañjihīrṣati nanu katham idam yuktam cetanāvanta iva puruṣā ahaṃśreṣṭha tāyai vivadantaḥ  anyonyam spardheḥ an  iti na hi cakṣuḥ ādīnām vācam pratyākhyāya pratyekam vadanam sambhavati tathā apagamaḥ  dehāt punar  praveśaḥ  brahma gamanam prāṇa stutiḥ vā upapadyate tatra agni ādi cetanāvat devatā adhiṣṭhita tvāt vāc ādīnām cetanāvat tvam tāvat siddham āgamataḥ tārkika samaya virodha iti ced deha ekasmin  aneka cetanāvat tve na īśvarasya nimittakāramatva abhyupagamāt ye tāvat īśvaram abhyupagacchanti tārkikāḥ te mana ādi kārya karamānām ādhyātmikānām bāhyānām ca pṛthivī ādīnām īśvara adhiṣṭhitānām eva niyamena pravṛttim icchanti ratha ādivat  na ca asmābhiḥ agni ādyāḥ cetanāvatyaḥ  api devatā adhyātmam bhoktryaḥ  abhyupagamyante kim tarhi kārya karaṇavatīnām hi tāsām prāṇa eka devatā bhedānām adhyātma adhibhūta adhidaiva bheda koṭi vikalpānāmadhya kṣatā mātreṇa niyanteśvaraḥ  abhyupagamyate sa hi akaraṇaḥ hiraṇyagarbham janayāmāna pūrvam ityādi ca śveta aśva tarīyāḥ paṭhanti bhoktā karma phala sambandhī dehe tad vilakṣaṇaḥ  jīva iti vakṣyāmaḥ vāc ādīnām ca iha saṃvādaḥ kalpitaḥ  viduṣaḥ  anvaya vyatirekābhyām prāṇa śreṣṭha tā nirdhāraṇa artham yathā loke puruṣā anyonyam ātmanaḥ śreṣṭha tāyai vivadamānāḥ kañcid guṇa viśeṣa abhijñam pṛcchanti kaḥ  naḥ śreṣṭhaḥ  guṇaiḥ iti tena uktā ekaika śyena ādaḥ kāryam sādhayitum udyacchata yena ādaḥ kāryam sādhyate sa vaḥ śreṣṭha iti uktāḥ tathā eva udyacchanta ātmanaḥ  anyasya vā śreṣṭhavān nirdhārayanti tata imam saṃvyavahāram vāc ādiṣu kalpitavatī śrutiḥ katham nāma vidvān vāc ādīnām ekaikasya abhāve api jīvanam dṛṣṭam na tu prāṇasya iti prāṇa śreṣṭha tām pratipadyata iti tathā ca śrutiḥ kauṣītakinām jīvati vāc apetaḥ  mūkān hi pasyāmaḥ  jīvati cakṣuḥ apetaḥ  andhān hi paśyāmaḥ  jīvati śrotra apetaḥ  badhirān hi paśyāmaḥ  jīvati mana upetaḥ  bālān hi paśyāmaḥ  jīvati bāhu  chinnaḥ jīvati ūru  chinnaḥ ityādyā sa ha uvāca mukhyaḥ prāṇaḥ kim me annam bhaviṣyati iti mukhyam prāṇam praṣṭāram iva kalpayitvā vāc ādīn prativaktṝn iva kalpayantī śrutiḥ āha yad idam loke anna jātam prasiddhamā śvabhiḥ saha āśakunibhyaḥ saha śakunibhiḥ sarva prāṇinām yad annam tad tava annam iti ha ūcuḥ vāc ādaya iti prāṇasya sarvam annam prāṇaḥ  attā sarvasya annasya iti evam pratipattaye kalpita ākhyāyikā rūpāt vyāvṛtya svena śruti rūpeṇa āha tad vā etad yad kiñcit loke prāṇibhiḥ annamadyate anasya prāṇasya tad annam prāṇena eva tad adyata iti arthaḥ sarva prakāra ceṣṭā vyāpti guṇa pradarśana artha mana iti prāṇasya pratyakṣam nāma prādi upasarga pūrva tve hi viśeṣa gatiḥ eva syāt  tathā ca sarvān nānā mattuḥ nāma grahaṇam iti idam pratyakṣam nāmāna iti sarvān nānā mattuḥ sākṣāt abhidhānam na ha vā evaṃvidi yathā ukta prāṇa vidi prāṇaḥ  aham asmi sarva bhūta sthaḥ sarvān na anāmatta iti tasmin  evaṃvidi ha vai kiñcana kiñcid api prāṇibhiḥ ādyam sarvaiḥ anannam annādyam na bhavati sarvam evaṃvidyannam bhavati iti arthaḥ prāṇa bhūta tvāt viduṣaḥ prāṇāt vā eṣa udeti prāṇe astam eti iti upakramya evaṃvidaḥ  ha vā udeti sūrya evaṃvidyaḥ tam eti iti śruti antarāt sa ha uvāca punar  prāṇaḥ pūrvavat eva kalpanā kim me vāsaḥ  bhaviṣyati iti āpa iti ha ūcuḥ vāc ādayaḥ yasmāt prāṇasya vāsa āpaḥ tasmāt vā etad aśiṣyantaḥ  bhoktavantaḥ ca brāhmaṇā vidvāṃsa etad kurvanti kim adbhiḥ vāsa sthānīyābhiḥ purastāt bhojanāt pūrvam upariṣṭāt ca bhojanāt ūrdhvam ca paridadhati paridhānam kurvanti mukhyasya prāṇasya lambhukaḥ  sambhana śīlaḥ  vāsaḥ  ha bhavati vāsasaḥ  labdhā eva bhavati iti arthaḥ anagnaḥ ha bhavati vāsasaḥ  lambhuka tvena artha siddha eva anagnatā iti anagnaḥ ha bhavati iti uttarīyavān bhavati iti etad  bhokṣyamāṇasya bhuktavataḥ ca yad ācamanam śuddhi artham vijñātam tasmin prāṇasya vāsa iti darśana mātram iha vidhīyate adbhiḥ paridadhati iti na ācamana antaram yathā laukikaiḥ prāmibhiḥ adyamānam annam prāṇasya iti darśana mātram tadvat kim me annam kim me vāsa ityādi praśna prativacanayoḥ tulya tvāt yadi ācamanam apūrvam tādarthyena kriyate tadā kṛmi ādi annam api prāṇasya bhakṣya tvena vihitam syāt  tulyayoḥ vijñāna arthayoḥ prasna prativacanayoḥ prakaraṇasya vijñāna artha tvāt ardha jaratīyaḥ  nyāyaḥ  na yuktaḥ kalpayitum yad tu prasiddham ācamanam prāyatya artham prāṇasya anagna tā artham ca na bhavati iti ucyate na tathā vayam ācamanam ubhaya artham brūmaḥ kim tarhi prāyatya artha ācamana sādhana bhūtā āpaḥ prāṇasya vāsa iti darśanam codyata iti brūmaḥ tatra ācamanasya ubhaya arthatva prasaṅga doṣa codanā anupapannā vāsortha eva ācamane tad darśanam syāt iti ced  na vāsaḥ jñāna artha vākye vāsortha apūrva ācamana vidhāne tatra anagnatā arthatva dṛṣṭi vidhāne ca vākya bhedaḥ ācamanasya tad artha tvam anya artha tvam ca iti pramāṇa abhāvāt  tad etad prāṇa darśanam stūyate katham tad ha etad prāṇa darśanam satya kāmaḥ  jābālaḥ  gośrutaye nāmnā vaiyāghrapadyāya vyāghrapadaḥ  apatyam vaiyāghrapadyaḥ tasmai gaḥ śruti ākhyāya uktvā uvāca anyat api vakṣyamāṇam vacaḥ kim tad uvāca iti āha yadi api śuṣkāya sthāṇava etad darśanam brūyāt prāṇa vid jāyeran  utpadyeran  eva asmin sthāṇau śākhāḥ praroheyuḥ ca palāśāni patrāmi kim u jīvate puruṣāya brūyāt iti atha anantaram yadi mahat mahat tvam jigamiṣet gantum icchet mahat tvam prāptum yadikāmayeta iti arthaḥ tasya idam karma vidhīyate mahat tve hi sati śrīḥ upanamate śrīmataḥ  hi artha prāptam dhanam tatas  karma anuṣṭhānam tatas ca deva yānam pitṛyāṇam vā panthānam pratipatsyata iti etad prayojana murarīkṛtya mahattva prepsoḥ idam karma na viṣaya upabhoga kāmasya tasya ayam kāla ādi vidhiḥ ucyate amāvāsyāyām dīkṣitvā dīkṣita iva bhūmi śayana ādi niyamam kṛtvā tapaḥ rūpam satya vacanam brahmacaryam ityādi dharmavān bhūtvā iti arthaḥ na punar daikṣam eva karma jātam sarvam upādatte atad vikāra tvāt mantha ākhyasya karmaṇaḥ upasadvratī iti śruti antarāt payaḥ mātra bha kṣamam ca śuddhikāramam tapa upādatte paurṇamāsyām rātrau karma ārabhate sarva auṣadhasya grāmya āraṇyānām oṣadhīnām yāvat śakti alpam alpam upādāya tad vituṣīkṛtyāmam eva piṣṭam dadhi madhunā uraudumbare kaṃsa ākāre camasa ākāre vā pātre śruti antarāt prakṣipya upamathya agratas  sthāpayitvā jyeṣṭhāya śreṣṭhāya svāhā iti agnau  āvasathya ājyasya āvāpa sthāne hutvā sruva saṃlagnam manthe saṃpātam avanayet saṃsravam adhas  pātayet  samānam anyat  vasiṣṭhāya pratiṣṭhāyai saṃpada āyatanāya svāhā iti pratyekam tathā eva saṃpātam avanayet hutvā atha pratisṛpya agneḥ īṣat apasṛpya añjalau mantham ādhāya japati imam mantram amaḥ  nāma āsyamā hi te ama iti prāṇasya nāma annena hi prāṇaḥ prāṇiti deha iti atas  mantha dravyam prāṇasya anna tvāt prāṇa tvena stūyate amaḥ  nāma asi iti kutas  yatas  amā saha hi yasmāt te tava prāṇa bhūtasya sarvam samastam jagat idamatas  sa hi prāṇa bhūtaḥ  manthaḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ śreṣṭhaḥ ca ata eva ca rājā dīptimān adhipatiḥ ca adhiṣṭhāya pālayitā sarvasya samā mām api manthaḥ prāṇaḥ  jyaiṣṭhī ādi guṇa pūgam ātmanaḥ  gamayatu aham eva idam sarvam jagadasāni bhavani prāṇavat  iti śabdaḥ  mantra parisamāpti arthaḥ atha anantaram khalu etayā vakṣyamāṇayarcā pacchas  pādaśa ācāmati bhakṣayati mantrasya ekaikena pādena ekaikam grāsam bhakṣayati tad bhojanam savituḥ sarvasya prasavituḥ prāṇam ādityam ca ekīkṛtya ucyate ādityasya vṛṇīmahe prārthayemahi mantha rūpam yena annena sāvitreṇa bhojanena upabhuktena vayam savitṛ svarūpa āpannā bhavema iti abhiprāyaḥ devasya savituḥ iti pūrveṇa sambandhaḥ śreṣṭham praśasyatamam sarva annebhyaḥ sarva dhātamam sarvasya jagataḥ  dhārayitṛtamam atiśayena vidhātṛtamam iti vā sarvathā bhojana viśeṣaṇam turam tvaram tūrṇam śīghram iti atat bhagasya devasya savituḥ svarūpam iti śeṣaḥ dhīmahi cintayemahi viśiṣṭa bhojanena saṃskṛtāḥ śuddha ātmānaḥ santa iti abhiprāyaḥ athavā bhagasya śriyaḥ kāraṇam mahat tvam prāptum karma kṛtavantaḥ  vayam tad homahi cintayemahi iti sarvam ca mantha lepam pibati nirṇijya prakṣālya kaṃsam kaṃsa ākāram camasam camasa ākāram vaudumbaram pātram pītvā ācamya paścāt agneḥ prāc śirāḥ saṃviśati carmaṇi vājine sthaṇḍile kevalāyām vā bhūmau vācaṃyamaḥ  vāgyataḥ san  iti arthaḥ aprasāhaḥ  na prasahyate na abhibhūyate strī ādi aniṣṭa svapna darśanena yathā tathā saṃyata cittaḥ san  iti arthaḥ sa evaṃbhūtaḥ  yadi sriyam paśyet svapneṣu tadā vidyāt samṛddham mama idam karma iti tad etasmin  artha eṣa ślokaḥ  mantraḥ  api bhavati yadā karmasu kāmyeṣu kāma artheṣu sriyam svapneṣu svapna darśaneṣu svapna kāleṣu vā paśyati samṛddhim tatra jānīyīt  karmaṇām phala niṣpattiḥ bhaviṣyati iti jānīyāt iti arthaḥ tasmin strī ādi praśasta svapna darśane satī iti abhiprāyaḥ dvis uktiḥ karma samāpti arthā brahma ādi stamba paryantāḥ saṃsāra gatayaḥ vaktavyā vairāgya hetoḥ mumukṣūṇām ityata ākhyāyikā ārabhyate śvetaketuna mitas  ha iti aitihya arthaḥ aruṇasya apatya aruṇiḥ tasya apatyam āruṇeyaḥ pañcālānām samitim sabhāmeyāya ājagāma tam āgatavantam ha pravāhaṇaḥ  nāmataḥ  jīvalasya apatyam jaivaliḥ uvāca uktavān he kumāra anu tvā tvām aśiṣa dan vasiṣat pitā kim anuśiṣṭaḥ tvam pitrā iti arthaḥ iti uktaḥ sa āha anu hi anuśiṣṭaḥ  asmi bhagava iti sūcayan  āha tam ha uvāca yadi anuśiṣṭaḥ  asi vettha yad itas  asmāt lokāt adhi ūrdhvam yad prajāḥ prayanti yad gacchanti tad kim jānīṣa iti arthaḥ na bhagava iti āha itaraḥ  na jāne aham tad yad pṛcchasi evam tarhi vettha jānīṣe yathā yena prakāreṇa punar āvartanta iti na bhagava iti pratyāha vettha pathoḥ mārgayoḥ saha prayāṇayoḥ deva yānasya pitṛyāṇasya ca vyāvartanam itaretara viyoga sthānam saha gacchatām iti arthaḥ na bhagava iti vetthā yathā asau lokaḥ pitṛ sambandhī yam prāpya punar āvartante bahubhiḥ prayadbhiḥ api yena kāramena na sampūryata iti na bhagava iti pratyāha vettha yathā yena krameṇa pañcamyām pañca saṃkhyā kāyām āhutau hutāyām āhuti nirvṛttā āhuti sādhanāḥ ca apaḥ puruṣa vacasaḥ puruṣa iti evam vacaḥ  abhidhānam yāsām hūyamānānām krameṇa ṣaṣṭha āhuti bhūtānām tāḥ puruṣa vacasaḥ puruṣa śabda vācyā bhavanti puruṣa ākhyām labhanta iti arthaḥ iti uktaḥ  na eva bhagava iti āha na eva aham atra kiñcana jānāmi iti arthaḥ atha evam ajñaḥ sankimanu kasmāt tvam anuśiṣṭaḥ  asmi iti avocathā uktavān asi yaḥ  hi imāni mayā pṛṣṭāni artha jātāni na vidyāt na vijānītyāt katham sa vidvatsu anuśiṣṭaḥ  asmi iti bruvīta iti evam sa śvetaketuḥ rājñā āyasta āyāsitaḥ sanpituḥ ardham sthāna meyāya āgatavān  tam ca pituḥ am uvāca ananuśiṣya anuśāsanam akṛtvā eva mā mām kila bhagavān samāvartana kāle abravīt uktavān anu tu āśiṣam anvaśiṣam tvām iti yatas  pañca pañca saṃkhyākān praśnān rājanya bandhū rājā anyā bandhavaḥ  asya iti rājanya bandhuḥ svayam durvṛtta iti arthaḥ aprākṣīt pṛṣṭavān  teṣām praśnānām na ekañcana ekam api nāśakam na śaktavān aham vivaktum viśeṣeṇa arthataḥ  nirṇetum iti arthaḥ sa ha uvāca pitā yathā mā mām vatsa tvam tad āgata mātra eva etān praśnān avada uktavān asi teṣām na ekañca nāśakam vivaktum iti tathā mām jānīhi tvadīyā jñānena liṅgena mama tad viṣayam ajñānam jānīhi iti arthaḥ katham yathā aham eṣām praśnānām ekañcana ekam api na veda na jāna iti yathā tvam eva aṅga etān praśnān na jānīṣe tathā aham api etān na jāna iti arthaḥ atas  mayi anyathā bhāva u na kartavyaḥ kuta etad evam yatas  na jāne yadi aham imān praśnāna vediṣyam viditavān asmi katham te tubhyam priyāya putrāya samāvartana kāle purā na avakṣyam na uktavān asmi iti uktvā sa ha gotrataḥ  rājñaḥ  jaivaleḥ ardham sthāna meyāya gatavān tasmai ha gautamāya prāptāya arhām arhūṇām cakāra kṛtavān sa ca gautamaḥ kṛta ātithya uṣitvā paredyus  prātaḥkāle sa bhāge sabhām gate rājñi udeyāya bhajanam bhāgaḥ pūjā sevā saha bhāgena vartamānaḥ  vā sa bhāgaḥ pūjyamānaḥ  anyaiḥ svayam gautama udeyāya rājānam udgatavān tam ha uvāca gautamam rājā mānuṣasya bhagavan gautama manuṣya sambandhinaḥ
