yad pūrvam iha loke bhavanti vabhūvuḥ iti arthaḥ tad eva punar āgatya bhavanti yuga sahasra koṭi antaritā api saṃsāriṇaḥ  jantoḥ yā purā bhāvitā vāsanā sā na naśyati iti arthaḥ yathāprajñam hi saṃbhavāḥ iti śrutti antarāt tāḥ prajā yasmin praviśya punar āvirbhavanti ye tvitas  anye sat sati ātma abhisaṃdhā yamaṇu bhāvam sadā ātmānam praviśya na āvartante sa ya eṣaḥ  aṇima ityādi vyākhyātam yathā loke svakīye gṛhe supta utthāya grāma antaram gataḥ  jānāti sva gṛhāt āgataḥ  asmi iti evam sata āgataḥ  asmi iti ca jantūnām kasmāt vijñānam na bhavati iti bhūya eva mā bhagavān vijñāpayatu iti uktaḥ tathā sobhyā iti ha uvāca pitā śṛṇu tatra dṛṣṭāntam yathā somya imā nadyaḥ  gaṅgā ādyāḥ purastāt pūrvām diśam prati prācyaḥ prāgañcanāḥ syandante sravanti paścāt pratīcīm diśam prati sindhva ādyāḥ pratīcīm añcanti gacchanti iti pratīcyaḥ tāḥ samudrāt ambhaḥ nidheḥ jala dharaiḥ ākṣiptāḥ punar vṛṣṭi rūpeṇa patitā gaṅgā ādi nadī rūpiṇyaḥ punar  samudram ambhonidhim eva apiyanti sa samudra eva bhavati tā nadyaḥ  yathā tatra samudre samudra ātmanā ekatām gatā na viduḥ na jānantīyam gaṅgā aham asmi iyam yamunā aham asmi itīyam mahyaham asmi iti ca evam eva khalu somya imāḥ sarvāḥ prajā yasmāt sati sampadya na viduḥ tasmāt sata āgamya na viduḥ sata āgacchāmaha āgatā iti vā ta iha vyāghra ityādi samānam anyat  dṛṣṭam loke jale vīcī taraṅga phena buda ādaya utthitāḥ punar tad bhāvam gatā vinaṣṭā iti jīvāḥ tu tad kāraṇam aṇu bhāvam pratyaham gacchantaḥ  api suṣupte maraṇa pralayayoḥ ca na vinaśyanti iti etad  bhūya eva mā bhagavān vijñāpayatu dṛṣṭāntena tathā somya iti ha uvāca pitā śṛṇu dṛṣṭāntam asya he somya mahataḥ  aneka śākhā ādi yuktasya vṛkṣasya asya iti agratas  sthitam vṛkṣam darśayan  āha yadi yaḥ kaścid asya mūle abhyāhanyāt paraśu ādinā sakṛt ghāta mātreṇa na śuṣyati iti jīvan  eva bhavati tadā tasya rasaḥ sravet  tathā yaḥ  madhye abhyāhanyāt jīvan sravet tathā yaḥ  agre abhyāhanyāt jīvan sravet sa eṣa vṛkṣa idānīm jīvena ātmanā anuprabhūtaḥ  anuvyāptaḥ pepīyamānaḥ  atyartham piban  udakam bhaumān  ca rasān mūlaiḥ gṛhṇan modamānaḥ  harṣam prāpnuvan  tiṣṭhati tasya asya yad ekām śākhām roga grastām āhatām vā jīvaḥ  jahā ati upasaṃharati śākhāyām viprasṛtam ātma aṃśam atha sā śuṣyati vāc manaḥ prāṇa karaṇa grāma anupraviṣṭaḥ  hi jīva iti tad upasaṃhāra upasaṃhriyate jīvena ca prāṇa yuktena aśitam potam ca rasa tām gatam jīvat śarīram vṛkṣam vardhayat rasa rūpeṇa jīvasya sadbhāve liṅgam bhavati aśita pītābhyām hi dehe jīvaḥ tiṣṭhati te cāśita pīte jīva karma anusāriṇī iti tasya eka aṅga vaikalya nimittam karma yadā upasthitam bhavati tadā jīva ekām śākhām jahāti śākhāyāḥ  ātmānam upasaṃharati atha tadā sā śākhā śuṣyati jīva sthiti nimittaḥ  rasaḥ  jīva karma ākṣiptaḥ  jīva upasaṃhāre na tiṣṭhati rasa apagame ca śākhā śoṣam upaiti tathā sarvam vṛkṣam eva yadā ayam jahāti tadā sarvaḥ  api vṛkṣaḥ śuṣyati vṛkṣasya rasa sravaṇa śoṣaṇa ādi liṅgāt jīvavat tvam dṛṣṭānta śruteḥ ca cetanāvantaḥ sthāvarā iti bauddha kāṇa ādamatam acetanāḥ sthāvarā iti etad asāram iti darśitam bhavati yathā asmin vṛkṣa dṛṣṭānte darśitam jīvena yuktaḥ  vṛkṣaḥ  aśuṣkaḥ  rasa pāna ādi yuktaḥ  jāvatī iti ucyate tad apetaḥ ca mriyata iti ucyate evam eva khalu somya viddhi iti ha uvāca jīva apetam jīva viyuktam vāva kila idam śarīram mriyate na jīvaḥ  mriyata iti kārya śeṣe ca supta utthitasya mama idam kārya śeṣam aparisamāptam iti smṛtvā samāpana darśanāt  jāta mātrāṇām ca jantūnām stanya abhilāṣaya ādi darśanāt ca atīta janma antara anubhūta stana  nya  pāna duḥkha anubhava smṛtiḥ gamyate agnihotra ādīnām ca vaidikānām karmaṇām arthavat tvāt na jīvaḥ  mriyata iti sa ya eṣaḥ  aṇima ityādi samānam katham punar idam atyanta sthīlam pṛthivī ādi nāma rūpavat jagat ati anta sūkṣmāt sat rūpāt nāma rūpa rah itāt sataḥ jāyata iti etad dṛṣṭāntena bhūya eva mā bhagavān vijñāpayatu iti tathā somya iti ha uvāca pitā yadi etad pratyakṣīkartum icchasi atas  asmān mahataḥ  nyagrodhāt phalam ekam āharā iti uktaḥ tathā cakāra sa idam bhagava upahṛtam phalam iti darśitavantam pratyāha phalam bhindhi iti bhinnam iti āha itaraḥ tam āha pitā kim atra paśyasi iti ukta āha aṇvyaḥ  aṇutarā iva imā dhānā bījāni paśyāmi bhagava iti āsām dhānānām ekām dhānām aṅga he vatsa bhindhī iti ukta āha bhinnā bhagava iti yadi bhinnā dhānā tasyām bhinnāyām kim paśyasi iti ukta āha na kiñcana paśyāmi bhagava iti tam putram ha uvāca vaṭa dhānāyām bhinnāyām yam vaṭa bījāṇi mānam he saumya etam na nibhālayase na paśyasi tathā api etasya vai kila somya eṣa mahān nyagrodhaḥ  bījasya aṇimnaḥ sūkṣmasya adṛśyamānasya kārya bhūtaḥ sthūla śākhā skandha phala palāśavān  tiṣṭhati utpannaḥ san  uttiṣṭhati iti vā ucchabdaḥ  adhyāhāryaḥ  atas  śraddhatsva somya sata eva aṇimnaḥ sthūlam nāma rūpa ādimat kāryam jagat utpannam iti yadi api nyāya āgamābhyām nirdhāritor athaḥ tathā eva iti avagamyate tathā api atyanta sūkṣmeṣu artheṣu bāhya viṣaya āsakta manasaḥ svabhāva pravṛttasya asatyām gurutarāyām śraddhāyām duravagam atvam syāt iti āha śraddhatsva iti śraddhāyām tu satyām manasaḥ samādhānam bubhutsiter athe bhavet tatas ca tad artha avagatiḥ anyatramanā abhūvam ityādi śruteḥ sa ya ityādi ukta artham yadi tad sajjagataḥ  mūlam kasmāt na upalabhyata iti etad dṛṣṭāntena mā bhagavān bhūya eva vijñāpayatu iti tathā somya iti ha uvāca pitā vidyamānam api vastu na upalabhyate prakāra antareṇa tu upalabhyata iti śṛṇu atra dṛṣṭāntam yadi ca imam artham pratyakṣaḥ  sa ha pitrā uktam artham pratyakṣīkartum icchan  tathā cakāra tam ha uvāca paredyus  prātarūpasīdathā upagacchethā iti sa ha pitrā uktam artham pratyakṣīkartum icchan  tathā cakāra tam ha uvāca paredyus  prātar yad lavam doṣā rātrau  udake avādhā nikṣiptavān asi aṅga he vatsa tadāharā iti uktaḥ tad lavaṇam ājihīrṣuḥ ha kila avamṛśya udake na viveda na vijñātavān yathā tad lavaṇam vidyamānam eva sat apsu līnam saṃśliṣṭam abhūtam yathā vilīnam lavaṇam na vettha tathā api tad cakṣuṣā sparśanena ca piṇḍa rūpam lavaṇam agṛhyamāṇam vidyata eva apsūpalabhyate ca upāya antareṇa iti etad putram pratyāyayitum icchan  āha aṅgāsya udakasya antāt upari gṛhītvā ācāma iti uktvā putram tathā akṛtavantam uvāca katham iti itara āha lavaṇam svādutaḥ iti tathā madhyāt udakasya gṛhītvā ācāma iti katham iti lavaṇam iti tathā antādadhas deśāt gṛhītvā ācāma iti katham iti lavaṇam iti yadi evam abhiprāsya parityajya etad udakam ācamya atha mā upasīt athā iti tad ha tathā cakāra lavaṇam parityajya pitṛ samīpam ājagāma iti arthaḥ idam vacanam bravan  tallavamam tasmin  eva udake yad mayā rātrau kṣiptam śāśvat nityam saṃvartate vidyamānam eva sat samyak vartate iti evam uktavantam tam ha uvāca pitā yathā idam lavaṇam darśana sparśanābhyām pūrvam gṛhītam punar udake vilīnam tābhyām agṛhyamāṇam api vidyata eva upāya antareṇa jihvayā upalabhyamāna tvāt  evam eva atra eva asmin  eva tejaḥ bannādi kārye śuṅgedehe vāva kila iti ācārya upadeśa smaraṇa pradarśana arthau sat tejaḥ banna ādi śuṅgakāramam vaṭa bījāṇim avat vidyamānam eva indriyaiḥ na upalabhase na nibhālayase yathā atraiva udake darśana sparśanābhyām anupalabhyamānam lavaṇam vidyamānam eva jihvayā upalabdhavān asi evam eva atra eva kila vidyamānam sat jagat mūlam upāya antareṇa lavaṇāṇimavat upalapsyasa iti vākya śeṣaḥ sa ya ityādi samānam yadi evam lavaṇāṇimavat indriyaiḥ anupalabhyamānam api jagat mūlam sat upāya antareṇa upalabdhum śakyate yad upalambhāt kṛtārthaḥ syām anupalambhāt ca akṛtārthaḥ syām aham tasya eva upalabdhau ka upāya iti etad bhūya eva mā bhagavān vijñāpayatu dṛṣṭāntena tathā somya iti ha uvāca yathā loke he somya puruṣam yam kañcid gandhārebhyaḥ  janapadebhyaḥ  abhinaddha akṣam baddha cakṣuṣam ānīya dravya hartā taskaraḥ tam abhinaddha akṣam eva baddha hastam araṇye tatas  api atijane atigata jane atyanta vigata jane deśe visṛjet sa tatra diś bhrama upetaḥ  yathā prāṅvā prāgañcanaḥ prāṅmukhaḥ  vā iti arthaḥ tathā udaṅva adharāṅvā pratyaṅvā pradhmāyīta śabdam kuryāt vikrośet  abhinaddha akṣaḥ  aham gandhārebhyaḥ taskareṇa ānītaḥ  abhinaddha akṣa eva visṛṣṭa iti evam vikrośataḥ tasya yathā abhinahanam yathābandhanam pramucya muktvā kāruṇikaḥ kaścid etām diśam uttaratas  gandhārā etām diśam vraja iti prabrūyāt sa evam kāruṇikena bandhanāt mokṣitaḥ  grāmāt grāma antaram pṛcchan paṇḍita upadeśavān medhāvaḥ  para upadiṣṭa grāma praveśa mārga avadhāraṇa samarthaḥ san gandhārān eva upasampadyeta na itaraḥ  mūḍha matiḥ deśa antara darśana tṛṣ vā yathā ayam dṛṣṭāntaḥ  varṇitaḥ sva viṣayebhyaḥ  gandhārebhyaḥ puruṣaḥ taskaraiḥ abhinaddha akṣaḥ  avivekaḥ  diś mūḍhaḥ  aśanāyā pipāsā ādimān vyāghra taskara ādi aneka bhaya anatharvrāta yutam araṇyam praveśitaḥ  duḥkha ārtaḥ  vikrośan bandhanebhyaḥ  mumukṣuḥ tiṣṭhati sa kathañcid eva kāruṇikena kenacid mokṣitaḥ sva deśān gandhārān eva āpannaḥ  nirvṛtaḥ sukhī abhūt evam eva sataḥ  jagadātmanaḥ svarūpāt tejaḥ vannādi mayam deha araṇyam vāta pitta kapha rudhira medaḥ māṃsa asthi majjā śukra kṛmi mūtra purīṣavat śīta uṣṇa ādi aneka dvandva sukha duḥkhavat ca idam moha paṭa abhinaddha akṣaḥ  bhāryā putra mitra paśu bandhva ādi dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa aneka viṣaya tṛṣṇā pāśitaḥ puṇya apuṇya ādi taskaraiḥ praveśitaḥ  aham amuṣya putraḥ  mama ete bāndhavāḥ sukhī aham duḥkhī mūḍhaḥ paṇḍitaḥ  dhārmikaḥ  bandhumāñjātaḥ  mṛtaḥ  jīrṇaḥ pāpī putraḥ  me mṛtaḥ  dhanam me naṣṭam hā hataḥ  asmi katham jāviṣyāmi kā me gatiḥ kim me trāṇam iti evam aneka śata sahasra anartha jālavān vikrośan kathañcid eva puṇya atiśayāt parama kāruṇikam kañcid sat brahma ātma vidam vimukta bandhanam brahmiṣṭham yad ā āsādayati tena ca brahma vidā kāruṇyāt darśita saṃsāra viṣaya doṣa darśana mārgaḥ  viraktaḥ saṃsāra viṣayebhyaḥ  na asi tvam saṃsāri amuṣya putratva ādi dharmavān kim tarhi sat yad tattvam asi iti avidyā moha paṭa abhinahanāt mokṣitaḥ  gandhāra puruṣavat ca svam sadā ātmānam upasampadya sukhī nirvṛtaḥ syāt iti etam eva artham āhācāryavān puruṣaḥ  veda iti tasya asya evam ācāryavataḥ  muktā vidyā abhinahanasya tāvat eva tāvān eva kālaḥ ciram kṣepaḥ sat ā ātma svarūpa sampatteḥ iti vākya śeṣaḥ kiyān kālaḥ ciram iti ucyate yāvat na vimokṣye na vimokṣyata iti etad puruṣa vyatyanena sāmarthyāt  yena karmaṇā śarīram ārabdham tasya upabhogena yena atha śabda ānantarya arthaḥ syāt  nanu yathā sat vijñāna antaram eva dehapātaḥ sat sampattiḥ ca na bhavati karma śeṣa vaśāt tathā pravṛtta phalāni prāk jñāna utpatteḥ janma antara sañcitāni api karmāṇi santi iti tad phala upabhoga artham patite asmin śarīra antaram ārabdhavyam utpanne ca jñāne yāvat jīvam vihitāni pratiṣiddhāni vā karmāṇi karoti eva iti tad phala upabhoga artham ca avaśyam śarīra antaram ārabdhavyam tatas ca karmāṇi tatas  śarīra antaram iti jñāna arthakyam karmaṇām phalavat tvāt  atha jñānavataḥ kṣīyante karmāṇi tadā jñāna prāpti sama kālam eva jñānasya sat sampatti hetutvāt mokṣaḥ syāt iti śarīra pātaḥ syāt  tathā ca ācārya abhāva iti ācāryavān puruṣaḥ  vede tyācāryavattva anupapattiḥ jñānān mokṣa abhāva prasaṅgaḥ ca deśa antara prāpti upāya jñānavat ana ekāntika phala tvam vā jñānasya na karmaṇām pravṛtta apravṛtta phalavattva viśeṣa upapatteḥ yad uktam apravṛtta phalānām karma mām dhruva phalavat tvāt brahma vidaḥ śarīre patite śarīra antaram ārabdha vyama pravṛtta karma phala upabhoga atharmiti etad asat  viduṣa stasya tāvat eva ciram iti śruteḥ prāmāṇyāt  nanu puṇyaḥ  vai pumyena karmaṇā abhavati ityādi śruteḥ api prāmāṇyam eva tasyam evam tathā api pravṛtta phalānām apravṛtta phalānām ca karmaṇām viśeṣaḥ  asti katham yāni pravṛtta phalāni karmāṇi yaiḥ vidvat śarīram ārabdham teṣām upabhogena eva kṣayaḥ yathā rahdha vegasya lakṣya mukteṣu ādeḥ vega kṣayāt eva sthitiḥ na tu lakṣya vedha sama kālam eva prayojanam na asti iti tadvat  anyāni tu apravṛtta phalāni iha prāk jñāna utpatteḥ ūrdhvam ca kṛtāni vā kriyamāṇāni vā atīta janma antara kṛtāni vā apravṛtta phalāni jñānena dahyante prāyaścittena iva kṣīyante ca asya karmāṇi iti ca ātharvaṇe atas  brahma vidaḥ  jīvana ādi prayojana abhāve api pravṛtta phalānām karmaṇām avaśyam eva phala upabhogaḥ syāt iti mukta iṣuvat tasya tāvat eva ciram iti yuktam eva uktam iti yathā ukta doṣa codana anupapattiḥ jñāna utpatteḥ ūrdhvam ca brahma vidaḥ karma abhāvam avocāma brahma saṃsthaḥ  amṛta tvam etī tyatra tad ca smartum arhasi sa ya ityādi ukta artham ācāryavān vidvān yena krameṇa sat sampadyate tam kramam dṛṣṭāntena bhūya eva mā bhagavān vijñāpayatu iti tathā somya iti ha uvāca puruṣam he somya uta upatāpinam jvara ādi upatāpavantam jñātayaḥ bāndhavāḥ parivārya upāsate mumūrṣum jānāsi mām tava pitaram putram bhrātaram vā iti pṛcchantaḥ tasya mumūrṣoḥ yāvat na vāc manasi sampadyate manaḥ prāṇe prāṇaḥ tejasi tejaḥ parasyām devatāyām iti etad uktartham saṃsāriṇaḥ  yaḥ  maraṇa kramaḥ sa eva ayam viduṣaḥ  api sat sampatti krama iti etad āha parasyām devatāyām tejasi sampanne atha na jānāti avidvān  tu sata utthāya prāc bhāvitam vyāghra ādi bhāvam deva manuṣya ādi bhāvam vā viśati vidvān  tu śāsra ācārya upadeśa janita jñāna dīpa prakāśitam sat brahma ātmānam praviśya na avartata iti eṣa sat sampatti kramaḥ anye tu mūrdhanyayā nāḍyā utkramyāt ityādi dvāreṇa sat gacchanti iti āhuḥ tad asat deśa kāla nimitta phala abhisandhānena gamana darśanāt  na hi sat ātma ekatva darśinaḥ satya abhisandhasya deśa kāla nimitta phala ādi anṛta abhisandhiḥ upapadyate virodhāt  avidyā kāma karmaṇām ca gamana nimittānām sat vijñāna hutāśana vipluṣṭa tvāt gamana anupapattiḥ eva paryāpta kāmasya kṛtātmanaḥ tivahā eva sarve pravilīyanti kāmāḥ iti ādi ātharvaṇe nadī samudra dṛṣṭānta śruteḥ ca sa ya ityādi samānam yadi mariṣyataḥ  mumukṣataḥ ca tulyā sat sampattiḥ tatra vidvān sat sampannaḥ  na avartata āvartate tu avidvān iti atra kāraṇam dṛṣṭāntena bhūya eva mā bhagavān vijñāpayatu iti tathā somya iti ha uvāca śṛṇu yathā somya puruṣam caurya karmaṇi sandihyamānam nigrahāya parīkṣaṇāya votā api hasta gṛhītam baddha hastam ānayanti rāja puruṣāḥ kim kṛtavān ayam iti pṛṣṭāḥ ca āhuḥ apahārśīt dhanam asya ayam te ca āhuḥ kim apaharaṇa mātrema bandhanam arhati anyathā datte api dhane bandhana prasaṅgāt iti uktāḥ punar āhuḥ steyam akārṣīt tauryeṇa dhanam apahā ārṣīt iti teṣu evam vadatsu itaraḥ  apahnate na aham tad kartā iti  te ca āhuḥ sandihyamānam steyam akārṣīḥ tvam asya dhanasya iti  tasmin  ca apahnavāne āhuḥ paraśum asmai tapata iti śodhayatva ātmānam iti sa yadi tasya stainyasya kartā bavati bahis ca apahnate sa evaṃbhūtaḥ tata eva anṛtam anyathābhūtam santam anyathāmānam kurute sa tathā anṛta abhisandhaḥ anṛtena ātmānam antardhāya vyavahitam kṛtvā paraśum taptam mohāt pratigṛhrāti sa dahyate atha hanyate rāja puruṣaiḥ sva kṛtena anṛta abhisandhi doṣeṇa atha yadi tasya karmaṇaḥ  akartā bhavati tatas  eva satyam ātmānam kurute sa satyena tayā stainya ākartṛ tayā ātmānam antardhāya paraśum taptam pratigṛhṇāti sa satya abhisandhaḥ sanna dahyate satya vyavadhānāt atha mucyate ca mṛṣā abhiyoktṛbhyaḥ tapta paraśu hasta tala saṃyogasya tulya tve api steya kartra kartroḥ anṛta abhisandhaḥ dahyate na tu satya abhisandhaḥ sa yathā satya abhisandhaḥ tapta paraśu grahaṇa karmaṇi satya vyavahita hasta tala tvāt na ādāhyeta na dahyeta iti etad evam sat brahma satya abhisandhītarayoḥ śarīra pāta kāle ca tulyāyām sat sampattau vidvān sat sampadya na punar vyāghra deva ādi deha grahaṇāya āvartate avidvān  tu vikāra anṛta abhisandhaḥ punar vyāghra ādi bhāvam devatā ādi bhāvam vā yathākarma yathāśrutam pratipadyate yad ātma abhisandhi anabhisandhi kṛte mokṣa bandhane yad ca mūlam jagataḥ  yad āyatanā yad pratiṣṭhāḥ ca sarvāḥ prajā yad ātmakam ca sarvam yad ca ājam amṛtam abhayam śivam advitīyam tad satyam sa ātmā tava atas tad tvam asi he śvetaketaḥ iti ukta artham asakṛt vākyam kaḥ punar asau śvetaketuḥ tvaṃśabda arthaḥ yaḥ  aham śvetaketuḥ uddālakasya putra iti veda ātmānam ādeśam śrutvā matvā vijñāya ca aśrutam amatamavijñātam vijñātum pitaram papraccha katham nu bhagavaḥ sa ādeśaḥ  bavati iti sa eṣaḥ  adhikṛtaḥ śrotā mantā vijñātā tejaḥ banna mayam kārya kāraṇa saṅghātam praviṣṭā para eva devatā nāma svarūpa vyākaraṇāya ādarśa iva puruṣaḥ sūryāduḥ iva jala ādau pratibodhitaḥ tattvam asīti dṛṣṭāntaiḥ hetubhiḥ ca tad pituḥ asya ha kila uktam sa deva aham asmi iti vijajñau vijñātavān dvis vacanam adhyāya parisamāpti artham kim punar atra ṣaṣṭhe vākya pramāṇena janitam phalam ātmani kartṛtva bhoktṛ tvayoḥ adhi kṛtatva vijñāna nivṛttiḥ tasya phalam yam vayam avocāma tvaṃśabda vācyam artham śrotum mantum ca adhikṛtam avijñāta vijñāna phala artham prāk ca etasmāt vijñānāt aham evam kariṣyāmi agnihotra ādīni karmāṇi aham atra adhikṛtaḥ eṣām ca karmaṇām phalam iha amutra ca bhokṣye kṛteṣu vā karmasu kṛta kartavyaḥ syām iti evam kartṛtva bhoktṛ tvayoḥ adhikṛtaḥ  asmi iti ātmani yad vijñānam abhūt tad tasya yad sajjagataḥ  mūlam ekam eva advitīyam tattvam asi iti anena vākyena pratibuddhasya nivartate virodhāt  na hi ekasmin  advitīya ātmani ayam aham asmi iti vijñāte mama idam anyat anena kartavyam idam kṛtvā asya phalam bhokṣya iti vā bheda vijñānam upapadyate tasmāt sat satya advitīya ātma vijñāne vikāra anṛta jīva ātma vijñānam nivartata iti yuktam nanu tad tvam asīti atra tvaṃśabda vācyer athe sat buddhiḥ ādhitsyate yathā āditya mana ādiṣu brahma ādi buddhiḥ yathā ca loke pratimā ādiṣu viṣṇu ādi buddhiḥ tadvat natu sat eva tvam iti yadi sat eva śvetaketuḥ syāt katham ātmānam na vijānīyāt yena tasmai tad tvam asi iti upadiśyate na āditya ādi vākya vailakṣaṇyāt  ādityaḥ  brahma ityādau  iti śabda vyavadhānāt na sākṣāt brahma tvam gamyate rūpa ādimat tvāt ca āditya ādīnām ākāśa manasoḥ ca iti śabda vyavadhānāt eva abrahma tvam iha tu sata eva iha praveśam darśayitvā tad tvam asi iti niraṅkuśam sat ātma bhāvam upadiśati nanu parākrama ādi guṇaḥ siṃhaḥ  asi tvam itivat tattvam asi iti syāt  na mṛd ādivat sat ekam eva advitīyam satyam iti upadeśāt na ca upacāra vijñānāt tasya tāvat eva ciram iti sat sampatti rūpa diśi eta mṛṣā tvāt upacāra vijñānasya tvam indraḥ  asi yama itivat  na api stutiḥ anupāsya tvāt śvetaketoḥ na api sat śvetaketutva upadeśena stūyeta na hi rājā dāsaḥ tvam iti stutyaḥ syāt  na api sataḥ sarva ātmana eka deśa nirodhaḥ  yuktaḥ tattvam asi iti deśa adhipateḥ iva grāma adhyakṣaḥ tvam iti na ca anyā gatiḥ iha sat ātmatva upadeśāt artha antara bhūtāḥ  sambhavati nanu sat asmi iti buddhi mātram iha kartavya tayā codyate na tu ajñātam sadasi iti jñāpyata iti ced  nanu asmin pakṣe api aśrutam śrutam bhavati ityādi anupapannam na sat asmi iti buddhi vidheḥ stuti artha tvāt  na ācāryavān puruṣaḥ  veda tasya tāvat eva ciram iti upadeśāt yadi hi sat asmi iti buddhi mātram kartavya tayā vidhīyate na tu tvaṃśabda vācyasya sat rūpa tvam eva tadā na ācāryavān veda iti jñāna upāya upadeśaḥ  vācyaḥ syāt  yathā agnihotram juhuyāt iti evamādiṣu artha prāptam eva acāryavat tvam iti tadvat  tasya tāvat eva ciram iti ca kṣepa karaṇam na yuktam syāt  sat ātma tattve avijñāte api sakṛt buddhi mātra karaṇe mokṣa prasaṅgāt  na ca tad tvam asi iti ukte na aham saditi pramāṇa vākya janitā buddhīḥ nivartayitum śakyā na utpannā iti vā śakyam vaktum sarva upaniṣad vākyānām tad para tayā eva upakṣayāt yathā agnihotra ādi vidhi janita agni hotra ādi kartavyatā buddhīnām atathārtha tvam anutpanna tvam vā na śakyate vaktum tadvat  yad tu uktam sat ātmā san  ātmānam katham na jānīyāt iti na asau doṣaḥ kārya karaṇa saṅghāta vyatiriktaḥ  aham jīvaḥ kartā bhoktā iti api svabhāvataḥ prāṇinām vijñāna adarśanāt kisu tasya sat ātma vijñānam katham evam vyatirikta vijñāne sati teṣām kartṛtva ādi vijñānam sambhavati dṛśyate ca tadvat tasya api deha ādiṣu ātma buddhi tvāt na syāt sadā ātma vijñānam tasmāt vikāra anṛta adhikṛta jīva ātma vijñāna nivartakam eva idam vākyam tad tvam asi iti siddham iti vāc vāva vāgiti indriyam jihvā bhūla ādiṣu aṣṭasu sthāneṣu sthitam varṇānām abhivyañjakam varṇāḥ ca nāma iti nāmnaḥ  vāc bhūyasi iti ucyate kāryat hi kāraṇam bhūyaḥ dṛṣṭam loke yathā putrāt pitā tadvat  katham ca vāc nāmnaḥ  bhūyasi iti āhavāc vā ṛgvedam vijñāpayati ayamṛgveda iti tathā yajurvedam ityādi samānam hṛdaya jñam hṛdaya priyam tad viparītam ahṛdaya jñam yad yadi vāc nābhaviṣyat dharma ādi na vyajñāpayiṣyat vāc abhāve adhyayana abhāve tad artha śravaṇa abhāvaḥ tad śravaṇa abhāve dharma ādi na vyajñāpayiṣyan  vijñātam abhaviṣyat iti arthaḥ tasmāt vāc eva etad śabda uccāraṇena sarvam vijñāpayati atas  bhūyasī vāc nāmnaḥ tasmāt vācam brahma iti upāḥsva samānam anyat  manaḥ  manasi ana viśiṣṭam antaḥkaraṇam vācaḥ  bhūyas  tad hi manasi ana vyāpāravat vācam vaktavye prerayati tena vāc manasi antar bhavati yad ca yasmin  antar bhavati tad tasya vyāpaka tvāt tatas  bhūyaḥ bhavati yathā vai loke dve vā āmalake phale dve vā kole badara phale dvau vā akṣau vibhītaka phale muṣṭiḥ anubhavati muṣṭiḥ te phale vyāpnoti muṣṭau hi te antarbhavataḥ evam vācam ca nāma ca āmalaka ādivat manaḥ  anubhavati sa yadā puruṣe yasmin kāle manasā antaḥkaraṇena manasyati manasyanam vivakṣā buddhiḥ katham mantrānadhīyīya uccārayeyam iti evam vivakṣām kṛtvā atha adhīte tathā karmāṇi kurvīya iti cikīrṣā buddhim kṛtvā atha kurute putrān  ca paśūn  ca iccheyā iti prāpti icchām kṛtvā tad prāpti upāya anuṣṭhānena atha icchate putra ādīn prāpnoti iti arthaḥ tathā imam ca lokam amum ca upāyena iccheyā iti tad prapti upāya anuṣṭhānena atha icchace prāpnoti manaḥ  hi ātma ātmanaḥ kartṛ tvam bhoktṛ tvam ca sati manasi na anyathā iti manaḥ  hi ātmā iti ucyate manaḥ  hi lokaḥ sati eva hi manasi lokaḥ  bhavati tad prāpti upāya anuṣṭhānam ca iti manaḥ  hi lokaḥ  yasmāt tasmāt manaḥ  hi brahma yata evam tasmāt mana upāḥsva iti sa yaḥ  ityādi samānam saṃkalpaḥ  vāva manasaḥ  bhūyān saṃkalpaḥ  api manasi anavat antaḥkaraṇa vṛttiḥ kartavyā kartavya viṣaya vibhāgena samarthanam vibhāgena hi samarthite viṣaye cikīrṣā buddhiḥ manasi ana anantaram bhavati katham yadā vai saṃkalpayate kartavyā ādi viṣayān vibhajata idam kartum yuktam iti atha manasyati mantrānadhīyīya ityādi atha anantaram vācam īrayati mantra ādi uccāraṇe tām ca vācam u nāmni nāma uccāraṇa nimittam vivakṣām kṛtvā irayati nāmni nāma sāmānye mantrāḥ śabda viśeṣāḥ santa ekam bhavanti antarbhavanti iti arthaḥ sāmānye hi viśeṣaḥ  antabhavati mantreṣu karmāṇi ekam bhavanti mantra prakāśitāni karmāṇi kriyante na amantrakam asti karma yad hi mantra prakāśanena labdha sattākam satkarma brāhmaṇena idam kartavyam asmai phalāya iti vidhīyate yā api utpattiḥ brāhmaṇeṣu karmaṇām dṛśyate sā api mantreṣu labdha sattākānām eva karmaṇām spaṣṭīkaraṇam na hi mantrā prakāśitam karma kiñcid brāhmaṇa utpannam dṛśyate trayī vihitam karma iti prasiddham loke trayī śabdaḥ ca ṝc yajuḥ sāma samākhyā mantreṣu karmāṇi kavayaḥ  yāni apaśyan  iti ca ātharvaṇe tasmāt yuktam mantreṣu karmāṇi ekam bhavanti iti tāni ha vā etāni mana ādīni saṃkalpa ekāyanāni saṃkalpa ekaḥ  ayanam gamanam pralayaḥ  yeṣām tāni saṃkalpa ekāyanāni saṃkalpa ātmakāni utpattau saṃkalpe pratiṣṭhitāni sthitau samakḷpatām saṃkalpam kṛtavatyau  iva hi dyauḥ ca pṛthivī ca dyāvāpṛthivyau niścale lakṣyete tathā samakalpetām vāyuḥ ca ākāśam ca etau  api saṃkalpam kṛtavantau  iva tathā samakalpantām āpaḥ ca tejaḥ ca svena rūpema niścalāni lakṣyante yatas teṣām dyāvāpṛthivī ādīnām saṃkḷptyai saṃkalpa nimittam varṣam saṃkalpante anna mayā hi prāṇā anna upaṣṭambhakāḥ annam dāma iti hi śrutiḥ teṣām saṃkḷptyai mantrāḥ saṃkalpante prāṇāvān hi mantrān adhīte na abalaḥ mantrāṇām hi saṃkḷptyai karmāṇi agnihotra ādīni saṃkalpante anuṣṭhīyamānāni mantra prakāśitāni samarthībhavanti phalāya tatas  lokaḥ phalam saṃkalpate karma kartṛ samavāyitayā samarthībhavati iti arthaḥ lokasya saṃkḷptyai sarvam jagat saṃkalpate svarūpā vaikalyāya etad hi idam sarvam jagat yad phala avasānam tad sarvam saṃkalpa mūlam atas  viśiṣṭaḥ sa eṣa saṃkalpaḥ atas  saṃkalpam upāḥsva iti uktvā phalam āha tad upāsakasya sa yaḥ saṃkalpam brahma iti brahma buddhyā upāstekḷptān vai dhātrāsya ime lokāḥ phalam iti kḷptān samarthitān saṃkalpitān sa vidvān dhruvāt nityān atyanta adhruva apekṣayā dhruvaḥ ca svayam lokinaḥ  hi adhruva tve loke dhruva kḷpti vyartha iti dhruvaḥ san pratiṣṭhita anupakaraṇa saṃpannān iti arthaḥ paśu putra ādibhiḥ pratitiṣṭhati iti darśanāt svayam ca pratiṣṭhita ātmīya upakaraṇa saṃpannaḥ  avyatham ānāna mitra ādi trāsa rah itānavyathamānaḥ ca svayam abhisidhyati abhiprāpnoti iti arthaḥ yāvat saṃkalpasya gatam saṃkalpa gocaraḥ tatra asya yathākāma cāraḥ  bhavati ātmanaḥ saṃkalpasya na tu sarveṣām saṃkalpasya iti uttara phala virodhāt  yaḥ saṃkalpam brahma iti upāsta ityādi pūrvavat  cittam vāva saṃkalpāt bhūyas  cittam cetayitṛ tvam prāpta kāla anurūpa bodhavat tvam atītāna gata viṣaya prayojana nirūpaṇa sāmarthyam ca tad saṃkalpāt api bhūyas  katham yadā vai prāptam iti cetayate tadā dānāya vā apohāya vā atha saṃkalpayate atha manasyati ityādi pūrvavat  tāni saṃkalpa ādīni karma phala antāni citta aikāyanāni citta ātmāni citta utpattīni citte pratiṣṭhitāni citta sthitāni iti api pūrvavat  kiñca cittasya māhātmyam yasmāt cittam saṃkalpa ādi mūlam tasmāt yadi api bahu vid bahu śāsra ādi parijñānavān sanna cittaḥ  bhavati prāpta ādi cetayitṛtva sāmarthya virahitaḥ  bhavati tam nipuṇā laukikānāyam asti vidyamānaḥ  api asat sama eva iti enam āhuḥ yad ca ayam kiñcid chāsra ādi veda śrutavān  tad api asya vṛthā eva iti kathayanti kasmāt  yadi ayam vidvān syāt ittham evam acittaḥ  na syāt tasmāt asya śrutam api aśrutam eva iti āhuḥ iti arthaḥ atha alpa vid api yadi cittavān bhavati tasmā etasmai tad ukta artha grahaṇāya eva utā api śuśrūṣante śrotum icchanti tasmāt ca cittam hi eva eṣām saṃkalpa ādīnām ekāyanam ityādi pūrvavat  citta an upacitān huddhimat guṇaiḥ sa citta upāsakaḥ  dhruvān ityādi ca ukta artham dhyānam vāva cittāt bhūyas  dhyānam nāma śāsra ukta devatā ādi ālambaneṣu acalaḥ  bhinna jātīyaiḥ anantaritaḥ pratyaya saṃtānaḥ ekāgra tā iti yam āhuḥ dṛśyate ca dhyānasya māhātmyam phalataḥ katham yathā yogī dhyāyat niścalaḥ  bhavati dhyāna phala lābhe evam dhyāyati iva niścalā dṛśyate pṛthivī dhyāyati iva antarikṣam ityādi samānam anyat  devāḥ ca manuṣyāḥ ca deva manuṣyā manuṣyā eva vā deva samā deva manuṣyāḥ śama ādi guṇa saṃpannā manuṣyā deva svarūpam na jahati iti arthaḥ yasmāt evam viśiṣṭam dhyānam tasmāt ya iha loke manuṣyāṇām eva dhanaiḥ vidyayā guṇaiḥ vā mahat tām mahat tvam prāpnuvanti dhana ādi mahattva hetum labhanta iti arthaḥ dhyāna apāda aṃśā iva dhyānasya āpādanam āpādaḥ  dhyāna phala lābha iti etad tasya aṃśaḥ  avayavaḥ kalā kācid dhyāna phala lābha kalāvanta iva eva iti arthaḥ te bhavanti niścalā iva lakṣyante na kṣudrā iva atha ye punar alpāḥ kṣudrāḥ kiñcid api dhana ādi mahattva eka deśam aprāptāḥ te pūrva ukta viparītāḥ kalahinaḥ kalaha śīlāḥ piśunāḥ para doṣa udbhāsakā upavādinaḥ para doṣam sāmīpya yuktam eva vaditum śīlam yoṣām ta upavādinaḥ ca bhavanti atha ye mahat tvam prāptā dhana ādi nimittam te anyān prati prabhavanti iti prabhavaḥ  vidyā ācārya rāja īśvara ādayaḥ  dhyāna apāda aṃśā iva ityādi ukta artham atas  dṛśyate dhyānasya mahat tvam phalataḥ atas  bhūyas cittādataḥ tad upāḥsva ityādi ukta artham vijñānam vāva dhyānāt bhūyas  vijñānam śāsra artha viṣayam jñānam tasya dhyāna kāraṇa tvāt dhyānāt bhūyaḥ tvam katham ca tasya bhūyastvam iti āha vijñānena vā ṛgvedam vijānāti aya mṛgveda iti pramāṇa tayā yasya artha jñānam dhyāna kāraṇam tathā yajurvedam ityādi kiñca paśu ādīn  ca dharma adharmau śāsra siddhau sādhu asādhunī lokataḥ siddhe smārte vā dṛṣṭa adṛṣṭa aviṣayam ca sarvam vijñānena eva vijānāti iti arthaḥ tasmāt yuktam dhyāna ādi jñānasya bhūyas tvam atas  vijñānam upāḥsva iti śṛṇu upāsana phalam vijñānavataḥ  vijñānam yeṣu lokeṣu tān vijñānavataḥ  lokān jñānavataḥ ca abhisidhyati abhiprāpnoti vijñānam śāsra artha viṣayam jñānam anya viṣayam naipuṇyam tadvadbhiḥ yuktān  lokāt na aprāpnoti iti arthaḥ yāvat vijñānasya ityādi pūrvavat  balam vāva vijñānāt bhūyas  balam iti anna upayoga janitam manasaḥ  vijñeye pratibhāna sāmarthyam anaśanādṛś ādīni na vai mā pratibhānti bhaḥ iti śruteḥ śarīre api tad eva utthāna ādi sāmarthyam yasmāt vijñānavatām śatam api ekaḥ prāṇī balavān ā kampayate yathā hastī mattaḥ  manuṣyāṇām śatam samuditam api yasmāt evam anna ādi upayoga nimittam balam tasmāt sa puruṣaḥ  yadā balī balena tad vān bhavati atha utthāta utthānasya kartā uttiṣṭhan  ca gurūṇām ācāryasya ca paricaritā paricaraṇasya śuśrūṣāyāḥ kartā bhavati paricaran  upasattā teṣām samīpa gaḥ antaraṅgaḥ prayaḥ bhavati iti arthaḥ upasīdan  ca samīpyam gacchan  ekāgra tayā ācāryasya anyasya ca upadeṣṭuḥ guroḥ draṣṭā bhavati tatas tad uktasya śrotā bhavati tatas  idam ebhiḥ uktam evam upapadyata iti upapattitaḥ mantā bhavati manvānaḥ ca boddhā bhavati evam eva idam iti tatas  evam niścitya tad ukta arthasya kartā anuṣṭhātā bhavati vijñāta anuṣṭhāna phalasya anubhavitā bhavati iti arthaḥ kiñca balasya māhātmyam balena vai pṛthivī tiṣṭhati ityādi ujvartham annam vāva balāt bhūyas  bala hetu tvāt  katham annasya bala hetutvam iti ucyate yasmāt bala kāraṇam annam tasmāt yadi api kaścid daśa rātrīḥ na aśnīyāt saḥ anna upayoga animittasya balasya hānyā mriyate na ced mriyate yadyu ha jīvet  dṛśyante hi māsam api anaśnantaḥ  jīvantaḥ athavā sa jīvan  api adraṣṭā bhavati guroḥ api tatas  eva aśrotā ityādi pūrva viparītam sarvam bhavati atha yadā bahūni ahāni anaśitaḥ  darśana ādi kriyāsu asamarthaḥ san  annasyāyī āgamana m āyaḥ  annasya prāptiḥ iti arthaḥ sā yasya vidyate saḥ  anna sya āyī āya iti etad varṇa vyatyayena atha annasya āyā iti api pāṭha evam eva arthaḥ draṣṭā ityādi kārya śravaṇāt dṛśyate hi anna upayoge darśana ādi sāmarthyam na tad aprāptāvataḥ annam upāḥ sva iti phalam ca annavataḥ prabhūtānnān vai sa lokān pānavataḥ prabhūta udakān  ca anna pānayoḥ nitya saṃbandhāt lokān abhisi dhyati samānam anyat  āpaḥ  vāva annāt bhūyasyaḥ  anna kāraṇa tvāt  yasmāt evam tasmāt yadā yasmin kāle su vṛṣṭiḥ sasya hitā śobhanā vṛṣṭiḥ na bhavati tadā vyādhīyante prāṇā duḥkhinaḥ  bhavanti kiṃnimittam iti āha annam asmin saṃvatsare naḥ kanīyaḥ  alpataram bhaviṣyati iti atha punar yadā su vṛṣṭiḥ bhavati tad ānandinaḥ sukhinaḥ  hṛṣṭāḥ prāṇāḥ prāṇinaḥ  bhavanti antam bahu prabhūtam bhaviṣyati iti ap saṃbhava tvāt mūrtasya annasya apa eva imā mūrta amṛrta bheda ākāra pariṇatā iti mūrtā yā iyam pṛthivī yad antarikṣam ityādi āpa eva imā mūrtā atas  apa upāḥsva iti phalam sa yaḥ  apaḥ  brahma iti upāsta āpnoti sarvān kāmān kāmyāt mūrtimataḥ  viṣayān iti arthaḥ apsaṃbhava tvāt ca tṛpteḥ ambu pāsanāt tṛptimān  ca bhavati samānam anyat  tejaḥ  vāvādbhyaḥ  bhūyas  tejasaḥ  apakāraṇa tvāt  katham apkāraṇa tvam iti āha yasmāt ap yoniḥ tejaḥ tasmāt tad vā etad tejaḥ  vāyum āgṛhya  aṣṭabhya sva ātmanā niścalīkṛtya vāyum ākāśam abhitapati ākāśam abhivyāpnuvat tapati yadā tad āhuḥ laukikā niśocati saṃtapati sāmānyena jagannitapati dehānataḥ varṣiṣyati vā iti prasiddham hi loke kāraṇam abhyudyatam dṛṣṭavataḥ kārya bhaviṣyati iti vijñānam teja eva tad pūrvam ātmānam udbhūtam darśayitvā atha anantaram apaḥ sṛjate atas  apsraṣṭṛ tvāt bhūnyaḥ  adbhyaḥ tejaḥ kiñca anyat tad etad teja eva stanayitnu rūpeṇa varṣa hetuḥ bhavati katham ūrdhvābhiḥ ca ūrdhva gābhiḥ vidyudbhiḥ tiraścībhiḥ ca tiryak gatābhiḥ ca saha ahrādāḥ stanana śabdāḥ caranti tasmāt tad darśanāt āhuḥ laukikā vidyotate stanayati varṣiṣyati vā ityādi ukta artham atas teja upāḥsva iti tasya tejasa upāsana phalam tejasvī vai bhavati tejasvata eva ca lokān bhāsvataḥ prakāśavataḥ  apahata tamaskān bāhya ādhyātmikā jñāna ādi apanīta tamaskānabhi sidhyati ṛjvartham anyat  ākāśaḥ  vāva tejasaḥ  bhūyān vāyu sahitasya tejasaḥ kāraṇa tvāt vyomnaḥ  vāyum āgṛhya iti tejasā saha uktaḥ  vāyuḥ iti pṛthak iha na uktaḥ tejasaḥ kāraṇam hi loke kāryāt bhūyaḥ dṛṣṭam yathā ghaṭa ādibhyaḥ  mṛd tathā ākāśaḥ  vāyu sahitasya tejasaḥ kāraṇam iti tatas  bhūyān katham ākāśaḥ  vai sūryācandramasau  ubhau tejaḥ rūpau vidyut nakṣatrāṇi agniḥ ca tejaḥ rūpāṇi ākāśe antar  yad ca yasya antar varti tad alpam bhūya itarat  kiñca ākāśena āhvayati ca anyam anya āhūtaḥ ca itara ākāśena śṛṇoti anya uktam ca śabdam anyaḥ pratiśṛṇoti ākāśe ramate krīḍati anyonyam sarvaḥ tathā na ramate ca ākāśe vadhvādi viyoga ākāśe jāyate na mūrtena avaṣṭabdhe tathā ākāśam abhilakṣya aṅkura ādi jāyate na pratilomam ata ākāśam upāḥ sva phalam śṛṇu ākāśavataḥ  vai vistāra yuktān sa vidvān  lokān prakāśavataḥ prakāśa ākāśayoḥ nitya saṃbandhāt prakāśavataḥ ca lokān asaṃbādhān saṃbādhanam saṃbādhaḥ saṃbādhaḥ  anyonya pīḍā tad rahitān asaṃbādha anurugāyavataḥ  vistīrṇa gatīn vistīrṇa pracārān  lokān abhisidhyati yāvat ākāśasya ityādi ukta artham smaraḥ  vā avāka ākāśāt bhūyas  smaraṇam smaraḥ  antaḥkaraṇa dharmaḥ sa ākāśāt bhūyān iti draṣṭavyam liṅga vyatyayena smartuḥ smaraṇe hi sati ākāśa ādi sarvam arthavat smaraṇavataḥ  bhogya tvāt  asati tu smarame sat api asat eva sattva kārya abhāvāt na api sattvam smṛti abhāve śakyam ākāśa ādīnām avagantum iti atas  smaraṇasya ākāśāt bhṛyaḥ tvam dṛśyate hi loke smaraṇasya bhūyas tvam yasmāt tasmāt yadi api samuditā bahava ekasmin  āsīḥ an  upaviśeyuḥ te tatra āsīnā anyonya bhāṣitam api na smarantaḥ ced syuḥ na eva te kañcana śabdam śṛṇuyuḥ tathā na manvīran mantavyam ced smareyuḥ tadā manvīran smṛti abhāvāt na manvīran  tathā na vijānīran yadā vāva te smareyuḥ mantavyam vijñātavyam śrotavyam ca atha śṛṇuyuḥ atha manvīran  atha vijānīran tathā smareṇa vai mama putrā eta iti putrān vijānāti smareṇa paśūn atas  bhūyas tvāt smaram upāḥsva iti ukta artham anyat  āśā vāva smarāt bhūyasī āśā prāpta vastu ākāṅkṣa āśā tṛṣṇā kāma iti yām āhuḥ paryāyaiḥ sā ca smarāt bhūyasī katham āśayā hi antaḥkaraṇa sthayā smarati smartavyam āśā viṣaya rūpam smaran  asau smaraḥ  bhavatyata āśeddha āśaya abhivardhitaḥ smara bhūtaḥ smarat nṛś ādīn mantrān adhīte adhītya ca tad artham brāhmaṇebhyaḥ  vidhīn  ca śrutvā karmāṇi kurute tad phala āśaya eva putrān  ca karma phala bhūtān icchate abhivāñchati āśayā eva tad sādhanāni anutiṣṭhati imam ca lokam āśā iddha eva smaran  loka saṃgraha hetubhiḥ icchate amum ca lokam āśā iddhaḥ smaran  tad sādhana anuṣṭhānena icchate ata āśā ra śāna avabaddham smara ākāśa ādi nām aparyantam jagat cakrībhūtam pratiprāṇi atra āśa āyāḥ smarāt api bhūyas tvam iti ata āśām upāḥ sva yaḥ tu āśām brahma iti upāste śṛṇu tasya phalam āśayā sadā upāsitayā asya upāsakasya sarve kāmāḥ samṛdhyanti samṛddhim gacchanti amoghā hāsya āśiṣaḥ prārthanāḥ sarvā bhavanti yad prārthitam sarvam tad avaśyam bhavati iti arthaḥ yāvat āśāyā gatam ityādi pūrvavat  nāma upakramam āśāntam kārya kāraṇa tvena nimitta naimittika tvena ca uttarottara bhūyastayā avasthitam smṛti nimitta sadbhāvam āśā raśanā pāśaiḥ vipāśitam sarvam sarvatas  bisam iva tantubhiḥ yasmin prāṇe samarpitam yena ca sarvatas  vyāpinā antar bahis gatena sūtre maṇi gaṇā iva sūtreṇa grathitam vidhṛtam ca sa eṣa prāṇaḥ  vā āśāyā bhūyān katham asya bhūyastvam iti āha dṛṣṭāntena samarthayan  tad bhūyaḥ tvam yathā vai loke ratha cakrasya ārā ratha nābhau samarpitāḥ saṃprotāḥ saṃpraveśitā iti etad  evam asmin  liṅga saṃghāta rūpe prāṇe prajñā ātmani dehike mukhye yasmin parā devatā nāma rūpa vyākaraṇāya ādarśa ādau pratibimbivat jīvena ātmanā anupratiṣṭā yaḥ ca mahā rājasya iva sarva adhikārī īśvarasya kasmin  at nu aham utkrānta utkrāntaḥ  baviṣyāmi kasmin vā pratiṣṭhite pratiṣṭhāsyāmi iti sa prāṇam asṛjata iti śruteḥ yaḥ tu cchāyā iva anugata īśvaram tad yathā rathasya āreṣu nemiḥ arpitaḥ  nābhāvarā arpitā evam eva etā bhūtamātrāḥ prajñāmātrāsu arpitāḥ prajñāmātrāḥ prāṇe arpitāḥ sa eṣa prāṇa eva prajñā ātmā iti kauṣītakinām ata evam asmin prāṇe sarvam yathā uktam samarpitam atas  sa eṣa prāṇaḥ  aparatantraḥ prāṇena sva śaktyā eva yāti na anya kṛtam gamana ādi kriyāsu asya sāmarthyam iti arthaḥ sarvam kriyā kāraka phala bheda jātam prāṇa eva na prāṇāt bahis bhūtam asti iti prakaraṇa arthaḥ prāṇaḥ prāṇam dadāti yad dadāti tad svītma bhūtam eva yasmai dadāti tad api prāṇāya eva atas  pitṛ ādi ākhyaḥ  api prāṇa eva katham pitṛ ādi śabdānām prasiddha artha utsargeṇa prāṇa viṣaya tvam iti ucyate sati prāṇe pitṛ ādiṣu pitṛ ādi śabda prayogāt tad utkrāntau ca prayoga abhāvāt katham tad iti āha sa yaḥ kaścid pitṛ ādīnām anyatamam yadi tam bhṛśam iva tad ananurūpam iva kiñcid vacanam tvaṅkāra ādi yuktam pratyāha tadā enam pārśva sthā āhuḥ vivekinaḥ  dhik tvā astu dhik astu tvām iti evam pitṛ hā vai tvam pituḥ hanta ityādi atha enāneva utkrānta prāṇān  tyakta dehān atha yadi api śūlena samāsam samasya vyatidahet vyatyasya saṃdahet evam api atikrūram karma samāsa vyatyāsa ādi prakāreṇa dahana lakṣaṇam tad deha saṃbaddham eva kurvāṇam na eva enam brūyuḥ pitṛ hā ityādi tasmāt anvaya vi atirekābhyām avagamyata etad pitṛ ādi ākhyaḥ  api prāṇa eva iti tasmāt prāṇaḥ  hi eva etāni pitṛ ādīni sarvāṇi bhavati calāni sthirāṇi ca sa vā eṣa prāṇa vid evam yathā ukta prakāreṇa paśyan phalataḥ  anubhavan  evam manvāna upapattibhiḥ cintayan  evam vijānan  upapattibhiḥ saṃyojya evam eva iti niścayam kurvan  iti arthaḥ manana vijñānābhyām hi saṃbhūtaḥ śāsra arthaḥ  niścitaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ  bhavet  ata evam paśyan  ativādī bhavati nāma ādya aśāntam atītya vadana śīlaḥ  bhavati iti arthaḥ tam ced brūyuḥ tam yadi evam ativādinam sarvadā sarvaiḥ śabdaiḥ nāma ādya aśāntam atītya vartamānam prāṇam evam vadantam evam paśyantam ativadana śīlam ativādinam brahma ādi stamba paryantasya hi jagataḥ prāṇa ātmā aham iti bruvāṇam yadi brūyuḥ ati vādyasi iti bāḍham ativādī asmi iti brūyāt na apahnuvīta kasmāt hi asau  apahnuvīta yad prāṇam sarveśvara mayam aham asmi iti ātma tvena upagataḥ eṣa tu vā ativadati yaḥ satyena ativadati saḥ  aham bhagavaḥ satyena ati vadāni iti satyam tu eva vijijñāsitavyam iti satyam bhagavaḥ  vijijñāsa iti sa eṣa nāradaḥ sarva atiśayam prāṇam svam ātmānam sarva ātmānam śrutvā na atas  param asti iti upararāma na pūrvavat kim asti bhagavaḥ prāṇāt bhūya iti papraccha yatas tam evam vikāra anṛta brahma vijñānena parituṣṭam akṛtārtham parama artha satya ativādinam ātmānam manyamānam yogyam śiṣyam mithyā graha viśeṣāt vipracyāvayan  āha bhagavān sanatkumāraḥ eṣa tu vā ativadati yam aham vakṣyāmi na prāṇa vid ati vādī paramārthataḥ nāma ādi apekṣam tu tasya ativādi tvam yaḥ tu bhūma ākhyam sarva atikrāntam tattvam parama artha satyam veda saḥ  ativādī iti ata āha eṣa tu vā ativadati yaḥ sateyana parama artha satya vijñāna vattayā ativadati saḥ  aham tvām prapannaḥ  bhagavan satyena ativadāni tathā amām niyunaktu bhagavān yathā aham satyena ativadāni iti abhiprāyaḥ yadi evam satyena ati vaditum icchasi satyam eva tu tāvat vijijñāsitavyam iti ukta āha nāradaḥ tathā astu tarhi satya bhagavaḥ  vijijñāse viśeṣeṇa jñātum iccheyam tvad taḥ  aham iti yadā vai satyam paramārtha taḥ  vijānāti idam parama arthaḥ satyam iti tatas  anṛtam vikāra jātam vācā ārambhaṇam hitvā sarva vikāra avastham sa deva ekam satyam iti tad eva atha vadati yadvat ati nanu vikāraḥ  api satyam eva nāma rūpe satyam tābhya mayam prāṇaḥ channaḥ prāṇā vai satyam teṣām eṣa satyam iti śruti antarāt satyam uktam satya tvam śruti antare vikārasya na tu parama artha apekṣam uktam kim tarhi indriya viṣayatva apekṣam sat ca tyat ca iti satyam iti uktam tad dvāreṇa ca parama artha satyasya upalabdhiḥ vivakṣitā iti prāṇā vai satyam teṣām eṣa satyam iti ca uktam iha api tad iṣṭam eva iha tu praṇaviṣayāt parama artha satya vijñāna abhimānāt vyutthāpya nāradam yad sat eva satyam paramārtha taḥ  bhūma ākhyam tad vijñāpayiṣyāmi iti eṣa viśeṣataḥ  vivakṣitor athaḥ na avijānan satyam vadati yaḥ tu avijānan vadati saḥ  agni ādi śabdena agni adīn parama artha sat rūpāt manyamānaḥ  vadati na tu te rūpa traya vyatirekeṇa parama arthaḥ santi tathā tāni api rūpāṇi sat apekṣayā na eva santi iti atas  na avijānan satyam vadati vijānan  eva satyam vadati na ca tad satya vijñānam avijijñāsitam aprārthitam jñāyata iti āha vijñānam tu eva vijijñāsitavyam iti yadi evam vijñānam bhagavaḥ  vijijñāsa iti evam satya ādīnām ca uttara uttarāṇām karoti antānām pūrva pūrva hetu tvam vyākhyeyam yadā vai manuta iti matiḥ mananam tarkaḥ  mantavya viṣaya ādaraḥ āstikya buddhiḥ śraddhā niṣṭhā guru śuśrūṣā ādiḥ tad para tvam brahma vijñānāya yadā vai karoti kṛtiḥ indriya saṃyamaḥ citta ekāgra tā karaṇam ca satyām hi tasyām niṣṭhā ādīni yathā uktāni bhavanti vijñāna avasānāni sā api kṛtiḥ yadā sukham labhate sukham niratiśayam vakṣyamāṇam labdhavyam mayā iti manyate tadā bhavati iti arthaḥ yathā dṛṣṭa phala sukhā kṛtiḥ tathā iha api na asukham labdhvā karoti bhaviṣyat api phalam labdhvā iti ucyate tad uddiśya pravṛtti upapatteḥ atha idānīm kṛtyādiṣu uttara uttareṣu satsu satyam svayam eva pratibhāsata iti na tad vijñānāya pṛthak yatnaḥ kārya iti prāptam tatas  idam ucyate sukham tu eva vijijñāsitavyam ityādi sukham bhagavaḥ  vijijñāsa iti abhimukhībhūtāya āha yaḥ  vai bhūmā mahat niratiśayam bahu iti paryāyāḥ tad sukham tator avāksa atiśaya tvāt alpam atas tasmin  alpe sukham na asti alpasya adhika tṛṣṇā hetu tvāt tṛṣṇā ca duḥkha bījam na hi duḥkha bījam sukham dṛṣṭam jvara ādi loke tasmāt yuktam na alpe sukham asti iti atas  bhūmā eva sukham tṛṣṇā ādi duḥkha bījatva asaṃbhavāt bhūmnaḥ kiṃlakṣaṇaḥ  asau bhūma iti āha yatra yasmin bhūmni tattve na anyat draṣṭavyam anyena karaṇena draṣṭā anyaḥ  vibhaktaḥ  dṛśyāt paśyati tathā na anyat śṛṇoti nāma rūpayoḥ eva antarbhāvāt viṣaya bhedasya tad grāhakayoḥ eva iha darśana śravaṇayoḥ grahaṇam anyeṣām ca upalakṣaṇa artha tvena mananam ca atra uktam draṣṭavyam na anyat manuta iti prāyaśas  manana pūrvaka tvāt vijñānasya tathā na anyat vijānāti evaṃlakṣaṇaḥ  yaḥ sa bhūmā kim atra prasidrā ani adarśana abhāvaḥ  bhūmni ucyate na anyat paśyati ityādinā atha anyat na paśyati ātmānam paśyati iti etad  kiñcātas  yadi anya darśana ādya bhāva mātram iti ucyate tadā dvaita saṃvyavahāra vilakṣaṇaḥ  bhūma iti uktam bhavati atha anyat raśana viśeṣa pratiṣedhena ātmānam paśyati iti ucyate tadā ekasmin  eva kriyā kāraka phala bhedaḥ  abhyupagataḥ  bhavet  yadi evam kaḥ  doṣaḥ syāt  nanu ayam eva doṣaḥ saṃsāra anivṛttiḥ kriyā kāraka phala bhedaḥ  hi saṃsāra iti ātmā ekatva eva kriyā kāraka phala bhedaḥ saṃsāra vilakṣaṇa iti ced  na ātmanaḥ  nirviśeṣa ekatva abhyupagame darśana ādi kriyā kāraka phala bheda abhyupagamasya śabda mātra tvāt  anya darśana ādi bhāva ukti pakṣe api yatra iti anyat na paśyati iti ca viśeṣaṇe anarthake syātām iti ced  dṛśyate hi loke yatra śūnye gṛhe anyat na paśyati iti ukte stambha ādīn ātmānam ca na na paśyati iti gamyate evam iha api iti ced  na tad tvam asi iti ekatva upadeśāt adhikaraṇa adhikartavya bheda anupapatteḥ tathā sat ekam eva advitīyam satyam iti ṣaṣṭhe nirdhārita tvāt  adṛśye anātmye na saṃdṛśe tiṣṭhati rūpam asya vijñāta āram are kena vijānīyāt  ityādi śrutibhyaḥ sva ātmani darśana ādi anupapattiḥ yatra iti viśeṣaṇam anarthakam prāptam iti ced  na avidyā kṛta bheda apekṣa tvāt yathā sati ekatva advitīyatva buddhim prakṛtām apekṣya sat ekam eva advitīyam iti saṃkhyā ādi anarham api ucyate evam bhūmni ekasmin  eva yatra iti viśeṣaṇam avidyā avasthāyām anya darśana anuvādena ca bhūmnaḥ tad abhāvatva lakṣaṇasya vivakṣita tvāt na anyat paśyati iti viśeṣaṇam tasmāt saṃsāra vyavahāraḥ  bhūmni na asti iti samudāya arthaḥ atha yatra avidyā viṣaye anyaḥ  anyena anyat paśyati iti tad alpam avidyā kāla bhāvi iti arthaḥ yathā svapna dṛśyam vastu prāk  prabodhāt tad kāla bhāvi iti tadvat  tatas  eva tad martyam vināśi svapna vastuvat eva tad viparotaḥ  bhūmā yaḥ tad amṛtam tad śabdaḥ  amṛtatva paraḥ sa tarhi evaṃlakṣaṇaḥ  bhūmā he bhagavan kasmin pratiṣṭhita iti uktavantam nāradam pratyāha sanatkimāraḥ sve mahimni iti sva  ātmīye mahimni māhātmye vibhūtau pratiṣṭhitaḥ  bhūmā yadi pratiṣṭhām icchasi kvacid yadi vā parama artham eva pṛcchasi na mahimni api pratiṣṭhita iti brūmaḥ apratiṣṭhitaḥ  anāśritaḥ  bhūmā kvacid api iti arthaḥ yadi sva mahimni pratiṣṭhitaḥ  bhūmā katham tarhi apratiṣṭha ucyate śṛṇu gaḥ aśvādi iha mahimā iti ācakṣate gāvaḥ ca aśvāḥ ca gaḥ aśvam dvandva ekavat bhāvaḥ sarvatra gavāśvādi mahimā iti prasiddham tad āśritaḥ tad pratiṣṭhaḥ caitraḥ  bhavati yathā na aham evam svatas  anyam mahimānam āśritaḥ  bhūmā caitravat iti bravīmi atra hetu tvena anyaḥ  hi anyasmin pratiṣṭhita iti vyavahitena sambandhaḥ kintu evam bravīmi iti ha uvāca sa eva ityādi kasmāt punar  kvacid na pratiṣṭhita iti ucyate yasmāt sa eva bhūma adhastāt na tad vyatirekeṇa anyat vidyate yasmin pratiṣṭhitaḥ syāt  tathā upariṣṭāt ityādi samānam sati bhūmnaḥ anyasmin bhūmā hi pratiṣṭhitaḥ syāt na tu tad asti sa eva tu sarvam atas tasmāt asau na kvacid pratiṣṭhitaḥ yatra na anyat paśyati iti adhikaraṇa adhikartavya tā nirdeśāt sa eva adhastāt iti ca parokṣa nirdeśāt draṣṭarjīvāt anyaḥ bhūmā syāt iti āśaṅkā kasyacid mā bhūt iti athātas  anantaram ahaṅkāra ādeśaḥ  ahaṅkāreṇa adiśyata iti ahaṅkāra ādeśaḥ draṣṭuḥ ananyatva darśana artham bhūmā eva nirdiśyate ahaṅkāreṇa aham eva adhastāt ityādinā ahaṅkāreṇa deha ādi saṃghātaḥ  api ādiśyate avivekibhiḥ iti atas tad āśaṅkā mā bhūt iti atha anantaram ātma ādeśa ātmanā eva kevalena sat svarūpeṇa śuddhena adiśyate ātmā eva sarvatas  sarvam iti evam ekam ajam sarvatas  vyomavat pūrṇam anya śūnyam paśyan sa vā eṣa vidvān manana vijñānābhyām ātma ratiḥ ātmani eva ratī ramaṇam yasya saḥ  ayam ātma ratiḥ tathā ātma krīḍaḥ deha mātra sādhanā ratiḥ bāhya sādhanā krīḍā loke srībhiḥ sakhibhiḥ ca krīḍati iti darśanāt  na tathā viduṣaḥ kim tarhi ātma vijñāna nimittam eva ubhayam bhavati iti arthaḥ mithunam dvaṃndva janitam sukham tad api dvandva nirapekṣam yasya viduṣaḥ tathā ātma ānandaḥ śabda ādi nimitta ānandaḥ  aviduṣām na tathā asya viduṣaḥ kim tarhi ātma nimittam eva sarvam sarvadā sarva prakāreṇa ca deha jīvita bhoga ādi nimitta bāhya vastu nirapekṣa iti arthaḥ sa evaṃlakṣaṇaḥ  vidvān jīvan  eva svārājye abhiṣiktaḥ patite api dehe svarāj ā iva bhavati yata evam bhavati tatas  eva tasya sarveṣu lokeṣu kāma cāraḥ  bhavati prāṇa ādiṣu pūrva bhūmiṣu tatra asya iti tāvat mātra paricchinna kāma cāratva m ukta manrāja tvam ca artha prāptam sa atiśaya tvāt yathā prāpta svārājya kāma cāratva anuvādena tatat nivṛttiḥ iha ucyate sa svarāj iti ādinā atha punar ye anyathāta ukta darśanāt anyathā vaiparītyena yathā uktam eva vā samyak na viduḥ te anya rājānaḥ  bhavanti anyaḥ paraḥ  rājā svāmī yeṣām te anya rājānaḥ te kiñca kṣayyaḥ  lokaḥ  yeṣām te kṣayi lokāḥ bheda darśanasya alpa viṣaya tvāt alpam ca tad martyam iti avocāma tasmāt ye dvaita darśinaḥ te kṣayya lokāḥ sva darśana ānurūpyeṇa eva bhavantyata eva teṣām sarveṣu lokeṣu akāma cāraḥ  bhavati tasya ha vā etasya ityādi svārājyam prāptasya prakṛtasya viduṣa iti arthaḥ prāk sat ātma vijñānāt svātmanaḥ  anyasmāt sataḥ prāṇa ādeḥ nāma antasya utpatti pralayau  abhūtām sat ātma avijñāne tu sati idānīm sva ātmata eva saṃvṛttau tathā sarvaḥ  api anyaḥ  vyavahāra ātmataḥ  eva viduṣaḥ kiñca tad etasmin  artha eṣa ślokaḥ  mantraḥ  api bhavati na paśyaḥ paśyati iti paśyaḥ yathā ukta darśī vidvān iti arthaḥ mṛtyum maraṇam rogam jvara ādi duḥkha tām duḥkha bhāvam ca api na paśyati sarvam ha sarvam eva sa paśyaḥ paśyati ātmānam eva sarvam tatas  sarvam āpnoti sarvaśas  sarva prakāraiḥ iti kiñca sa vidvān prāc sṛṣṭi prabhedāt ekadhā eva bhavati ekadhā eva ca saṃsridha ādi bhedaiḥ ananta bheda prakāraḥ  bhavati sṛṣṭi kāle punar  saṃhāra kāle mūlam eva svam pārama arthakam ekadhā bhāvam pratipadyate svatantra eva iti vidyām phalena prarocayan stauti atha idānīm yathā uktāyāḥ  vidyāyāḥ samyak avabhāsa kāraṇam mukha avabhāsa kāraṇasya iva ādarśasya viśuddhi kāraṇam sādhanam upadiśyate āhāra śuddhau āhriyata iti āhāraḥ śabda ādi viṣaya vijñānam bhoktuḥ bhogāya āhriyate viśuddhi kāraṇam sādhanam upadiśyate āhāra śuddhau āhriyata iti āharaḥ śabda ādi viṣaya vijñānam bhoktuḥ bhogāya āhriyate tasya viṣaya upalabdhi lakṣaṇasya vijñānasya śuddhiḥ āhāra śuddhī rāga dveṣa moha doṣaiḥ asaṃsṛṣṭam viṣaya vijñānam iti arthaḥ tasyām āhāra aśuddhau satyām tadvataḥ  antaḥkaraṇasya sattvasya śuddhiḥ nairmalyam bhavati sattva śuddhau ca satyām yathā avagate bhūma ātmani dhruva avicchinnā smṛtiḥ avismaramam bhavati tasyām ca labdhāyām smṛti lambhe sati sarveṣām avidyā kṛta anartha pāśa rūpāṇām aneka janma antara anubhava bhāvanā kaṭhinīkṛtānām hṛdaya akṣayāṇām granthīnām vipramokṣaḥ  viśeṣeṇa pramokṣaṇam vināśaḥ  bhavati iti yata etad uttarottaram yathā uktam āhāra śuddhi mūlam tasmāt sā kāryā iti arthaḥ sarvam śāsra artham aśeṣata uktvā ākhyāyikām upasaṃharati śrutiḥ tasmai mṛdita kaṣāyāya vārkṣādiḥ iva kaṣāyaḥ  rāga dveṣa ādi doṣaḥ sattvasya rañjanā rūpa tvāt sa jñāna vairāgya abhyāsa rūpa kṣāreṇa kṣālitaḥ  mṛditaḥ  vināśitaḥ  yasya nāradasya tasmai yogyāya mṛdita kaṣāyāya tamasaḥ  avidyā lakṣaṇāt pāram parama artha tattvam darśayati darśitavān iti arthaḥ kaḥ  asau bhagavān utpattim pralayam ca eva bhūtānām āgatim gatim vetti vidyām avidyām ca sa vācyaḥ  bhagavān iti evandharmā sanatkumāraḥ tam eva sanatkumāram devam skanda iti ācakṣate kathayanti tad vidaḥ dvis vacanam adhyāya parisamāpti artham katham sarveṣu lokeṣu kāma cāraḥ  bhavati iti ucyate ya ātmānam yata ukta lakṣaṇam hṛdi sākṣātkṛtavān vakṣyamāṇa brahmacarya ādi sādhana saṃpannaḥ san  tad sthān  ca satyān kāmān sa tyakta dehaḥ  yadi pitṛ loka kāmaḥ pitaraḥ  janayitāraḥ ta eva sukha hetu tvena bhogya tvāt lokā ucyante teṣu kāmaḥ  yasya taiḥ pitṛbhiḥ saṃbandha icchā yasya bhavati tasya saṃkalpa mātrāt eva pitaraḥ samuttiṣṭhinti ātma saṃbandhi tām āpadyante viśuddha sattva tayā satya saṃkalpa tvāt īśvarasya iva tena pitṛ lokena bhogena saṃpannaḥ saṃpattiḥ iṣṭa prāptiḥ tayā samṛddhaḥ  mahīyate pūjyate vardhate vā mahimānam anubhavati samānam anyat  mātaraḥ  janayitryaḥ  atītāḥ sukha hetu bhūtāḥ sāmardhyāt  na hi duḥkha hetu bhūtāsu grāma sūkara ādi janma nimittāsu mātṛṣu viśuddha sattvasya yogina icchā tad saṃbandhaḥ  vā yuktaḥ yam yanamtam pradeśam abhikāmaḥ  bhavati yam ca kāmam kāmayate yathā ukta vyatirekeṇa api saḥ  asya antar  prāptum iṣṭaḥ kāmaḥ ca saṃkalpāt eva samuttiṣṭhati asya tena icchā vighāta tayā abhipreta artha prāptyā ca saṃpannaḥ  mahīyata iti ukta artham yathā ukta ātma dhyāna sādhana anuṣṭhānam prati sādhakānām utsāha janana artham anukrośanti āha kaṣṭam idam khalu vartate yad sva ātma sthāḥ śakya prāpyā api ta ime satyāḥ kāmā anṛta apidhānāḥ teṣām ātma sthānām sva āśrayāṇām eva satām anṛtam bahya viṣayeṣu strī anna bhojana ācchādana ādiṣu tṛṣṇā tad nimittam ca sva icchā pracāra tvam mithyājñāna nimitta tvāt anṛtam iti ucyate tad nimittam satyānām kāmānām aprāptiḥ iti apidhānam iva apidhānam katham anṛta apidhāna nimittam teṣām alābha iti ucyate yaḥ  yaḥ  hi yasmāt asya jantoḥ putraḥ  bhrātā veṣṭa itas  asmāt lokāt praiti pragacchati mriyate tam iṣṭam putram bhrātaram vā sva hṛdaya ākāśe vidyamānam api iha punar darśanāya icchan  api na labhate atha punar ye ca asya viduṣaḥ  jantoḥ jīvā jīvanti iha putrā bhrātrādayaḥ  vā ye ca pretā mṛtā iṣṭāḥ saṃbandhinaḥ  yad ca anyat iha loke vastra anna pāna ādi ratna ādi vā vastu icchat   labhate tad sarvam atra hṛdaya ākāśa ākhye brahmaṇi gatvā yathā uktena vidhinā vindate labhate atra asmin hārda ākāśe hi yasmāt asya ete yathā uktāḥ satyāḥ kāmā vartante anatā pidhānāḥ katham iva tad anyāyyam iti ucyate tad tatra yathā hiraṇyanidhim hiraṇyam eva punar grahaṇāya nidhātṛbhiḥ nidhīyata iti nidhiḥ tam hiraṇyanidhim nihitam bhūmeḥ adhastāt nikṣiptam akṣetra jñā nidhi śāsraiḥ nidhi kṣetram ajānantaḥ te nidheḥ upari upari saṃcarantaḥ  api nidhim na vindeyuḥ śakya vedanam api evam eva imā avidyavatyaḥ sarvā imāḥ prajā yathā uktam hṛdaya ākāśa ākhyam brahma lokam brahmā eva lokaḥ  brahma lokastam aharahar  pratyaham gacchantyaḥ  api suṣupta kāle na vidandanti na labhanta eṣaḥ  aham brahma loka bhāvam āpannaḥ  asmi adya iti anṛtena hi yathā uktena hi yasmāt pratyūḍhā hṛtāḥ sva rūpāt avidyā ādi doṣaiḥ bahipakṛṣṭā iti arthaḥ atas  kaṣṭam idam vartate jantūnām yad sva āyattam api brahma na labhyata iti abhiprāyaḥ sa vai ya ātma apahata pāpmā iti prakṛtaḥ  vaiśabdena tam smārayati eṣa vivakṣita ātmā hṛdi hṛdaya puṇḍarīka ākāśa śabdena abhihitaḥ tasya etasya hṛdayasya etad eva niruktam nirvacanam na anyata hṛdi ayam ātmā vartata iti yasmāt  tasmāt hṛdayam hṛdaya nāma nirvacana prasiddhyā api sva hṛdaya ātmā iti avagantavyam iti abhiprāyaḥ aharahar vai pratyaham evaṃvid hṛdyayam ātmā iti jānan svargam lokam hārdam brahma eti pratipadyate nanu anevaṃvid api suṣupta kāle hārdam brahma pratipadyata eva suṣupta kāle satā somya tadā saṃpanna iti ukta tvāt  bāḍham evam tathā api asti viśeṣaḥ yathā jānan  ajānan  ca sarvaḥ  jantuḥ sat brahmā eva tathā api tad tvam asi iti pratibodhitaḥ  vidvān sadeva na anyaḥ  asmi iti jānan sat eva bhavati evam eva vidvān avidvān  ca suṣupte yadi api sat saṃpadyate tathā api evaṃvid eva svargam lokam eti iti ucyate dehapāte api vidyā phalasya avaśyaṃbhāvi tvāt iti eṣa viśeṣaḥ suṣupta kāle svena āmanā satā saṃpannaḥ san samyak prasīdati iti jāgrat svapnayoḥ viṣaya indriya saṃyoga jātam kāluṣyam jahāti iti saṃprasāda śabdaḥ  yadi api sarva jantūnām sādhāraṇaḥ tathā api evaṃvid svargam lokam eti iti prakṛta tvāt eṣa saṃprasāda iti saṃnihitavat yatna viśeṣāt saḥ  atha idam śarīram hitvā asmāt śarīrāt samutthāya śarīra ātma bhāvanām parityajya iti arthaḥ na tu āsanāt iva samutthāya iti iha yuktam svena rūpeṇa iti viśeṣaṇāt  na hi anyata utthāya svarūpam saṃpattavyam svarūpam eva hi tad na bhavati pratipattavyam ced syāt  param paramātma lakṣaṇam vijñapti svabhāvam jyotiḥ upasaṃpadya svāsthyam upagamya iti etad  svena ātmīyena rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyate prāk etasyāḥ svarūpa saṃpatteḥ avidyayā deham eva aparam rūpam ātma tvena upagata iti tad apekṣayā it am ucyate svena rūpeṇa iti aśarīra tā hi ātmanaḥ svarūpam yad svam param jyotiḥ svarūpam āpadye saṃprasāda eṣa ātmā iti ha uvāca sa brūyāt iti yaḥ śrutyā niyuktaḥ  antevāsibhyaḥ kiñca etad amṛtam avināśi bhūmā yaḥ  vai bhūmā tad amṛtam iti uktam ata eva abhayam bhūmnaḥ dvitīya abhāvādata etad brahma iti tasya ha vā etasya brahmaṇaḥ  nāma abhidhānam kim tad satyam iti satyam hi avitatham brahma tad satyam sa ātmā iti hi uktam atha kimartham idam nāma punar ucyate tad upāsana vidhistuti artham tāni ha vā etāni trīṇi akṣarāṇi satīyam iti tad yad sattdamṛtam atha yad ti tad martyam atha yadyam tena ubhe yacchati yad anena ubhe yacchati tasmāt yam aharaharvā evaṃvid svargam lokam eti tāni ha vā etāni brahmaṇaḥ  nāma akṣarāṇi trīṇi etāni satīyāmati sa kārastakāraḥ  yam iti ca takāra īkāraḥ uccāraṇa arthaḥ  anubandhaḥ hrasvena eva akṣareṇa punar  pratinirdeśāt teṣām tad tatra yad sat sakāraḥ tad amṛtam sat brahma amṛta vācaka tvāt amṛta  eva sa kāra stakārantaḥ  nirdiṣṭaḥ atha yad titakāraḥ tad martyam atha yadyam akṣaram tena akṣareṇa amṛta martya ākhye pūrve ubhe akṣare yacchati yamayati niyamayati vaśīkaroti ātmana iti arthaḥ yadi asmāt anena yam iti etena ubhe yacchati tasmāt yām saṃyate iva hi etena yamā lakṣyete braṅma nāma akṣarasya api idam amṛtatva ādi dharmavat tvam mahābhāgyam kim uta nāmavata iti upāsya tvāya stūyate brahma nām nirvacanena eva nāmavataḥ  vettā evaṃvid  aharahar vā evaṃvid svargam lokam eti iti ukta artham atha ya ātmā iti ukta lakṣaṇaḥ  yaḥ saṃprasādaḥ tasya svarūpam vakṣyamāṇaiḥ uktaiḥ ca guṇaiḥ punar  stūyate brahmacarya sādhana saṃbandha artham ya eṣa yathā ukta lakṣaṇa ātmā sa setuḥ iva setuḥ vidhṛtiḥ vidharaṇaḥ anena hi sarvam jagat varṇa āśrama ādi kriyā kāraka phala ādi bheda niyamaiḥ kartuḥ anurūpam vidadhatā vidhṛtam adhriyamāṇam hi īśvareṇa idam viśvam vinaśyet yatas tasmāt sa setuḥ vidhṛtiḥ kimartham sa setuḥ iti āha eṣām bhūḥ ādīnām kartṛ karmala āśrayāṇām asaṃbhedāya avidāraṇāya avināśāya iti etad  kiṃviśṣṭaḥ ca asau setuḥ iti āha na etam setum ātmānam ahorātre sarvasya janimataḥ paricchedake satī na etam tarataḥ yathā anye saṃsāriṇaḥ kālena ahorātra ādi lakṣaṇena paricchedyā na tathā ayam kāla paricchedya iti abhiprāyaḥ yasmāt arvāk saṃvatsaraḥ  ahobhiḥ parivartata iti śruti antarāt ata eva enam na jarā tarati na prāpnoti tathā na mṛtyuḥ na śokaḥ  na sukṛtam na dṛṣkṛtam sukṛta duṣkṛte dharma adharmai prāptiḥ atra taraṇa śabdena abhipretā na atikramaṇam kāraṇam hi ātmā na śakyam hi kāraṇa atikramaṇam kartum kāryeṇa ahorātra ādi ca sarvam sataḥ kāryam anyena hi anyasya prāptiḥ atikramaṇam vā kriyeta na tu tena eva tasya na hi ghaṭena mṛd prāpyate atikramyate vā yadi api pūrvam ya ātma apahata pāpma ityādinā pāpma ādi pratiṣedha ukta eva tathā api ihāyam viśeṣaḥ  na tarati iti prāpti viṣaya tvam pratiṣidhyate tatra viśeṣeṇa jarā ādi abhāva mātram uktam ahorātra ādyā uktā anuktāḥ ca anye sarve pāpmāna ucyante atas  asmāt ātmanaḥ setoḥ nivartante aprāpya eva iti arthaḥ apahata pāpmā hi eṣa brahmā eva lokaḥ  brahma loke  uktaḥ yasmāt ca pāpma kārya māndhi ādi śarīravataḥ syāt na tu aśarīrasya tasmāt vā etam ātmānam setum tīrvā prāpya anandhaḥ  bhavati dehavat tve pūrvam andhaḥ api san tatā viddhaḥ sandehavat tve sa deha viyoge setum tīrtvā prāpya anandhaḥ  bhavati dehavat tve pūrvam andhaḥ api san tathā viddhaḥ sandehavat tve sa deha viyogaḥ  setum prāpya aviddhaḥ  bhavati tathā upatāpī roga ādi upatāpavān san  anupatāpī bhavati kiñca yasmāt ahorātre na staḥ setau tasmāt vā etam setum tīrtvā prāpya naktam api tamaḥ rūpam rātriḥ api sarvam ahar eva abhiniṣpadyate vijñapti ātma jyotiḥ sva rūpam ahar ivāhar  sadā eka rūpam viduṣaḥ saṃpadyata iti arthaḥ sakṛt vibhātaḥ sadā vibhātaḥ sadā eka rūpaḥ svena rūpeṇa eṣa brahma lokaḥ tad tatra evam sati etam yathā uktam brahma lokam brahmacaryeṇa srī viṣaya tṛṣṇā tyāgena śāsra ācārya upadeśam anuvindanti sva ātma saṃvedya tām āpādayanti ye teṣām eva brahmacarya sādhanavatām brahma vidām eṣa brahma lokaḥ na anyeṣām srī viṣaya saṃparka jāta tṛṣṇānām brahma vidām api iti arthaḥ teṣām sarveṣu lokeṣu kāma cāraḥ  bhavati iti ukta artham tasmāt paramam etad sādhanam brahmacaryam brahma vidām iti abhiprāyaḥ ya ātmā setutva ādi guṇaiḥ stutaḥ tad prāptaye jñāna sahakāri sādhana antaram brahmacarya ākhyam vidātavyam iti āha yajña ādibhiḥ ca tad stauti kartavyā artham atha yad yajña iti ācakṣate loke parama puruṣa artha sādhanam kathayanti śiṣṭāḥ tad brahmacaryam eva yajñasya api yad phalam tad brahmacaryavāllaṃbhate atas  yajñaḥ  api brahmacaryam bhavati pratipattavyam katham brahmacaryam yajña iti āha brahmacaryeṇa eva hi yasmāt yaḥ  jñātāsa tam brahma lokam yajñasya api pāramparyeṇa phala bhūtam vindate labhate tatas  yajñaḥ  api brahmacaryam eva iti yaḥ  jñāta iti akṣara anuvṛtteḥ yajñaḥ  brahmacaryam eva atha yad iṣṭam iti ācakṣate brahmacaryam eva tad  katham brahmacaryeṇa eva sādhanena tam īśvaram iṣṭvā pūjayitvā athavā eṣaṇām ātma viṣayām kṛtvā tam ātmānam anuvindate eṣaṇa ādiṣṭam api brahmacaryam eva atha yad sat trāyaṇam iti ācakṣate brahmacaryam eva tad tathā sataḥ parasmāt ātmana ātmanasrāṇam rakṣaṇam brahmacarya sādhanena vindate atas  sattrāyaṇa śabdam api brahmacaryam eva sat  atha yad maunam iti ācakṣate brahmacaryam eva tad brahmacaryeṇa eva sādhanena yuktaḥ san  ātmānam śāsra ācāryābhyām anuvidya paścāt manute dhyāyati atas  mauna śabdam api brahmacaryam eva atha yad anāśakāyanam iti ācakṣate brahmacaryam eva tad  yam ātmānam brahmacaryeṇa anuvindate sa eṣa hi ātmā brahmacarya sādhanavataḥ  na naśyati tasmāt anāśakāyanam api brahmacaryam eva atha yad araṇyāyanam iti ācakṣate brahmacaryam eva tad  araṇya śabdayoḥ arṇavayoḥ brahmacaryavataḥ  ayanāt araṇyāyanam brahmacaryam yaḥ  jñānāt yajña eṣaṇa ādiṣṭam satasrāṇāt sattrāyaṇam mananāt mauna manaśanāt anāśakāyanam araṇyayoḥ gamanāt araṇyāyanam ityādibhiḥ mahadbhiḥ puruṣa artha sādhanaiḥ stuta tvāt brahmacaryam paramam jñānasya sahakāri kāraṇam sādhanam iti atas brahma vidā yatnataḥ  rakṣaṇīyam iti arthaḥ tad tatra hi brahma loke araḥ ca ha vai prasiddhaḥ  ṇyaḥ ca arṇavau samudra upame vā sarasī tṛtīyasyām bhuvam antarikṣam ca apekṣya tṛtīyā dyauḥ tasyām tṛtīyasya amitas  asmāt lokāt ārabhya gaṇyamānāyām divi tad tatra eva cairamira annam tad maya airaḥ maṇḍaḥ tena pūrṇam airam madīyam tad upayoginām mada karam harṣa utpādakam saraḥ tatra eva ca aśvatthaḥ  vṛkṣaḥ soma savanaḥ nāmataḥ somaḥ  amṛtam tad niḥsravaḥ  amṛta srava iti vā tatra eva ca brahma loke brahmacarya sādhana rahitaiḥ brahmacarya sādhanavadbhyaḥ  anyaiḥ na jīyata iti aparājitā nāma pūḥ purī brahmaṇaḥ  hiraṇyagarbhasya brahmaṇā ca prabhuṇā viśeṣeṇa mitam nirmitam tad ca hiraṇmayam sauvarṇam prabhu vimitam maṇḍapam iti vākya śeṣaḥ tad tatra hi brahma loke  etau  arṇavau yāvaraṇī ākhyau  uktau brahmacaryeṇa sādhanena anuvindanti ye teṣām eva eṣa yaḥ  vyākhyātaḥ  brahma lokaḥ teṣām ca brahmacarya sādhava na tām brahma vidām sarveṣu lokeṣu kāma cāraḥ  bhavati na anyeṣa ām abrahmacarya parāṇām bāhya viṣaya āsakta buddhīnām kadācid api iti arthaḥ nanu atra tvam indraḥ tvam yamaḥ tvam varuṇa ityādibhiḥ yathā kaścid stūyate mahārha evam iṣṭa ādibhiḥ śabdaiḥ na strī ādi viṣaya tṛṣṇā nivṛtti mātram stuti arham kim tarhi jñānasya mokṣa sādhana tvāt tad eva iṣṭa ādibhiḥ stūyata iti kecid  na strī ādi bāhya viṣaya tṛṣṇā apahṛta cittānām pratyagātma viveka vijñāna anupapatteḥ parāñci khāni vyatṛṇat svayaṃbhūḥ tasmāt parāṅpaśyati na antarātman ityādi śruti smṛti śatebhyaḥ jñāna sahakāri kāraṇam strī ādi viṣaya tṛṣṇā nivṛtti sādhanam vidhātavyam eva iti yuktā eva tad stutiḥ nanu ca yajña ādibhiḥ stutam brahmacaryam iti yajña ādīnām puruṣa artha sādhana tvam gamyate satyam gamyate na tu iha brahma lokam prati yajña ādīnām sādhana tvam abhipretya yajña ādibhiḥ brahmacaryam stūyate kim tarhi teṣām prasiddham puruṣa artha sādhana tvam apekṣya yathā indra ādibhī rājā na tu yatra indra ādīnām vyāpāraḥ tatra eva rājña iti tadvat  ya imer aṇavādayaḥ  brāhma laukikāḥ saṃkalpa jāḥ ca pitṛ ādayaḥ  bhogāḥ te kim pārthivā āpyāḥ ca yathā iha loke dṛśyante tad had arṇava vṛkṣa pūḥ svarṇa maṇḍapāni āhosvid mānasa pratyaya mātrāṇi iti kiñcātas  yadi pārthivā āpyāḥ ca sthūlāḥ syuḥ hṛdi ākāśe samādhāna anupapattiḥ purāṇe ca manaḥ mayāni brahma loke śarīra ādīnī ti vākyam virudhyeta aśoka mahimam ityādyāḥ ca śrutayaḥ nanu samudrāḥ saritaḥ sarāṃsi vāpyaḥ kūpā yajñā vedā mantra ādayaḥ ca mūrtimantaḥ  brahmāṇam upatiṣṭhanta iti mānasa tvai virudhyeta purāṇa smṛtiḥ na mūrtimat tve prasiddha rūpāṇām eva tatra gamana anupapatteḥ tasmāt prasiddha mūrti vyatirekeṇa sāgara ādīnām mūrti antaram sāgara ādibhiḥ upāttam brahma loka gantṛ kalpanāyām yathāprasiddhā eva mānasya ākāravatyaḥ puṃstri ādyā mūrtayaḥ yuktāḥ kalpayitum mānasa deha ānurūpya saṃbandha upapatteḥ dṛṣṭā hi mānasya eva akāravatyaḥ puṃstri ādyā mūrtayaḥ svapne nanu tā anṛtā eva ta ime satyāḥ kāmā iti śrutiḥ tathā sati virudhyeta na mānasa pratyayasya sattva upapatteḥ mānasā hi pratyayāḥ srī puruṣa ādi ākārāḥ svapne dṛśyante nanu jāgrat vāsanā rūpāḥ svapna dṛśyā na tu tatra strī ādayaḥ svapne vidyante atyalpam idam ucyate jāgrat viṣayā api mānasa pratyaya abhinirvṛttā eva sa dīkṣā abhinirvṛtta tejaḥ  abanna maya tvāt jāgrat viṣayāṇām saṃkalpamūlā hi lokā iti ca uktam samakḷpatām dyāvāpṛthivī iti atra sarva śrutiṣu ca pratyak ātmana utpattiḥ pralayaḥ ca tatra eva sthitiḥ ca yathā vā arā nābhau ityādinā ucyate tasmāt mānasānām bāhyānām ca viṣayāṇām itaretara kārya kāraṇam iṣyata eva bīja aṅkuravat  yadi api bāhyā eva mānasā mānasā eva ca bāhyā na anṛta tvam teṣām kadācid api sva ātmani bhavati nanu svapne dṛṣṭāḥ pratibuddhasya anṛtā bhavanti viṣayāḥ satyam eva jāgrat bodha apekṣam tu tad anṛta tvam na svatas  tathā svapna bodha apekṣam ca jāgrat dṛṣṭa viṣaya anṛta tvam na svatas  viśeṣa ākāra mātram tu sarveṣām mithyā pratyaya nimittam iti vācā ārambhaṇam vikāraḥ  nāmadheyam anṛtam trīṇi rūpāṇi iti eva satyam tāni api ākāra viśeṣataḥ  anṛtam svatas  sat mātra rūpa tayā satyam prāc sat ātma pratibodhāt sva viṣaye api sarvam styam eva svapna dṛśyā iva iti na kaścid virodhaḥ tasmāt mānasā eva brāhma laukikā araṇya ādayaḥ pitṛ ādayaḥ kāmāḥ bāhya viṣaya bhogavat aśuddhi rahita tvāt śuddha sattva saṃkalpa janyā iti niratiśaya sukhāḥ satyāḥ ca īśvarāṇām bhavanti iti arthaḥ sat sati ātma pratibodhe api rajjvām iva kalpitāḥ sarpa ādayaḥ sat ātma svarūpa tām eva pratipadyanta iti sat ātmanā satyā eva bhavanti yaḥ tu hṛdaya puṇḍarīka gatam yathā ukta guṇa viśiṣṭam brahma brahmacarya ādi sādhana saṃpannaḥ tyakta bāhya viṣaya anṛta tṛṣṇaḥ san  upāste tasya iyam mūrdhanyayā nāḍyā gatiḥ vaktavyā iti nāḍīkhaṇḍa ārabhyate atha yā etā vakṣyamāṇā hṛdayasya puṇḍarīka ākārasya brahma upāsana sthānasya saṃbandhinyaḥ  nāḍyaḥ  hṛdaya māṃsa piṇḍāt sarvatas  viniḥsṛtā āditya maṇḍalāt iva raśmayaḥ tāḥ ca etāḥ piṅgalasya varṇa viśeṣa viśiṣṭasya aṇimnaḥ sūkṣma rasasya rasena pūrṇāḥ tad ākārā eva tiṣṭhanti vartanta iti arthaḥ tathā śuklasya nīlasya pītasya lohitasya ca rasasya pūrṇā iti sarvatra adhyāhāryam saureṇa tejasā pitta ākhyena pāka abhinirvṛttena kaphena alpena saṃparkāt piṅgalam bhavati sauram tejaḥ pitta ākhyām tad eva ca vāta bhūyastvāt nīlam bhavati tad eva ca kapha bhūyaḥ tvāt śuklam kaphena samatāyām pītam śoṇita bāhulyena lohitam vaidyakāt vā varṇa viśeṣā anveṣṭavyāḥ katham bhavanti iti śrutiḥ tu āha āditya saṃbandhāt eva tad tejasaḥ  nāḍīṣu anugatasya ete varṇa viśeṣā iti katham asau vā ādityaḥ piṅgalaḥ  varṇata eṣa ādityaḥ śuklaḥ  api eṣa nīla eṣa pīta eṣa lohita āditya eva tasya adhyātmam nāḍībhiḥ katham saṃbandha iti atra dṛṣṭāntam āha tad tatra yathā loke mahān vistīrṇaḥ panthā mahāpatha ātataḥ vyāpta ubhau gacchati imam ca saṃnihitam amum ca viprakṛṣṭam dūra stham evam yathā dṛṣṭāntaḥ  mahāpatha ubhau grāmau praviṣṭa evam eva etā ādityasya raśmaya ubhau lokau  amum ca āditya maṇḍalam imam ca puruṣam gacchanti ubhayatra praviṣṭāḥ yathā mahāpathaḥ katham amuṣmādāditya maṇḍalāt pratāyante saṃtatā bhavanti tā adhyātmam āsu piṅgala ādi varṇāsu yathā uktāsu nāḍīṣu sṛptā gatāḥ praviṣṭā iti arthaḥ ābhyaḥ  nāḍībhyaḥ pratāyante pravṛttāḥ santāna bhūtāḥ satyaḥ te amuṣmin raśmīnām ubhaya liṅga tvāt ta iti ucyante tad tatra evam sati yatra yasmin kāla etad svapana mayam jīvaḥ suptaḥ  bhavati svāpasya dvi prakāra tvāt viśeṣaṇam samasta iti upasaṃhṛta sarva karaṇa vṛttiḥ iti etad  atas  bāhya viṣaya saṃparka janita kāluṣya abhāvāt samyak prasannaḥ saṃprasannaḥ  bhavati ata eva svapnam viṣaya ākāra ābhāsam mānasam svapna pratyayam na vijānāti na anubhavati iti arthaḥ yadā evam suptaḥ  bhavati āsu saura tejaḥ pūrṇāsu yathā uktāsu nāḍīṣu tadā sṛptaḥ praviṣṭaḥ  nāḍībhiḥ dvāra bhūtābhiḥ hṛdaya ākāśam gataḥ  bhavati iti arthaḥ na hi anyatra sat saṃpatteḥ svapna adarśanam asti iti sāmarthyāt nāḍīṣu iti saptamī tṛtīyayā pariṇamyate tam satā saṃpannam na kaścana na kaścid api dharma adharma rūpaḥ pāpmā spṛśati iti svarūpa avasthita tvāt tad ātmanaḥ deha indriya viśiṣṭam hi sukha duḥkha kārya pradānena pāpmā spṛśati iti na tu sat saṃpannam svarūpa avastham kaścid api pāpmā spraṣṭum utsahate aviṣaya tvāt  anyaḥ  hi anyasya viṣayaḥ  bhavati na tu anya tvam kenacid kutaścid api sat saṃpannasya svarūpa pracyavanam tu ātmanaḥ  jāgrat svapna avasthām prati gamanam bāhya viṣaya pratibodhaḥ  avidyā kāma karma bījasya brahma vidyā hutāśā dāha nimittam iti avocāma ṣaṣṭha eva tad iha api pratyetavyam yadā evam suptaḥ saureṇa tejasā hi nāḍī antargatena sarvatas  saṃpannaḥ  vyāptaḥ  bhavati atas  viśeṣeṇa cakṣuḥ ādi nāḍī dvāraiḥ bāhya viṣaya bhogāya aprasṛtāni karaṇāni asya tadā bhavanti tasmāt ayam karaṇānām nirodhāt svātmani eva avasthitaḥ svapnam na vijānāti iti yuktam tatra evam sati atha yatra yasmin kāle abali mānam abala bhāvam dehasya roga ādi nimittam jarā ādi nimittam vā kṛśībhāvam etad nayanam nītaḥ prāpitaḥ  devadattaḥ  bhavati mumūrṣarya dā bhavati iti arthaḥ tam abhitas  sarvatas  veṣṭayitvā āsīnā jñātaya āhuḥ jānāsi mām tava putram jānāsi mām pitaram ca ityādi sa mumūrṣuḥ yāvat asmāt śarīrāt an utkrāntaḥ  anirgataḥ  bhavati tāvat putra ādīn jānāti atha yatra yadā etad kriyā viśeṣaṇam iti asmāt śarīrāt utkrāmati atha tadā etaiḥ eva yathā uktābhiḥ  raśmibhiḥ ūrdhvam ākramate yathā karma arjitam lokam pratyavidvān itaraḥ tu vidvān yathā ukta sādhana saṃpannaḥ sa om iti uṅkāreṇa ātmānam dhyāyan yathāpūrvam vā ha eva udva ūrdhvam vā vidvān  ceditaraḥ tiryaṅva iti abhiprāyaḥ mīyate pramīyate gacchati iti arthaḥ sa vidvān utkramiṣyan yāvat kṣipyet manaḥ  yāvatā kālena manasaḥ kṣepaḥ syāt tāvatā kālena ādityam gacchati prapnoti kṣipram gacchati iti arthaḥ  na tu tāvatā eva kālena iti vivakṣitam kimartham ādityam gacchati iti ucyate etad vai khalu prasiddham brahma lokasya dvāram ya ādityaḥ tena dvāra bhūtena brahma loke  gacchati vidvān atas  viduṣām prapadanam prapadyate brahma lokam anena dvāreṇa iti prapadanam nirodhanam nirodhaḥ  asmāt āditi ādaviduṣām bhavati iti nirodhaḥ saureṇa tejasā deha eva niruddhāḥ santaḥ  mūrdhanyayā nāḍyā na utkramanta eva iti arthaḥ viṣvaṅṅanyā iti ślokāt  tad etasmin i athā ukter atha eṣa ślokaḥ  mantraḥ  bhavati śatam ca ekā ca eka uttara śatam nāḍyaḥ  hṛdayasya māṃsa piṇḍa bhūtasya saṃbandhinyaḥ pradhānataḥ bhavanti ānantyāt deha nāḍīnām tāsām ekā mūrdhānam abhiniḥsṛtā vinirgatā tayā ūrdhvamāyan ga  chan  amṛta tvam amṛta bhāvam eti viṣvak na anāgatayaḥ tiryak visarpiṇya ūrdhva gāḥ ca anyā nāḍyaḥ  bhavanti saṃsāra gamana dvāra bhūtā na tu amṛta tvāya kim tarhyat kamaṇa eva utkrānti artham eva bhavanti iti arthaḥ dvis abhyāsaḥ prakaraṇa samāpti arthaḥ atha ya eṣa saṃprasādaḥ  asmāt śarīrāt samutthāya param jyotiḥ upasaṃpadya svena rūpeṇa abhiniṣpadyata eṣa ātmā iti ha uvāca etad amṛtam abhayam etad brahma iti uktam tatra kaḥ  asau saṃprasādaḥ katham vā tasya adhigamaḥ  yathā saḥ  asmāt śarīrāt sa vijijñāsitavya iti ca eṣa niyama vidhiḥ eva na apūrva vidhiḥ evam anveṣṭa vyaḥ  vijijñāsitavya iti arthaḥ dṛṣṭa artha tvāt anveṣaṇa vijijñāsanayoḥ dṛṣṭa artha tvam ca darśayiṣyati na aha mātra bhogyam paśyāmi iti anena asakṛt  para rūpeṇa ca deha ādi dharbhaiḥ avaganyamānasya ātmanaḥ sva rūpa adhigame viparīta adhigama nivṛttiḥ dṛṣṭam phalam iti niyama artha tā eva asya vidheḥ yuktā na tvā agni hotra ādīnāmi bā pūrva vidhi tvam iha saṃbhavati tad ha ubhaya iti ādya ākhyāyikā prayojanam uktam tad ha kila prajāpateḥ vacanam ubhaye deva asurā devāḥ ca asurāḥ ca deva asurā anu paramparā gatam sva karṇa gocara āpannam anububudhire anubuddhavantaḥ te ca etad prajāpati vacaḥ  buddhvā kim akurvan  iti ucyate te ha ūcuḥ uktavantaḥ  anyonyam devāḥ sva pariṣadya surāḥ ca hanta yadi anumatiḥ bhavatām prajāpatinā uktam tam ātmānam anvicchāmaḥ  anveṣaṇam kurmaḥ  yam ātmānam anviṣya sarvān  ca lokān āpnoti sarvāḥ ca kāmān iti uktvā indraḥ  ha eva rājā eva svayam devānām itarān devān  ca bhoga paricchadam ca sarvam sthāpayitvā śarīra mātreṇa eva prajāpatim pratyabhipravavrāja pragatavān  tathā virocanaḥ  asurāṇām vinayena guravaḥ  abhigantavyā iti etad darśayati trailokya rājyāt ca gurutarā vidyate yatas  devāsura rājau mahārha bhoga arhai santau tathā gurum abhyupagatavantau tau ha kila asaṃvidānau  eva anyonyam saṃvidam akurvāṇau vidyā phalam pratyanyonyam īrṣyām darśayantau samidh pāṇī samidh bhāra hastau prajāpati sakāśam ājagma tuḥ āgatavantau tau ha gatvā dvātriṃśatam varṣāṇi śuśrūṣā parau bhūtvā brahmacarya mūṣa tuḥ uṣitavantau abhiprāya jñaḥ prajāpatiḥ tau  uvāca kim icchantau kim prayojanam abhipretya icchantau  avāstamuṣitavantau yuvām iti iti uktau tau ha ūcatuḥ ya ātmā ityādi bhagavataḥ  vacaḥ  vedayante śiṣṭā atas tam ātmānam jñātum icchantau  avāstam iti yadi api prāc prajāpateḥ samīpa āgamanāt anyonyam īrṣyā yukta avabūtām tathā api vidyā prāpti prayojana gauravāt tyakta rāga dveṣa moha īrṣyā ādi doṣau  eva bhūtvā ūṣatuḥ brahmacaryam prajāpatau tena idam prakhyāpitam ātma vidyā gauravam tau  evam tapasvinau śuddha kalmaṣau yogyau  upalabhya prajāpatiḥ uvācaha ya eṣaḥ  akṣiṇi puruṣaḥ  nivṛtta cakṣurbhiḥ mṛdita kaṣāyaiḥ dṛśyate yogibhiḥ draṣṭā eṣa ātma apahata pāpma ādi guṇa u yam avocam purā aham yad vijñānāt sarva loka kāma avāptiḥ etad amṛtam bhama ākhyam ata eva abhayam ata eva brahma vṛddhatamam iti atha etad prajāpatinā uktam akṣiṇi puruṣaḥ  dṛśyata iti vacaḥ śrutvā chāyā rūpam puruṣam jagṛhatuḥ gṛhītvā ca dṛḍhīkaraṇāya prajāpatim pṛṣṭavantau atha yaḥ  ayam he bhagavaḥ  apsu parikhyāyate parisamantāt jñāyate yaḥ ca ayam ādarśa ātmanaḥ pratibimba ākāraḥ parikhyāyate khaḍga ādau ca katama eṣa eṣām bhagavadbhiḥ uktaḥ kiṃva eka eva sarveṣu iti evam pṛṣṭaḥ prajāpatiḥ uvāca eṣa u eva yaḥ cakṣuṣi draṣṭā mayā ukta iti etad manasi kṛtvā eṣu sarveṣu anteṣu madhyeṣu parikhyāyata iti ha uvāca nanu katham yuktam śiṣyoḥ viparīta grahaṇam anujñātum prajāpateḥ vigata doṣasya ācāryasya sataḥ satyam eva na anujñātam katham ātmani adhyāropita pāṇḍitya mahattva boddhṛ tvau hi indra virocanau tathā eva ca prathitau loke tau yadi prajāpatinā mūḍhau yuvām viparīta grāhiṇau  iti uktau syātām tatas taḥ tayoḥ citte duḥkham syāt tad janitāt ca citta avasādāt punar  praśna śravaṇa grahaṇa avadhāraṇam pratyutsāha vidhātaḥ syāt atas  rakṣaṇīyau śiṣyau  iti manyate prajāpatiḥ gṛhṇītām tāvat tad udaśarāva dṛṣṭāntena apaneṣyāmi iti ca nanu na yuktam eṣa u eva iti anṛtam vaktum na ca anṛtam uktam katham ātmanā uktaḥ  akṣi puruṣaḥ  manasi saṃnihitataraḥ śiṣya gṛhītācchāyā ātmanaḥ sarveṣām ca abhyantaraḥ sarva antaraḥ iti śruteḥ tam eva avocat eṣa u eva iti atas  na anṛtam uktam prajāpatinā tathā ca tayoḥ viparīta grahaṇa nivṛtti artham hi āha udaśarāva udaka pūrṇe śarāvādau  ātmānam avekṣya anantaram yad tatra ātmānam paśyantau na vijānīthaḥ tad me mama prabrūtam ācakṣīya athām iti uktau tau ha tathā eva udaśarāve avekṣāñcakrāte avekṣaṇam cakratuḥ tathā kṛtavantau tau ha prajāpatiḥ uvāca kim paśyatha iti nanu tad me prabrūtam iti uktābhyām udaśarāve avekṣaṇam kṛtvā prajāpataye na niveditam idam āvābhyām na viditam iti anivedite ca ajñāna hetau ha prajāpatiḥ uvāca kim paśyatha iti tatra kaḥ  abhiprāya iti ucyate na eva tayoḥ idam āvayoḥ aviditam iti āśaṅkā bhūt chāyā ātmani ātma pratyayaḥ niścita eva āsīt  yena vakṣyati tau ha śānta hṛdayau pravavrajatuḥ iti na hi aniścite abhipreta arthe praśānta hṛdaya tvam upapadyate tena na ūcatur idam āvābhyām aviditam iti viparīta grāhiṇau ca śiṣyau  anupekṣaṇīyau  iti svayam eṣa papraccha kim paśyatha iti viparīta niścaya apanayāya ca vakṣyati sādhu ala kṛtau  iti evamādi tau ha ūcatuḥ sarvam eva idam āvām bhagava ātmānam paśyāva ā lomabhya ā nakhebhyaḥ pratirūpam iti yathā eva āvām he bhagavaḥ  loma nakha ādimantau sva  evam eva idam loma nakha ādi sahitam āvayoḥ pratirūpam udaśarāve paśyāva iti tau ha punar  prajāpatiḥ uvāca cchāyā ātma niścaya apanayāya sādhu alaṅkṛtau yathā sva gṛhe su vasanau mahārha vastra paridhānau pariṣkṛtau chinna loma nakhau ca bhūtvā uda śarāve tayoḥ chāyā ātma grahaḥ  apanītaḥ syāt  sādhu alaṅkāra su vasana ādīnām āgantukānām chāyākara tvam udaśarāve yathā śarīra saṃbaddhānām evam śarīrasya api cchāyākara tvam pūrvam babhūva iti gamyate śarīra eka deśānām ca loma nakha ādīnām nitya tvena abhipretānām akhaṇḍitānām chāyā kara tvam pūrvam āsīt  chinneṣu ca teṣu na eva loma nakhāt icchāyā dṛśyate atas  loma nakha ādivat śarīrasya api āgama apāyi tvam siddham iti udaśarauvādau dṛśyamānasya tad nimittasya ca dehasya anātma tvam siddham uda śārāva ādau chāyā kara tvāt deha saṃbaddha alaṅkāra ādivat  na kevalam etāvat etena yāvat kiñcid ātmīyatva abhimatam sukha duḥkha rāga dveṣa moha ādi ca kādācitka tvāt nakha loma ādivat ana ātmā iti pratyetavyam evam aśeṣa mithyā graha apanaya nimitte sādhu alaṅkāra ādi dṛṣṭānte prajāpatinā ukte śrutvā tathā kṛtavatoḥ api cchāyā ātma viparīta grahaḥ  na apajagāma yasmāt tasmāt sva doṣeṇa eva kenacid pratibaddha viveka vijñānau  indra virocanau  abhūtām it i gamyate tau pūrvavat eva dṛḍha niścayau papraccha kim paśyatha iti tau tathā eva pratipannaḥ  yathā eva idam iti pūrvavat yathā sādhu alaṅkāra ādi viśiṣṭau  āvām sva  evam eva imau chāyā ātmānau  iti sutarām viparīta niścayau babhūvatuḥ yasya ātmanaḥ  lakṣaṇam ya ātma apahata pāpmā iti uktavā punar tad viśeṣam anviṣyamāṇayoḥ ya eṣaḥ  akṣiṇi puruṣaḥ  dṛśyata iti sākṣāt ātmani nirdiṣṭe tad viparīta graha apanayāyodaśa rāva sā dhu alaṅkāra dṛṣṭānte api abhihita ātma svarūpa bodhāt viparīta grahaḥ  na apagataḥ atas  sva doṣeṇa kenacid pratibaddha viveka vijñāna sāmarthyau  iti matvā yathā abhipretam eva ātmānam manasi nidhāya eṣa ātmā iti ha uvāca etad amṛtam abhayam etad brahma iti prajāpatiḥ pūrvavat  na tu tad abhipretam ātmānam ya ātmā iti ādi ātma lakṣaṇa śravaṇena akṣi puruṣa śrutyā coda śarāva ādi upapattyā ca saṃskṛtau tāvat  mad vacanam sarvam punar  punar  smaratoḥ pratibandha kṣayāt ca svayam eva ātma viṣaye vivekaḥ  bhaviṣyati iti manvānaḥ punar brahmacarya ādeśe ca tayoḥ citta dukha utpattim parijihīrṣan kṛta artha buddhi tayā gacchantau  api upekṣitavān prajāpatiḥ tau ha indra virocanau śānta hṛdayau tuṣṭa hṛdayau kṛtārtha buddhī iti arthaḥ na tu śama eva śamaḥ ced tayoḥ jātaḥ  viparīta grahaḥ  vigataḥ  abhaviṣyat pravavrajatuḥ gatavantau evam tayoḥ gatayoḥ indra virocana yaḥ rājñoḥ bhoga āsaktayoḥ yathā ukta vismaraṇam syāt iti āśaṅkya apratyakṣam pratyakṣa vacanena ca citta duḥkham parijihīrṣuḥ tau dūram gacchan tau  anvīkṣya ya ātma apahata pāpma ityādi vacanavat etad api anayoḥ śravaṇa gocara tvam eṣyati iti matvā uvāca prajāpatiḥ anupalabhya yathā ukta lakṣaṇam ātmānam ananuvidya sva ātma pratyakṣam ca akṛtvā viparīta niścayau ca bhūtvā indra virocanau  etau vrajataḥ  gaccheyātām atas  yatare devāḥ  vā asurā vā kim viśeṣitena etad upaniṣada ābhyām yā gṛhīta ātma vidyā sā iyam upaniṣadyeṣām devānām asurāṇām vā ta etad upaniṣada evaṃvijñānā etad niścayā bhaviṣyanti iti arthaḥ te kim parābhaviṣyanti śreyaḥ mārgāt parābhūtā bahis bhūtā vinaṣṭā bhaviṣyanti iti arthaḥ sva gṛham gacchatoḥ sura asura rājayoḥ yaḥ  asura rājaḥ sa ha śānta hṛdaya eva san virocanaḥ  asurān jagāma gatvā ca tebhyaḥ  asurebhyaḥ śarīra ātma buddhiḥ yā upaniṣattām etām upaniṣadam provāca uktavān deha mātram eva ātmā pitrā ukta iti tasmāt ātmā eva deha iha loka mahayyaḥ pūjanīyaḥ tathā paricaryaḥ paricaraṇīyaḥ tathā ātmānam eva iha loke deham mahayan paricaran  ca ubhau lokau  avāpnoti imam ca amum ca ihaloka para lokayoḥ eva sarve lokāḥ kāmāḥ ca antarbhavanti iti rājñaḥ  abhiprāyaḥ tasmāt tad saṃpradāyaḥ  adya api anuvartata iti iha loke adadānam dāna m akurvāṇam avibhāga śīlam aśraddadhānam satkāryeṣu śraddhā rahitam yathāśakti ayajamānam aya jana svabhāvam āhuḥ āsuraḥ khalu ayam yata evaṃsvabhāvaḥ  bata iti khidyamānā āhuḥ śiṣṭāḥ asurāṇām hi yasmāt aśraddadhāna tā ādi lakṣaṇa eṣā upaniṣad  tayā upaniṣadā saṃskṛtāḥ santaḥ pretasya śarīram kuṇapam bhikṣayā gandha mālya anna ādi lakṣaṇayā vasanena vasra ādinā ācchādana ādi prakāreṇa alaṅkāreṇa dhvaja patākā ādi karaṇena iti evam saṃskurvanti etena kuṇapa saṃskāreṇa amum pretya pratipattavyam lokam jeṣyantaḥ  manyante atha ha kila indraḥ  aprāpya eva devān daivya akraurya ādi saṃpadā yukta tvāt guroḥ vacanam punar  punar  smaran  eva gacchan  etad vakṣyamāṇam bhayam sva ātma grahaṇa nimittam dadarśa dṛṣṭavān udaśara avadṛṣṭāntena prajāpatinā yad arthaḥ  nyāya uktaḥ tad eka deśaḥ  maghavataḥ pratyabhāt buddhau yena cchāyā ātma grahaṇe doṣam dadarśa katham yathā eva khalu ayam asmin śarīre sādhu alaṅkṛte chāyā ātmā api sādhu alaṅkṛtaḥ  bhavati su vasane ca su vasanaḥ pariṣkṛte pariṣkṛtaḥ  yathā nakha loma ādi deha avayava apagame chāyā ātmā api pariṣkṛtaḥ  bhavati nakha loma ādi rahitaḥ  bhavati evam eva ayam chāyā ātmā api asmin śarīre nakha loma ādibhiḥ deha avayava tvasya tulya tvāt andhe cakṣuṣaḥ  apagame andhaḥ bavati srāme srāmaḥ srāmaḥ kileka netraḥ tasya andha tvena gata tvāt  cakṣuḥ nāsikā vā yasya sadā sravati sa srāmaḥ parivṛkṇaḥ chinna hastaḥ chinna pādaḥ  vā srāme parivṛkṇe vā dehe chāyā ātmā api tathā bhavati tathā asya dehasya nāśam anveṣa naśyati atas  na aham atra asmin  chāyā ātma darśane deha ātma darśane vā bhogyam phalam paśyāmi iti evam doṣam deha  chāyā ātma darśane adhyavasya sa samidh pāṇiḥ brahmacaryam vastum punar eyāya tam ha prajāpatiḥ uvāca magha vanyat śānta hṛdayaḥ prāvrājīḥ pragatavān asi virocanena sārdham kim icchan punar āgama iti vijānan  api punar  papraccha indra abhiprayā abhivyaktaye yad vettha tena mā upasīda iti yadvat  tathā ca sva abhiprayām prakaṭam akarot yathā eva khalu ayam ityadi evam eva iti ca anvamodata prajāpatiḥ nanu tulye akṣi puruṣaśravame deha  chāyām indraḥ  agrahīt ātmā iti deham eva va virocanaḥ tad kiṃnimittam tatra manyate yathā indrasya uda śarā  ādi prajāpati vacanam smarataḥ  devān aprāptasya eva ācārya ukta buddhyā chāyā ātma grahaṇam tatra doṣa darśanam ca abhūt  na tathā virocanasya kim tarhi deha eva ātma darśanam na api tatra doṣa darśanam babhūva tadvat eva vidyā grahaṇa sāmarthya pratibandha doṣa alpatva bahutva apekṣam indra virocanayoḥ chāyā ātma dehayoḥ grahaṇam indraḥ  alpa doṣa tvāt dṛśyata itiśruti artham eva śraddadhāna tayā jagrāha itaraḥ chāyā nimittam deham hitvā śruti artham lakṣaṇayā jagrāha prajāpatinā uktaḥ  ayam iti doṣa bhūyaḥ tvāt yathā kila nīla ānīlayoḥ ādarśe dṛśyamānayoḥ vāsasoḥ yad nīlam tad mahārham ya ātma apahata pāpma ādi lakṣaṇaḥ  ya eṣaḥ  akṣiṇī ityādinā vyākhyāta eṣa saḥ kaḥ  asau yaḥ svapne mahīyamānaḥ strī ādibhiḥ pūjyamānaḥ carati anekavidhān svapna bhogān anubhavati iti arthaḥ eṣa ātmā iti ha uvāca ityādi samānam sa ha evam ukta indraḥ śānta hṛdayaḥ pravavrāja sa ha aprāpya eva devān pūrvavat asmin  api ātmani bhayam dadarśa katham tad idam śarīram yadi api andham dhavati svapna ātmā yaḥ  anandhaḥ sa bhavati yadi srāmam idam śarīram
