asrāmaḥ ca sa bhavati na eva eṣa svapna ātmā asya dehasya doṣeṇa duṣyati na api asya vadhena sa hanyate chāyā ātmavat na ca asya srāmyeṇa srāmaḥ svapna ātmā bhavati yad adhyāya ādau  āgama mātreṇa upanyastam na asya jarayā etad jīryati ityādi tad iha nyāyena upapādayitum upanyastam na tāvat ayam chāyā ātmavat deha doṣa yuktaḥ kintu dhnanti tu eva enam eva śabda iva arthe ghnanti iva enam kecana iti draṣṭavyam prajāpatim pramāṇīkurvataḥ  anṛta vāditva āpādana anupapatteḥ etad amṛtam iti etad prajāpati vacanam katham mṛṣā kuryāt indraḥ tam pramāṇīkurvan nanu cchāyā puruṣe prajāpatinā ukte asya śarīrasya nāśam anveṣa naśyati iti doṣam abhyadhāt tathā iha api syāt  na evam kasmāt  ya eṣaḥ  akṣiṇi puruṣaḥ  dṛśyata iti manyate tadā katham prajāpatim pramāṇīkṛtya punar  śravaṇāya samidh pāṇiḥ gacchet  jagāma ca tasmāt na cchāyā ātmā prajāpatinā ukta iti manyate tathā ca vyākhyātam draṣṭākṣiṇi dṛśyata iti tathā vicchādayantī iva vidrāvayanti iva tathā ca putra ādi maraṇa nimittam apriyavettā iva bhavati api ca svayam api roditi iva nanu apriyam vetti eva katham vettā iva iti ucyate na amṛta abhayatva vacana anupapatteḥ dhyāyati iva iti ca śruti antarāt nanu pratyakṣa virodha iti ced  na śarīra ātmatva pratyakṣavat bhrānti saṃbhavāt tiṣṭhatu tāvat apriya vettā iva na vā iti na aham atra bhogyam paśyāmi svapna ātma jñāne api iṣṭam phalam na upalabha iti abhiprāyaḥ evam eva eṣa tava abhiprāyeṇa iti vākya seṣaḥ ātmanaḥ  amṛta abhaya guṇavat tvasya abhipreta tvāt dvis uktam api nyāyataḥ  mayā yathāvat na avadhārayati tasmāt pūrvavat asya adya api pratibandha kāraṇam asti iti manvānaḥ tad kṣapaṇāya vasā parāṇi dvātriṃśatam varṣāṇi brahmacaryam iti ādideśa prajāpatiḥ tathā uṣitavate kṣapita kalmaṣāya āha pūrvavat etam tu eva ta iti ādi uktvā tad yatra etad supta ityadi vyākhyātam vākyam akṣiṇi yaḥ  draṣṭā svapne ca mahīyamānaḥ carati sa eṣa suptaḥ samastaḥ saṃprasannaḥ svapnam na vijānāti eṣa ātmā iti ha uvāca etad amṛtam abhayam etad brahma iti sva abhipretam eva maghavān  tatra api doṣam dadarśa katham na āha na eva suṣupta sthaḥ  api ātmā khalu ayam saṃprati samyak idānīm ca ātmānam jānāti na evam jānāti katham ayam aham asmi iti naḥ eva imāni bhūtāni ca iti yathā jāgrati svapne vā atas  vināśam eva vināśam iva iti pūrvavat draṣṭavyam api ita u api gataḥ  bhavati vinaṣṭa iva bhavati iti abhiprāyaḥ jñāne hi sati jñātuḥ sadbhāvaḥ  avagamyate na asati jñāne na ca suṣuptasya jñānam dṛśyate atas  vinaṣṭa iva iti abhiprāyaḥ na tu vināśam eva ātmanaḥ  manyate amṛta abhaya vacanasya prāmāṇyam icchan pūrvavat evam eva iti uktvā yaḥ  mayā ukta sribhiḥ paryāyaiḥ tam eva etam naḥ eva anyatra etasmāt ātmanaḥ  anyam kañcana kim tarhi etam eva vyākhyāsyāmi su alpaḥ tu doṣaḥ tava avaśiṣṭaḥ tad kṣapaṇāya vasā parāṇi anyāni pañca varṣāṇi iti uktaḥ sa tathā cakāra tasmai mṛdita kaṣāya ādi doṣāya sthāna traya doṣa saṃbandha rahitam ātmanaḥ svarūpam apahata pāpmatva ādi lakṣaṇam maghavate tasmai ha uvāca tāni eka śatam varṣāṇi saṃpeduḥ saṃpannāni babhūvuḥ yad āhuḥ loke śiṣṭā eka śatam ha vai varṣāṇi maghavān prajāpatau brahmacaryam uvāsa iti tad etad dvātriṃśatam ityādinā darśitam iti ākhyāyikātaḥ  apasṛtya śrutyā ucyate evam kila etad indra tvāt api gurutaram indreṇa api mahatā yatnena eka uttara varṣa śata kṛta āyāsena prāptam ātma jñānam atas  na atas  param puruṣa artha antaram asti iti ātma jñānam stauti maghavat martyam vai maraṇa dharmī idam śarīram yad manyase akṣi ādhāra ādi lakṣaṇaḥ saṃprasāda lakṣaṇa ātmā mayā uktaḥ  vināśam eva apītaḥ  bhavati iti śṛṇu tatra kāraṇam yad idam śarīram vai tad etad martyam vināśi tad ca attam mṛtyunā grastam satatam eva kadācid eva mriyata iti martyam iti ukte na tathā saṃtrāsaḥ  bhavati yathā grastam eva sadā vyāptam eva mṛtyunā iti ukta iti vairāgya artham viśeṣa iti ucyata āttam mṛtyunā iti katham nāma deha abhimānataḥ  viraktaḥ sannivartata iti śarīram iti atra saha indriya manobhiḥ ucyate tad śarīram asya saṃprasādasya tri sthāna tayā gamyamānasya amṛtasya maraṇa ādi dehandriya manaḥ dharma varjitasya iti etad  amṛtasya iti anena eva aśarīra tve siddhe punar aśarīrasya iti vacanam vāyu ādivat sāvayavatva mūrtimat tve mā bhūtām iti ātmanaḥ ātmanaḥ  vā sata īkṣituḥ tejaḥ banna ādi krameṇa utpannam adhiṣṭhānam jīva rūpeṇa praviśya sa deva adhitiṣṭhati asmin  iti vā adhiṣṭhānam yasya idam īdṛśam nityam eva mṛtyu grastam dharma adharma janita tvāt priya apriyavat adhiṣṭhānam tad adhiṣṭhitaḥ tad vā ansa śarīraḥ  bhavati aśarīra svabhāvasya ātmanaḥ tad eva aham śarīram śarīram eva ca aham iti avivekāt ātma bhāvaḥ sa śarīra tvam ata eva sa śarīraḥ sannāttaḥ  grastaḥ priya apriyābhyām prasiddham etad  tasya ca na vai sa śarīrasya sataḥ priya apriyayoḥ bāhya viṣaya saṃyoga viyoga nimittayoḥ bāhya viṣaya saṃyoga viyogau mama iti manyamānasya apahatiḥ vināśa ucchedaḥ santati rūpayoḥ na asti iti tam punar deha abhimānāt aśarīra sva rūpa vijñānena vinartitau  iveka jñāna śarīram santam priya apriye na spṛśataḥ spṛśiḥ pratyekam saṃbadhyata iti priyam na spṛśati apriyam na spṛśati iti vākya dvayam bhavati na mleccha aśuci adhārmikaiḥ saha saṃbhāṣete ti yadvat  dharma adharma kārye hi te aśarīra tā tu svarūpam iti tatra dharma adharmayoḥ asaṃbhavāt tad kārya bhāvaḥ  dūrata eva iti atas  na priya apriye spṛśataḥ nanu yadi priyam api aśarīram na spṛśati iti yad maghavatā uktam suṣupta sthaḥ  vināśam eva apītaḥ  bhavati iti tad eva iha api āpannam na eṣa doṣaḥ dharma adharma kāryayoḥ śarīra saṃbandhinoḥ priya apriyayoḥ pratiṣedhasya vivakṣita tvāt  aśarīram na priya apriye spṛśata iti āgama apāyinoḥ hi sparśa śabdaḥ  dṛṣṭaḥ  yathā śīta sparśa uṣṇa sparśa iti na tu agneḥ uṣṇa prakāśayoḥ svabhāva bhūtayoḥ agninā sparśa iti bhavati tathā agneḥ savituḥ voṣṇa prakāśavat svarūpa bhūtasya ānandasya priyasya api na iha pratiṣedhaḥ vijñānam ānandam brahma ānandaḥ  brahma ityādi śrutibhyaḥ iha api bhūmā eva sukham iti ukta tvāt  nanu bhūmnaḥ priyasya ekatve asaṃvedya tvāt svarūpeṇa vā nitya saṃvedya tvāt nirviśeṣa tā iti na indrasya tad iṣṭam na āha khalu ayam saṃprati ātmānam jānātyayam aham asmi iti naḥ eva umāni bhūtāni vināśam eva apītaḥ  bhavati na aham atra bhogyam paśyāmi iti ukta tvāt  tad ha undrasya iṣṭam yad bhatāni ca ātmānam ca jānāti na ca apriyam kiñcid vetti sa sarvān  ca lokān āpnoti sarvān  ca kāmānyena jñānena satyam etad iṣṭam indrasya imāni bhūtāni mattaḥ  anyāni lokāḥ kāmāḥ ca sarve mattaḥ  anye aham eṣām svāmī iti na tu etad indrasya hitam hitam ca indrasya prajāpatinā vaktavyam vyomavat aśarīra ātma tayā sarva bhūta loka kāma ātmatva upagamena yā prāptiḥ tad hitam indrāya vaktavyam iti prajāpatinā abhipretam na tu rājñaḥ  rājya āptivat anya tvena tatra evam sati kam kena vijānīyāt ātmā ekatva imāni bhūtāni ayam aham asmi iti nanu asmin pakṣe strībhiḥ vā yānaiḥ vā sa yadi pitṛ loka kāmaḥ sa ekadhā bhavati iti ādi aiśvarya śrutayaḥ anupapannāḥ na sarva ātmanaḥ sarva phala saṃbandha upapatteḥ avirodhāt mṛda iva sarva ghaca karaka kuṇḍa ādi āptiḥ nanu sarva ātma tve duḥkha saṃbandhaḥ  api syāt iti ced na duḥkhasya api ātmatva upagamāt avirodhaḥ ātmani avidyā kalpanā nimittāni duḥkhāni rajjvām iva sarpa ādi kalpanā nimittāni sāca avidyā śarīra ātmā ekatva svarūpa darśanena duḥkha nimitta ucchinneni duḥkha saṃbandha āśaṅkā na saṃbhavati śuddha sattva saṃkalpa nimittānām tu kāmānām īśvara deha saṃbandhaḥ sarva bhūteṣu mānasānām para eva sarva sattva upādhi dvāreṇa bhoktā iti sarva avidyā kṛta saṃvyavahārāṇām para eva ātma āspadam na anyaḥ  asti iti vedānta siddhāntaḥ ya eṣaḥ  akṣiṇi puruṣaḥ  dṛśyati śyāmāt śabalam prapadya ityādi mantra āmnāya pāvanaḥ  japa arthaḥ ca dhyāna arthaḥ  vā śyāmaḥ  gambhīraḥ  varṇaḥ śyāma iva śyāmaḥ  hārdam brahma atyanta durava gāhya tvāt tad dhārda brahma jñātvā dhyānena tasmāt śyāmāt śabalam śabala iva śabalaḥ  araṇi ādi aneka kāma miśra tvāt brahma lokasya śābalya tam brahma lokam śabalam prapadye manasā śarīra pātāt vordhvam gaccheyam yasmāt aham śabalāt brahma lokān nāma rūpa vyākaraṇāya śyāmam prapadye hārda bhāvam prapannaḥ  asmi iti abhiprāyaḥ atas tam eva prakṛti svarūpam ātmānam śabalam prapadya iti arthaḥ katham śabalam brahma lokam prapadya iti ucyate aśva iva svāni lomāni vidhūya kampanena śramam pāṃsvādi ca romataḥ  apanīya yathā nirmalaḥ  bhavati evam hārda brahma jñānena vidhūya pāpam dharma adharmākyam candra iva ca rāhu grastaḥ tasmāt rahormukha ātma pramucya bhāsvaraḥ  bhavati yathā evam dhūtvā prahāra śarīram sarvān artha āśrayam iha eva dhyānena kṛtātmā kṛtakṛtyaḥ sanna kṛtam nityam brahma lokam abhisaṃbhavāmi iti dvis vacanam mantra samāpti artham ākāśaḥ  vā ityādi brahmaṇaḥ  lakṣaṇa nirdeśa artham ādhyānāya ākāśaḥ  vai nāma śrutiṣu prasiddha ātmā ākāśa iva aśarīra tvā sūkṣma tvāt ca sa ca ākāśaḥ  nāma rūpayoḥ sva ātma sthayoḥ jagat bīja bhūtayoḥ salilasya iva phena sthānīyayoḥ nirvahitā nirvoḍhā vyākartā te nāma rūpe yad antarā yasya brahmaṇaḥ  antarā madhye vartete tayoḥ vā nāma rūpayoḥ antarā madhye yad nāma rūpābhyām aspṛṣṭam yad iti etad tad brahma nāma rūpa vilakṣaṇam nāma rūpābhyām aspṛṣṭam tathā api tayoḥ nirvoḍhu tvam lakṣaṇam brahma iti arthaḥ idam eva maitreyī brāhmaṇena uktam cit mātra anugama ātma sarvatra cit svarūpa tā eva iti gamyata eka vākyatā kartha tad avagamyata iti āha sa ātmā ātmā hi nāma sarva jantūnām pratyak cetanaḥ sva saṃvedyaḥ prasiddhaḥ tena eva sva rūpeṇa unnīya aśarīraḥ  vyomavat sarva gata ātmā brahma iti avagantavyam tad ca ātmā brahma amṛtam amaraṇa dharmā ata ūrdhva  mantraḥ prajāpatiḥ caturmukhaḥ tasya sabhām veśma prabhu vimitam veśma prapadye gaccheyam kiñca yaśaḥ  aham yaśaḥ  nāma ātmā aham bhavāmi brāhmaṇānām brāhmaṇā eva hi viśeṣataḥ tam upāsate tatas teṣām yaśaḥ  bhavāmi tathā rājñām viśām ca te api adhikṛtā eva iti teṣām api ātmā bhavāmi tad yaśaḥ  aham anuprāpatsi anuprāptum icchāmi sa ha aham yaśasām ātmanām deha indriya manaḥ buddhi lakṣaṇānām ātmā kim artham aham evam prapadya iti ucyate śyetam varṇataḥ pakva badara samam rohitam tathā ādat kam danta rahitam api adat kam bhakṣayitṛ srī vyañjanam tad sevinām tejaḥ bala vīrya vijñāna dharmāṇām apahantṛ vināśayitriti etad  yad evaṃlakṣaṇam śyetam lindu picchilam tad mā abhigām mā abhigaccheyam dvis vacanam atyanta anartha hetutva pradarśana artham tad ha etad ātma jñānam sa upakaraṇam om iti etad akṣaram ityādyaiḥ saha upāsanaiḥ tad vācakena granthena aṣṭa adhyāyī lakṣaṇena saha brahmā hiraṇyagarbhaḥ parameśvaraḥ  vā tad dvāreṇa prajāpataye kaśyapāya uvāca asau  api manave sva putrāya manuḥ prajābhya iti evam śruti artha saṃpradāya paramparayā āgatam upaniṣad vijñānam adya api vidvatsu avagamyate yathā iha ṣaṣṭha ādi adhyāya traye prakāśita ātma vidyā saphala avagamyate tathā karmaṇām na kaścana artha iti prāpte tad ānarthakya prāpti parijihīrṣayā idam karmaṇaḥ  vidvadbhiḥ anuṣṭhīyamānasya viśiṣṭa phalavat tvena arthavat tvam ucyate ācārya kulāt vedam adhītya sahārthataḥ  adhyayanam kṛtvā yathā vidhānam yathāsmṛti uktaiḥ niyamaiḥ yuktaḥ san  iti arthaḥ sarvasya api vidheḥ smṛti uktasya upakaparvāṇakam prati kartavya tve guru śuśrūṣāyāḥ prādhānya pradarśana artham āha guroḥ karma yad kartavyam tad kṛtvā karma śūnyaḥ yaḥ  atiśiṣṭaḥ kālaḥ tena kālena vedam adhītya iti arthaḥ evam hi niyamavata adhītaḥ  vedaḥ karma jñāna phala prāptaye bhavati na anyathā iti abhiprāyaḥ abhisamāvṛtya dharma jijñāsām samāpayitvā guru kulat nivṛtya nyāyataḥ  dārān āhṛtya kuṭumbe sthitvā gārhatthve vihite karmaṇi tiṣṭhan  iti arthaḥ tatra api gārhasthya vihitānām karmaṇām svādhyāyasya prādhānya pradarśana artham ucyate śucau vivikte amedhya ādi rahite deśe yatāvat āsīnaḥ svādhyāyam adhīyānaḥ  naityakam adhikam ca yathāśakti ṛc ādi abhyāsam ca kurvan dhārmikān putrān śiṣyān  ca dharma yuktān vidadhat dhārmika tvena tān niyamayan  ātmani sva hṛdaye hārde brahmaṇi sarva indriyāṇi saṃpratiṣṭhāpya upasaṃhṛtya indriya grahaṇāt karmāṇi ca saṃnyasya ahiṃsa hiṃ  sām para pīḍām akurvan sarva bhūtāni sthāvara jaṅgamāni bhūtāni apīḍayan  iti arthaḥ bhikṣā nimittam aṭana ādinā api para pīḍā syāt iti ata āha anyatra tīrthebhyaḥ tīrtham nāma śāsra anujñā viṣayaḥ tatas  anyatra iti arthaḥ sarva āśramiṇām ca etad samānam tīrthebhyaḥ  anyatra hiṃsā eva iti anye varṇayanti kuṭumba eva etad sarvam kurvan sa khalu adhikṛtaḥ  yāvat āyuṣam yāvajjīvam evaṃyathā uktena prakāreṇa eva vartayan brahma lokam abhisaṃpadyatedeha ante na ca punar āvartate śarīra grahaṇāya punarāvṛtteḥ prāptāyāḥ pratiṣedhāt  arciḥ ādinā mārgeṇa kārya brahma loka bhisaṃpadya yāvat brahma loka sthitiḥ tāvat tatra eva tiṣṭhati prāk tatas na avartata iti arthaḥ dvis abhyāsa upaniṣad vidyā parisamāpti arthaḥ iti śrīmat govinda bhagavat pūjya pāda śiṣya parama haṃsapar ivrājaka ācārya śrīmat śaṅkara bhagavat pāda kṛtau cchānda ugya upaniṣad vivaraṇe aṣṭamaḥ  adhyāyaḥ
